Chapter 51: Forgotten Something

Back when Qi Wu first found the old hunter, there were also a few households in the vicinity. They might have appeared normal, but in fact, they were all tiger-henchman ghosts in disguise.

After the tiger demons were brought to justice, the tiger-henchman ghosts were at a loss. Some suggested to leave the mountain, while others said to continue hiding in the mountains, but there was no consensus.

Just as they were about to break into an argument, Lu Yang’s group appeared and captured them all. Meng Jingzhou let out a sliver of Pure Yang energy, causing the tiger-henchman ghosts to squirm on the ground and wail in agony.

“We don’t have to leave so many alive. Only two will be enough to pose as diabolic cultivators,” Lu Yang stated coldly. There is no need to sympathize with these tiger-henchman ghosts who acted as accomplices to the tiger demons in their evil deeds. They became tiger-henchman ghosts only because they agreed to the tiger demon’s request.

They deserve to die.

Lu Yang tried a few times but was still unable to take in a ghost servant, so he could only let his soul leave his body.

“Man Gu, we’re counting on you.”

Man Gu didn’t say anything, simply leaving behind two tiger-henchman ghosts who were originally travelers while killing the rest swiftly.

Using tiger-henchman ghosts transformed from hunters might raise the diabolic creed’s suspicion and cause them to guess that they had been obtained from the tiger demon after killing it. The risk would be much smaller with travelers.

“Return.”Man Gu absorbed one male and one female traveler tiger-henchman ghosts into his body.

This was also a part of ghost commanding techniques—absorbing the ghost into one’s body and summoning them again in battle.

When the three of them headed to Yanjiang County, they bumped into Qi Wu and the others. They were still going around in circles in the mountain forest. As it was still raining and they didn’t know the way, they naturally couldn’t find the path down the mountain.

“Benefactors!” Qi Wu and the rest were overjoyed to see the trio who they viewed as their lifeline.

“Benefactors, we won’t forget your great favor and kindness.”

“The Mountain God has shown their power!”

“We are forever indebted to you!

All of them showered words of gratitude at the trio with overflowing sincerity.

Seeing the people they had rescued and hearing their heartfelt gratitude, the gloomy haze in Lu Yang’s heart slowly dissipated. He stopped thinking about the bones and corpses in the caves.

“As cultivators, we ought to follow the righteous path. There’s no need for thanks,” Meng Jingzhou expressed his stance solemnly. It is only right for me to save people; I’m not doing it to receive others’ gratitude.

Man Gu observed Meng Jingzhou’s righteous visage. As expected of my role model—staying calm and collected in all situations; that’s not something I can achieve.

Even without looking at Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang could tell that the latter was just pretending. There’s probably a flower blooming from joy in his heart right now.

And why did Lu Yang know that? It was because he, too, was wearing a righteous expression.

After sending the traveling merchants to Yanjiang County, the sky was already starting to turn bright. The tempest ravaging the whole night finally stopped, and a faint rainbow arched across the horizon.

“By the way, did we forget something?” Meng Jingzhou couldn’t brush off the feeling that he had forgotten something.

“Probably not?” Lu Yang counted the number of people. There’s three people; there’s three brains. We didn’t forget anything.

“I just keep feeling like we’re missing something...never mind, I shall not think about it anymore.”

~~~

In Qinghuai County, a carriage was parked in the backyard of an inn. An old horse was slowly nibbling on the feed left by Meng Jingzhou.

Why hasn’t that young fellow from the Meng Family come to fetch me? The feed won’t last more than a few days. What happened to finishing the mission in five to six days?!

As an aberrant demon beast, the old horse naturally couldn’t consume normal feed like ordinary horses. It always ate expensive feed bought by Meng Jingzhou since they were meticulously prepared and infused with spirit energy.

The old horse snorted and puckered its lips, feeling very bored. That was when it suddenly caught sight of a snow-white female horse next door.

~~~

After entering the city, the trio randomly chose a teahouse and ordered a pot of tea with a few plates of pastries as they planned their next move.

“Yanjiang Commandery is so big. How are we going to find this Qin Yuanhao? Do we get the local authorities to help?” Man Gu knitted his brow.

Yanjiang Commandery was not a major cultivation hub. Compared to other commanderies, its population was also ranked at the bottom, and it was inconspicuous on the map, even missing from less detailed maps. Nonetheless, it was still a commandery with a population of two million people. Finding someone was akin to searching for a needle in a haystack.

Lu Yang waved his hand. “Not a good idea. We don’t know how long the diabolic creed has hidden in this place, and there is likely a complex web of forces behind them, possibly including the local authorities.”

Man Gu didn’t understand what Lu Yang was getting at. “Doesn’t everyone want to exterminate the diabolic creeds? Why would the authorities help them?”

Lu Yang didn’t have to answer; Meng Jingzhou was most familiar in such aspects. “It’s precisely because everyone wants to exterminate them that the Great Xia Dynasty has added a key performance indicator: Slain Devil Count. Basically, the more devils one eradicates, the higher their cultivation and the better their political track record becomes.

“Think about it, diabolic creeds could simply strike a deal with the commandery governor—they would provide devils to the commandery governor regularly while the commandery governor would agree not to reveal the diabolic creed’s location.”

What Meng Jingzhou had shared was not just a story—they were facts that he had personally heard from the seniors who were officials in his family. Despite the Xia Emperor executing them batch after batch, there were still some who slipped through the net.

Some people in court had also proposed removing this performance metric, but it was stopped by the prime minister. With the performance indicator in place, most officials would assiduously eliminate those from the diabolic path, though a minority still colluded with the diabolic creeds. However, with the performance metric removed, it would be hard to determine how many officials would still be willing to invest the efforts in tracking down traces of the diabolic creeds.

All in all, this evaluation indicator did more good than harm.

Man Gu felt like Meng Jingzhou’s words had completely overturned his understanding of the world; he had never thought about such matters before.

Lu Yang chimed in, “The probability of the commandery governor being in league with the diabolic creed is low, but we should still prepare for the worst. If they are really in cahoots and we reveal our intentions in coming here, the commandery governor would hand over Qin Yuanhao to avoid detection. However, if the whole Yanjiang Branch gets wind of it, they would go into hiding, causing us to miss our chance to infiltrate the diabolic creed. That will be penny wise, pound foolish, and not at all ideal.

“Our best bet for now is to keep our identities hidden and search for Qin Yuanhao first. If we really can’t find him, it wouldn’t be too late to ask the authorities for help then.”

Man Gu nodded, feeling that both of them made sense. “How should we draw Qin Yuanhao out?” Many ideas flashed past Man Gu’s mind, but he found noticeable flaws in all of them.

Posting flyers or notices definitely won’t work; that’s too obvious.

Inquiring at the black market? If Qin Yuanhao learns that someone is looking into him, he’ll hide himself. Who knows if he’ll even lead the members of the diabolic creed to ambush us. We’ll be at their mercy then. That won’t work.

I wonder what brilliant ideas Brother Lu and Brother Meng have.

Lu Yang had already thought of a plan when they were on their way down the mountain. He laughed mischievously. “Do you know that unlike us righteous sects, these people who roam the jianghu care about their face the most, especially people from diabolic creeds. They see their face as their status. If someone causes a blow to their reputation, it’s even more unbearable than killing them.

“That’s why we must widely spread rumors that Qin Yuanhao is a kind person who doesn’t work but does good deeds. Once this spreads throughout the whole of Yanjiang Commandery, the members of the diabolic creed would think that Qin Yuanhao is a good guy. Qin Yuanhao will feel that he has lost face and won’t be able to resist coming out!

“And that would be our chance!”

Meng Jingzhou summarized it succinctly, “Basically, we make things up and spread rumors.”

Coincidentally, Meng Jingzhou was a natural in doing so.

Man Gu suddenly saw the light. This is a really good idea! If we can’t find Qin Yuanhao, we’ll just force him out.

But what did he mean by “unlike us righteous sects?”

Chapter 52: Who Are You Scolding To Be A Good Guy?!

Inside a small tavern, a drinker was speaking loudly, drawing the attention of many. “Have you heard? A righteous hero has emerged from our commandery. His name is Qin Yuanhao, and even those from the Five Great Immortal Sects are impressed by his deeds!” The corners of Lu Yang’s eyes rose upward, looking especially excited, as if he had some interesting news to share with everyone.

“Really? Why haven't I heard of this person?”

“I vaguely remember the name, but he doesn't seem to be a good person.”

“Stop arguing, let this brother here tell us what's up with Qin Yuanhao!”

Lu Yang paused for a bit before continuing, “This hero named Qin Yuanhao has considerable cultivation and is at the Foundation Establishment Stage. He stands up for justice and has an extensive network of friends. Everyone who knows him is willing to call him ‘Big Brother.’”

Hearing that Qin Yuanhao was at the Foundation Establishment Stage, the patrons’ eyes lit up. This was certainly news for them.

In the past, they would hear rumors about the jianghu, how impressive the top-rank wulin experts were and how thrilling their experiences were. Although they all sounded remarkable and exciting when listening to the stories, after calming down, they knew deep down that the top-rank wulin experts weren't actually very powerful.

The consensus was that the top-rank wulin experts corresponded to Level Eight to Level Nine of the Qi Training Stage. That was the limit for them.

Now that there were rumors of a Foundation Establishment expert, they naturally wanted to hear all about it; that would give them something to boast about in the future.

“Let me tell you about that one day when Qin Yuanhao and his close friend went to an auction. His close friend took a liking to a treasure and asked Qin Yuanhao to lend him several thousands of low-grade spirit stones.

Qin Yuanhao laughed out loud and said, ‘With the relationship we have, talking about money is too vulgar. Just take these eight thousand low-grade spirit stones; no need to pay me back.’

“His close friend was extremely touched.”

“Eight thousand low-grade spirit stones?” a passer-by called Meng Jingzhou exclaimed. “Spirit stones are the currency of the cultivation world. Eight thousand low-grade spirit stones is enough to buy a big mansion in the county center with gorgeous maidservants for life!”

Only with the aid of Meng Jingzhou’s explanation did the patrons understand the value of eight thousand low-grade spirit stones. This person called Qin Yuanhao is so generous! He could give away those spirit stones just like that!

“After his close friend won the bid for that treasure, he became the target of another bidder who was a diabolic cultivator. The latter successfully ambushed Qin Yuanhao and his good friend. As his good friend was unwilling to part with the treasure, he struggled vigorously, but the diabolic cultivator killed him and stole the treasure. When Qin Yuanhao wanted to give chase, unfortunately, the diabolic cultivator had already fled.”

Lu Yang stopped and pointed at his throat. Understanding his gesture, the patrons offered him drinks. He sipped from a cup of grain wine and proceeded with his story, “Before his good friend died, he entrusted his wife and daughter to Qin Yuanhao. With tears welling up in his eyes, Qin Yuanhao promised to take good care of them.

“The mother and daughter were rare beauties. The mother bore an ageless appearance and had a graceful figure, while the daughter was cheerful, adorable, and playfully mischievous. Despite all that, Qin Yuanhao’s heart did not waver in front of this beautiful duo.

“After losing their pillar of support, the mother and daughter found Qin Yuanhao to be someone they could entrust themselves to for life, so they tried to seduce him. However, Qin Yuanhao outrightly told them that he cultivated the Virgin Boy Kungfu[1] and couldn't lose his chastity.

“Following through with his promise, Qin Yuanhao looked after the two without overstepping his boundaries. Finally, he found a suitable man and entrusted the mother and daughter to him.”

Meng Jingzhou remarked, “To think that there is such an upright hero in this world—wealthy yet not greedy and unswayed when faced with beauties.” His words resonated with the people around him.

“Qin Yuanhao is really a great person.”

“It's a pity I don't know Qin Yuanhao, otherwise I would definitely borrow some spirit stones from him!

“Who said that even heroes have a weakness for beauties? Hasn't Qin Yuanhao proved otherwise?!”

In the corner, Man Gu watched as Lu Yang entertained the crowd and Meng Jingzhou supported him ardently. He found them to be incredible as they needed no script; they simply made up a story on the spot.

When will I finally have such a talent?

Drinkers liked flaunting about things others didn't know. They had drunk quite a bit when listening to Lu Yang’s story, so there were some details that were fuzzy. This was something they realized when boasting after drinking yet again. However, they were already halfway through the story, and there was no way they could lose face by admitting that they had forgotten the remaining half. Hence, they made up the rest of the story with their imagination.

The parts everyone forgot were different, so the additional stories they fabricated were different, resulting in all sorts of rumors about Qin Yuanhao.

~~~

“Have you heard of that great philanthropist called Qin Yuanhao?”

“Do you mean the one who secretly found a spirit stone quarry, became a tycoon among local cultivators overnight, and lent others money without having them pay him back?”

“I think so, but what I heard was that Qin Yuanhao stays away from women and is interested in men?”

“Yes yes yes, I heard that Qin Yuanhao cultivates the Virgin Boy Kungfu and likes little boys best!”

“Are you for real? Is that how you practice the Virgin Boy Kungfu? Didn't they say that those who cultivate the Virgin Boy Kungfu must eat Boy Chicken[2]?”

“They're all wrong. I heard that Qin Yuanhao obtained the legendary immortal artifact, the Merit Logbook by chance. He became recognized as its true owner by dripping his blood on it. The more good deeds he does, the more merits he accumulates. These merits can be exchanged for rewards, even including spirit treasures, immortal artifacts, and cultivation!”

“I also heard that he is the destined overlord of the Nine Netherworlds who manages everyone's life, death, and merits. Don't be misled by his current weak strength; he's just amassing power and growing in secret. As soon as he gets the chance, he'll become a dragon that soars the Nine Heavens and ascend to an immortal!

“He endured humiliation and forced himself to join a diabolic creed only because he wanted to infiltrate the higher-ups and wipe them out so that they could also become his merits!”

“He views the diabolic creed as something already in his pocket; such strong and valiant vigor!”

~~~

In Yanjiang Commandery, the diabolic creed was holding their regular meeting.

The followers lined up deferentially in two rows while the branch leader sat on a stone carved from a whole chunk of crimson agate. The armrests were carved with a dragon’s and tiger’s head, signifying his authority as the branch leader.

This chair was a tribute from Qin Yuanhao.

Qin Yuanhao was in a very foul mood. His forehead had darkened, and the corners of his mouth would twitch every now and then, revealing beast-like teeth.

His colleagues paid no heed to him. Considering their similar cultivation and status, they wouldn't be implicated no matter how furious he was. That was simply how diabolic creeds work—what does the other party's life and death have to do with me? I'm not the unlucky one.

However, Qin Yuanhao couldn't be blamed for his bad mood as people were already asking him before the meeting started, “Can you lend me some spirit stones? After all, you have a spirit stone quarry.”

“Do you know any beautiful sisters or mother-daughter pairs? Do recommend one pair to me.”

“I'm sorry, I shouldn't have taken you to the brothel to listen to music. It must have been very painful for you to go to that kind of place, right?”

“Big Brother Qin, I'm going to stick with you from now on. The Merit Logbook isn't as important; what I value most is you as a person.”

“Upright and righteous, generous with money, uninterested in women...Qin Yuanhao, you're really a disgrace to us diabolic creeds. Don't tell me that you're a spy sent by the righteous path?”

Qin Yuanhao clenched his fists, vowing to find the person who defamed him, chop them into pieces, and feed them to dogs!

I'm a self-respecting bad guy. How did I suddenly become a good guy?!

Who are you scolding to be a good guy?!

1. It’s one of the Shaolin Arts and needs to be practiced from a very young age. It directly translates to “child kungfu” or “boy kungfu.” ☜

2. This is the literal translation of spring chicken, young chicken, or Poussin in Chinese. ☜

Chapter 53: The Diabolic Creeds’ Large-Scale Recruitment

In pitch-darkness, a dozen pairs of eyes glowed with a mysterious light, as if they belonged to poisonous snakes hiding in caves. These dozen pairs of eerie eyes were fixated on the branch leader, silently waiting for him to speak.

Finally, the branch leader who was sitting lazily spoke in a hoarse voice that sounded like he hadn't spoken for several decades. Every word he uttered carried a weight to them.

“Why are the lamps not lit?”

An administrator respectfully replied, “Branch Leader, have you forgotten? During the previous meeting, you gave high praise for the atmosphere at the meetings with higher-ups. You even mentioned that our Yanjiang Branch doesn't have the atmosphere of a diabolic creed.

“After thinking about it, I realized that it was indeed the case. Perhaps this was the reason for the Yanjiang Branch ranking the lowest among the branches. That got me thinking, don't the stories often mention that we diabolic creeds like to plot sinister schemes in dark places? So, I deliberately didn't let the servants light the lamps.

“Actually, you know what? Not lighting the lamps really gives off the atmosphere of us doing evil deeds.”

It was evident that this administrator was very clear about his own actions, aware that diabolic creeds were not places for doing good deeds.

The branch leader fell silent for a long while. Is this administrator hinting to me that he wants to leave the creed? Is he hinting that the Yanjiang Branch hasn't had a raise in budget for a long time? Or is he hinting that we should buy insurance for the members?

He's probably not planning to leave the creed.

He has been industrious in doing bad deeds and doesn't differentiate between friends and enemies. Not only does he do evil outside, but he also sabotages his own people in the diabolic creed. He's no doubt a bad egg.

It's not about increasing our budget either.

The diabolic creed’s budget is linked to the local treasury and is already an enormous sum, considering that it is three times that of local officials. As Yanjiang Commandery is a remote and small commandery, its budget can't possibly be at the same level as the headquarters.

It's even less likely that he's requesting to buy insurance. Most members of diabolic creeds don't even have successors; who will the payouts even go to? Besides, the Luodi Merchant Guild won't let diabolic creeds buy insurance. If they were to sell life insurance or accident insurance to diabolic creed members, the diabolic creeds would be confident of making the merchant guild pay through the nose and not even have money left for their underwear.

“Let's light the lamps first.”

“Understood.” The administrator gave a puff, and specks of flame fell onto the lamps, igniting the wicks. In an instant, the entire hall became bright.

The branch leader spoke again, “Everyone may have more or less heard about the rumors regarding Little Qin. Stop spreading them; don’t let others see us as a joke. We are all witnesses to Little Qin’s character. He’s evil to the core and there’s nothing he wouldn’t do. If he gets arrested by the authorities, even decapitation is a light punishment for him. That’s enough to prove that Little Qin’s character is a good fit for our creed’s doctrine.

“As for the talk of Little Qin being a member of the righteous path, that’s just utter nonsense. Those who can join our creed have all passed the creed leader’s tests. The creed leader’s assessment of him was ‘diabolic nature to the bone.’ Our creed leader’s judgment definitely won’t be wrong.”

Qin Yuanhao bowed. “That is wise of you, branch leader.” He felt slightly better. After I get back, I’m determined to slaughter the ones spreading the rumors!

The branch leader made no mention of Qin Yuanhao’s matter again. He had spoken those few lines simply because of Qin Yuanhao’s favor in gifting him the chair.

“The reason I have gathered everyone here today is that the headquarters has assigned us a task.” He paused for a bit. “They request branches from all locations to recruit new disciples.”

Qin Yuanhao and the others were taken aback. The diabolic creed hadn’t conducted a large-scale recruitment for thirty years. New members in the recent thirty years had joined only through referrals. One example was Qin Yuanhao’s attempt at recruiting the tiger demon. Unfortunately, the tiger demon was insistent on staying at Pine Mountain.

“I believe everyone here is aware of the news regarding the Great Era. Geniuses of the era would rise, renowned experts could be defeated by some unknown youngster, and countless undiscovered ancient cave ruins would appear once again. This is an era of fortuitous opportunities and challenges.

“The Five Great Immortal Sects, S-Class Sects, and First-Class Sects are teeming with geniuses. Once scarce, Dual Spirit Roots are now a common sight instead. If we let these geniuses truly grow up, we can forget about competing in this Great Era.

“If we want to fight, now is the only time!

“If we grab hold of the fortuitous opportunities, we’ll be able to encounter the rain and transform into dragons, soaring through the Nine Heavens and becoming carefree immortals! However, fortuitous opportunities aren’t so easy to grasp. The damn Great Xia Dynasty and Five Great Immortal Sects have intensified their efforts in suppressing us, and many of our comrades have fallen.

“To secure a place in this Great Era, we must expand our diabolic creed and gain more followers. The Four Great Diabolic Creeds have already reached a consensus on this. What all of you need to do is to disseminate news of the diabolic creeds’ recruitment through your own channels. Try to gather all the diabolic cultivators from Yanjiang Commandery and nearby commanderies or those who are interested in joining our creed.”

Someone voiced a concern, “If we recruit on such a large scale, wouldn’t we give the righteous path a chance to infiltrate the diabolic creeds?”

He wasn’t the only one with this question. The diabolic creeds had always been cautious for survival. If a few undercovers from the righteous path wormed their way in, the diabolic creeds would be in a precarious position.

The branch leader shook his head. “This recruitment is organized by the creed leader with his almighty powers. Those from the righteous path can never pass the trials he sets.”

All skepticism vanished, replaced by boundless fervor. The creed leader was an omnipotent figure in the diabolic creed. They believed him to be the guiding star that could lead their Everlasting Creed to glory!

~~~

After the meeting adjourned, Qin Yuanhao immediately touched on his connections to find out who was trying to frame him. Through multiple means, he finally traced the source to a small tavern.

“That customer was eight feet tall, eight feet wide, and had a face full of pockmarks. He was a burly fellow who looked like he could eat three children for a meal.” The tavern owner gestured, having a vivid impression of Lu Yang.

Based on the descriptions, Qin Yuanhao soon drew a portrait that looked nothing like the real Lu Yang.

After all, Lu Yang and the others had disguised themselves before entering the tavern to spread the rumors.

Qin Yuanhao’s eyes were frigid. You dare to start a rumor when you’re so conspicuous? Did you think I’m a pushover?

It was already late at night, but there was no curfew in the Great Xia Dynasty. Qin Yuanhao and his gang of underlings were enjoying barbeque on the streets—there were pork skewers, beef skewers, roasted lamb legs, roasted chicken feet, roasted pork rind, roasted beef tendons, roasted cow trotters, roasted river prawns, tender-grilled kidney, grilled chives, roasted potatoes, grilled tomatoes, roasted tofu...

The grilled skewers were tender and well-seasoned. They were bursting with flavor. Slathered with a dark-colored oily secret sauce, they would sizzle and a fragrance would assault the nostrils when they were grilled over charcoal.

The pork was skewered on long bamboo sticks and grilled over a large pot of fire. The fatty parts were rich but not greasy, and the lean parts bore an intense meaty flavor.

The lamb legs were placed inside the tandoors and barbecued. With the combination of stewing and roasting, the heat was evenly distributed, resulting in just the right crispness and tenderness while encompassing a fresh fragrance.

The chicken feet were first stewed in lu sauce and then grilled. The presence of the tendons, skin, and crunchy bones offered a bountiful texture, and chewing on them was pure satisfaction.

The chicken legs were grilled raw. It required precise control of the fire to prevent excessive loss of moisture and oil so that the skin, meat, tendons, and bones could achieve a balance between flavor and texture.

The potatoes were barbecued while wrapped then smoked, finally adding a secret sauce. It was crispy on the outside and tender on the inside with a fine texture blessing the mouth.

All of them ate until their mouths were covered in oil. When they were full, Qin Yuanhao arrogantly ordered his underlings. “You lot, go and search the whole city for these few people. Don’t come back until you find them!”

“Roger, Big Brother!” The underlings replied in unison and split up.

After finishing his barbeque meal, Qin Yuanhao was content and temporarily cast aside all thoughts about the annoying rumor mongers. At the same time, he didn’t notice Lu Yang lurking underground.

Few people pay attention to what is beneath their feet.

And Qin Yuanhao was no exception.

Chapter 54: Naming The Shop

Chapter 54: Naming The Shop

After identifying the location of their destination, Lu Yang reconvened with the other two and analyzed, “Judging from Qin Yuanhao’s walking posture and breathing frequency, he should be at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

“He stays in a normal estate which isn’t too big. It also doesn’t look like there are servants or anyone else. Let’s observe him nearby for a while longer. First, it’s to observe his habits; we can’t be totally clueless when people in the diabolic creed ask us after we join. Second, it’s to follow him and see if we can find the Yanjiang Branch’s base.”

Man Gu was puzzled. “Qin Yuanhao has so many underlings, so why aren’t we following them to find the Yanjiang Branch?”

Meng Jingzhou rejected this idea as he knew a bit more about diabolic creeds. “Those people don’t have cultivation. It’s true that they’re Qin Yuanhao underlings, but they’re not members of the diabolic creed. Joining a diabolic creed is not as easy as you think. Besides, we’re not even sure if these people know that Qin Yuanhao belongs to a diabolic creed.

“Anyways, where should we hide to observe him? There are no hostelries nearby. The only establishments are a few teahouses and taverns. We can partake in tea in the morning, but what about at night?”

Diabolic creeds love acting at night.

Lu Yang was also slightly fazed by this conundrum. Suddenly, the corner of his eye lit up upon catching sight of a teahouse with a signboard for rent. “This teahouse’s location is perfect! We can observe Qin Yuanhao from the second floor. Let’s rent this teahouse and keep an eye on him while under the guise of opening a shop!”

Meng Jingzhou nodded and followed up with a question, “What shop do we open?”

“Although opening a shop is a facade, we need to make sure that our pretense is convincing. I’m not good at brewing tea, so continuing to run a teahouse is out of the question. There’s a senior in my family who is well-versed in linguistic spells; I spent some time learning the four fundamentals of xiangsheng comedy—speak, learn, tease, and sing.” Meng Jingzhou was very dedicated. “I propose we open a xiangsheng house. I’ll perform a solo xiangsheng.”

Lu Yang was impressed by the multi-talented Meng Jingzhou. “But xiangsheng is only lively in the day; there’ll be hardly anyone left at night. The best solution is to find a business that operates at night, maybe an entertainment venue so that it can be full of buzz and people can drink and make merry. By letting everyone enjoy themselves, we can observe Qin Yuanhao from the second floor without him noticing us.”

Meng Jingzhou blushed. Although he was a little hesitant, he was mostly excited. “A nighttime business...don’t tell me that you want to open...”

Lu Yang nodded. “That’s right, I’m talking about a barbeque shop.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. “...That’s right, I was thinking of that too.”

Lu Yang had thought it through. Barbeque was easy to pick up, and even if they were inexperienced, they should probably get the hang of it after charring the barbeque for more than ten times.

“You can leave the barbeque to me.” Man Gu smiled with overflowing confidence. To prove his competency, he even fished out a piece of paper that wrote “Ancestral Barbeque Secret Recipe.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou found the secret recipe very familiar. Isn’t this the ancestral barbeque secret recipe on the rewards list that can only be exchanged with a hundred contribution points?!

Man Gu smiled sheepishly. “Back home, I often barbecued wild beasts myself, including black bears, wild boars, and small rabbits. I noticed that there are many things to eat in the Dao-Seeking Sect but very few barbeque shops, so I put my ancestral barbeque secret recipe out there.”

Lu Yang had already been baffled then. Who would place a barbeque secret recipe on the rewards boards? So you were the one who put it there!

Meng Jingzhou was curious. “Did anyone buy it?”

Man Gu answered honestly, “A senior brother told me that after he bought the barbeque secret recipe, he went on a mission with a fellow female disciple in the wilderness and used his barbeque to win her heart.”

Meng Jingzhou didn’t know what to say. I shouldn’t have asked.

A faint smile appeared on Man Gu’s face. “There’s also another benefit to opening a barbeque shop.”

“And what’s that?”

Man Gu summoned the two tiger-henchman ghosts. “I don’t have to do the work myself. We can let these two tiger-henchman ghosts barbecue in the rear kitchen, and we don’t even have to give them any wages; it’s very convenient.” This way, we won’t even have to hire a waiter. It’s both cost-saving and secretive, truly well thought out.

After learning from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou for so long, Man Gu had managed to learn a thing or two. However, Lu Yang adamantly refused to admit that Man Gu had learned anything from him.

Man Gu spent the night researching the secret recipe. His old home was in the wilderness, so the original version of the barbeque recipe consisted of many ingredients that were unique to the wild. He had to study how these could be substituted.

He suddenly asked, “By the way, do you eat grilled bugs and grilled cow eyes?”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou shook their heads, persuading Man Gu to stick to things that were within the general public’s comfort zone.

Man Gu simply replied, “Oh.”

He pondered about it briefly. Firstly, I’m a normal person. Secondly, I can accept these things, so whatever I can accept, normal people can also accept.

Conclusion reached.

Man Gu retained the grilled bugs, grilled cow eyes, and other barbeque ingredients with special regional traits, hoping that people in Yanjiang Commandery would like them.

Early the next morning, Meng Jingzhou demonstrated his extraordinary wealth by purchasing the whole teahouse.

“Hold on, didn’t we say to rent?” Lu Yang stared at Meng Jingzhou in a stupor.

Meng Jingzhou had acted too quickly. Before Lu Yang could react, the teahouse was already under their names. We're just doing the mission for a few months. Don’t tell me you're planning to run the place for your whole life?

Meng Jingzhou defended himself with conviction. “I have always only used my own things; if I can buy it, I’ll never rent it! Worst case, I’ll just sell it off again after we’re done with the mission.”

Seeing how swiftly Meng Jingzhou handed over the money, the original teahouse owner rapidly packed up and left. After his departure, a very serious problem lay in front of them.

What should be the name of the barbeque shop?

Meng Jingzhou proposed, “I suggest calling it ‘Waiter Meng Barbeque Shop.’”

Lu Yang cast a glance at Meng Jingzhou and was dismissive. “This name is too vulgar. I suggest calling it ‘Just Drink Three Bowls Barbeque Shop.’ [1]

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu shook their heads, finding it not at all appropriate.

It was rare for Man Gu to raise a different opinion. “The name ‘Just Drink Three Bowls’ is too long. Why don’t we follow our tribe’s style and call it ‘Hahaha Barbeque Shop’ or ‘Heeheehee Barbeque Shop?’”

Lu Yang had heard of the naming customs of the Barbarian Tribe in the wild. Such methods were considered progressive even within the fairly progressive Dao-Seeking Sect. There were the ‘Hehehe Weapon Shop,’ ‘Roar Roar Roar Tavern,’ ‘Ow Ow Ow Brothel’ and more...

“What about calling it ‘Transcendent Tribulation Barbeque Shop?’”

“We might as well call it ‘Immortal Ascension Barbeque Shop.’”

“I think Light Boat Barbeque Shop sounds acceptable.”

“Who would give a barbeque shop such an elegant name?”

The three discussed for a while more, but they eventually had to acknowledge a frustrating fact—they were all terrible at coming up with names.

“Forget it, the three of us can write a name each on a piece of paper and crumple them up; we’ll shake them and pick randomly,” Lu Yang recommended a solution, and the other two agreed.

Considering that Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou weren’t exactly known to be pure-hearted, they decided that it’d be safer to have Man Gu shake the paper lots. Pressing his hands together, Man Gu hugged the three small paper balls. Swaying up and down and with his thumb shifting away, two small paper balls flew out.

Opening up one of them, he saw what was written on the paper: One More Time [2]

Man Gu opened the other paper in confusion. The words written on it were: Thank You For Your Patronage

Question marks were madly popping out of Man Gu’s head. It took a while for him to register what was happening.

We’re just naming the shop and not participating in a lottery...right?

1. This is based on one of China’s earliest and most successful advertisements. It was promoting their alcohol, and it stated how three bowls was just the right quantity. ☜

2. It can mean “one more time” or “come again. ☜

Chapter 55: Flourishing Business

He glanced at Lu Yang, then at Meng Jingzhou, and slowly asked. “You came up with these names?”

Lu Yang nodded. “I came up with ‘One More Time Barbeque Shop.’”

Meng Jingzhou also nodded. “I came up with ‘Thank You For Your Patronage Barbeque Shop.’”

In comparison to their ideas, Man Gu felt that the name “Lamb Lamb Lamb Barbeque Shop” was too ordinary.

The first paper Man Gu unraveled was Lu Yang’s, so according to their rules, the barbeque shop would be named “One More Time.”

“By the way, do any of you have a method to conceal your aura waves?” Lu Yang asked.

When they were on the streets, Lu Yang had noticed that many people’s breathing methods had different affinities with spirit energy, so he could verify that they were cultivators. However, when he used his spiritual consciousness to scan them, he couldn't discern their cultivation.

Having one or two people with higher cultivation than himself was still reasonable, but when everyone's cultivation was higher than his, that was clearly impossible. Unlike Taiping Village, although there were many cultivators, it was not to the extent of everyone being minimally at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Upon further contemplation, Lu Yang figured it out. A cultivator’s cultivation determined their status. If they wanted to roam the jianghu without being bullied, they either had exceptional cultivation or hid their cultivation so that others wouldn't dare to recklessly make a move against them.

With how we don't conceal ourselves at all when we go out, we're practically telling everyone that we're greenhorns. If we want to infiltrate the diabolic creed, we need to pretend to be old jianghu veterans.

“I do have one; we used it when hunting back home.” Man Gu took out a sheepskin scroll from his chest pocket. “The prey in the wilderness are very sly; they will run at the slightest hint of danger. If we wanted to be successful, we had to conceal our aura waves and set up an ambush beforehand.”

The Barbarian Tribe Man Gu belonged to had the noblest bloodline in the wilderness. Not only did the Qi Training and Foundation Establishment tribe members go out to hunt, even the Golden Core members who could fast also had to. For the Barbarian Tribe, the prey weren't just for sustenance but rather because they bore the properties of natural treasures.

“But you can't move when you use this secret spell. If you move, the spell is broken.”

The greater the restrictions, the more effective a spell often was. The effects of the sheepskin scroll’s concealment effect alone was enough to rank it among the top three.

“I have an ordinary concealment spell here, but someone who is one major cultivation stage above you can tell your cultivation.” Meng Jingzhou whipped out a bamboo scroll.

It was unclear how long it had been stored as it still emitted a faint bamboo scent. From the quality of the bamboo, one could also discern how extraordinary the spell it recorded was.

There were still a plethora of other spells and magical items he brought from home stored inside his jade pendant. In fact, there were so many that he didn't have enough time to learn all of them.

Lu Yang gave Meng Jingzhou an odd look. “Didn't you leave your house and family? Where did you get so many good things from?”

“My younger sister secretly gave them to me.”

“Fine.”

The three of them began learning the concealment spell. All of them were promising talents, so it was a walk in the park for them to learn such a small spell. They picked it up in just an hour, and the only thing left was practice.

Lu Yang cupped his fist in gratitude. “When I learn new spells, I'll definitely teach them to you!

It might not look like it, considering how effortless it was for Man Gu and Meng Jingzhou to take out their spells, but Lu Yang knew deep down that the two types of concealment spells were rare. That fully demonstrated their trust in him.

Meng Jingzhou laughed it off, and Man Gu similarly told Lu Yang not to take it to heart.

~~~

“Hmm? I remember that this was a teahouse, but it's now a barbeque shop?” Under the curtain of the night, two heroes from the jianghu happened to realize that the original teahouse was gone, now replaced by a barbeque shop with a very interesting name.

“One More Time Barbeque Shop. Oh, what a fragrant smell.”

The two jianghu heroes sniffed the air as the aroma assailed their nostrils and made their mouths water.

“Shall we grab a bite?”

“Let’s go in.”

The two instantly agreed with each other and walked into the barbeque shop.

As soon as they entered, they were flabbergasted by the boisterous atmosphere inside. Customers were clinking cups of wine with one another, wolfing down skewers, downing alcohol heartily, and stuffing themselves with euphoria plastered across their faces. Their voices were so loud that it could almost detach the roof. Burly men who looked like waiters were holding skewers as they ran in and out.

Such a burly waiter; is it to prevent customers from dining and dashing?

“This new shop is so popular?”

The two were quite excited. There must be a reason for the shop to be such a hit; we must try it. They were very lucky as there was only one available table left.

After the two sat down, another waiter by the name of Lu Yang held a small book and walked over, wearing the standard smile of the service industry. “Hello, what would the two of you like to have?”

“Two bottles of wine, one plate of boiled peanuts, thirty lamb skewers, thirty beef skewers, and two servings of roasted potatoes...all mildly spicy. Both of us can't take too much spice.”

“Mmm,” Lu Yang noted. He then sent an auditory message to Man Gu, “Can you adjust your recipe? Your barbeque is too delicious and has attracted too many people. How are we going to spy on Qin Yuanhao?”

Lu Yang hadn't expected Man Gu’s secret recipe to be so “effective.” The first night, a few customers came. The second day, a few tables were filled. The third day, the place was packed. Today was the fourth day, and just as the two jianghu heroes occupied the last table, a queue had already started to form outside.

Lu Yang suspected that by the fifth day, someone would already be asking for reservations or sharing tables with others. On the thirtieth day, they would be able to open a chain store in the neighboring commandery. A year later, there would be two hundred chains in the northern region of the Central Continent. In three years, they would become a sensation across the continent. Five years after that, they would be listed on the stock market...that was if the concept of a stock market existed here.

There's nothing wrong with Man Gu’s recipe right? He didn't add any illegal substance inside the sauce, right?!

This was just a joke. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had tasted the barbeque prepared by Man Gu and found no illegal substance. Although it was indeed delectable, they didn't expect to attract so many customers.

Lu Yang finally realized the reason after a while. I've been constantly eating supreme-quality delicacies at Heaven’s Gate Peak, so my palate is already spoiled. The fact that I still find Man Gu’s barbeque yummy speaks volumes about the uniqueness of his recipe.

In other words, I definitely can't let the shop continue being so popular.

“It seems quite busy downstairs; do you need me to go down and help?” Meng Jingzhou’s lazy voice echoed in their ears.

He was the only one monitoring Qin Yuanhao from the second floor.

“Just stay put and continue spying on Qin Yuanhao. Don't come down and cause trouble!” Lu Yang warned.

If Meng Jingzhou comes downstairs, he's certainly not going to just be a waiter. Based on his understanding of Meng Jingzhou, the latter could deliver a round of xiangsheng comedy even while serving dishes.

Meng Jingzhou let out a big yawn that made the rest sleepy. “But it's really boring on the second floor. It's been four days, but Qin Yuanhao doesn't have any intentions of leaving his house. He either meditates or meditates; he doesn't even have any form of entertainment.

“If you ask me, I'd say that we might as well pretend to be jianghu entertainers. I'll go to Qin Yuanhao’s house to perform xiangsheng comedy while you perform lifting huge vats. While he's distracted, Man Gu can plant an eavesdropping talisman or something.”

Lu Yang and Man Gu completely ignored Meng Jingzhou. The best solution to deal with a talkative fellow was to pretend they didn't exist.

Noticing that no one was paying attention to him, Meng Jingzhou could only change the topic. “Man Gu, are you seriously not considering making the skewers taste worse?”

Man Gu had his own staunch principles. “Our family is a barbeque ancestral clan. All eighteen generations of us can barbecue. I can't ruin the reputation of our Barbarian Tribe!”

Chapter 56: An Underling Must Strictly Follow Their Boss’ Orders

That was the truth. The Barbarian Tribe’s primary cooking method was barbeque.

Man Gu’s eyes were ablaze with a fervent fighting spirit.

Lu Yang didn't know what to say. Why must your fighting spirit be ablaze here? We’re here to infiltrate the diabolic creed, not open chain stores for your family!

He sighed. Since Man Gu was unwilling to lower the quality, they could only raise the price.

“Dear guests, what wine would you like?”

The two jianghu heroes were open-minded people and shouted unrestrainedly, “The stronger the better! I’m known in the jianghu as the one who never gets drunk even after a thousand cups!”

The other person also yelled, “And I’m known in the jianghu as the one who never gets drunk after ten thousand cups!”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Stop boasting, the two of you. Are you sure you can handle it if I serve you two bottles of pure alcohol?

In the end, Lu Yang served them two bottles of Laobaigan Liquor,[1] hoping that their alcohol tolerance was really as good as they had bragged.

Standing at the entrance to take care of the customers, Lu Yang hollered, “Please take a queue number and don’t cut the queue. We have prepared complimentary tea and snacks for everyone. We seek your kind patience. A table will free up soon!

“Also, there are no discounts even if you bring in new customers; stop bringing in new people!”

Although Lu Yang wasn’t sure if it would be effective, he decided to shout a few times first. We musn’t open a chain store.

The people lining up were restless and bombarded him with questions.

“Can we reserve a table in advance?”

“Do you offer doorstep delivery?”

“Can we book the whole venue?”

Apart from heroes, there were also cultivators, and they were swimming in money.

“Reservations are possible.

“If it’s not too far away, we can do doorstep delivery, but there’ll be an additional service fee.

“There’s no problem with booking the whole venue.”

Lu Yang wished someone would just book the place so that he could have some peace.

“Attention, everyone! Qin Yuanhao has left his estate.” Lu Yang and Man Gu received Meng Jingzhou’s auditory message at the same time. The former felt a surprising sense of relief.

“I’ll go follow him; you come down and switch with me. And Man Gu, keep an eye on him and don’t let him cause a mess.”

As Lu Yang had grasped two spells, Shrinking Earth and To Inches, he had an overwhelming advantage in battle and tailing people. Since he couldn’t just dive into the soil in public, he went to the backyard where there were two tiger-henchman ghosts busy with barbeque, their heads covered in sweat from exhaustion. They wished they could grow eight more arms to work. Their movements were so rapid that they almost seemed to blur.

They probably haven’t experienced such fulfilling and busy lives when they were alive.

In addition, the tiger-henchman ghosts were wearing clothes of traveling merchants from when they were alive. To prevent drunk drinkers from running to the backyard and accidentally noticing something wrong with the tiger-henchman ghosts’ clothes, the trio had spent half a day studying how they could change the tiger-henchman ghosts’ clothes—from getting a Daoist to hold a ritual and getting monks to chant scriptures to browsing through ancient books and verifying legends. By the time they neared the end, the two tiger-henchman ghosts had become more transparent.

Fortunately, Lu Yang found the simplest solution—burn the clothes for the tiger-henchman ghosts.[2]

As the two tiger-henchman ghosts were engrossed with work, they didn’t even notice that Lu Yang had come. The latter successfully sank into the ground, and he gingerly tailed Qin Yuanhao.

After Meng Jingzhou quickly changed his clothes to take over for Lu Yang, he served some lamb skewers. “Lamb skewers are ready; do enjoy, dear guest.

“When it comes to these lamb skewers, they have quite the story. Please hear me out slowly. There was this one day when golden light radiated in the northern grassland. A baby was born...”

~~~

When Qin Yuanhao walked in the dark, his figure seemed to almost blend in with the night. Even the passers-by didn’t notice his presence.

“A technique related to shadows or related to darkness?” Lu Yang observed secretly as he tried his best to collect information.

For the purpose of creating his own techniques, he read extensively and gained some knowledge of the manifold types of techniques.

Lu Yang continued to follow Qin Yuanhao. The latter stepped onto a muddy lane and arrived at the winding small alley. Despite hiding underground, Lu Yang could still smell the stench.

Hearing Qin Yuanhao’s hastening footsteps, Lu Yang could deduce that the other party was in a foul mood.

Qin Yuanhao furrowed his brow, not liking such a place. With his face darkened as he kicked open a room’s door, he startled his underlings who were deep asleep.

“You still have the mood to sleep?!”

The underlings hurriedly got up and trembled, not understanding why their boss had flown into a rage. We have worked hard and never dared to slack off. After being busy the whole day, is it wrong to sleep at night?!

On the contrary, Boss doesn’t sleep at night and doesn’t wake up in the morning. Compared to our boss, our schedules are much too regular.

Qin Yuanhao kicked the underling to the wall, questioning with wrath. “Why has no one reported to me these few days? What about the people I told you to look for?!”

The underling felt as if a hammer had just smashed his heart, and he said in an aggrieved manner, “Boss, you said that we can only return when we find the people.

“We couldn’t find the people you mentioned and didn’t dare to go look for you. Why are we also wrong for listening to your orders?”

The underling felt wronged. As an underling, I do whatever my Big Brother says, yet he’s not even satisfied with this; he’s so hard to please.

Qin Yuanhao fell silent. He actually thought that the underling made a good point.

But I just want to hit him; what should I do?

“If you’re not coming to see me, don’t you know how to write a letter?”

“But you said that important matters have to be reported in person.”

Qin Yuanhao flared up. “Didn’t I say that special situations call for special measures?!”

“You did say that special situations call for special measures, but you also mentioned that whether something constitutes a special situation requires us to discuss it internally before you make the final decision.”

“So did you discuss?”

“We’ve discussed it two days ago. We unanimously agree that it’s a special situation this time around and that it will need your judgment and decision.”

“Then why don’t I see all of you letting me decide?!”

“You said that important matters must be reported in person. Since we still couldn’t find the person who started the rumor, we couldn’t go meet you.”

Qin Yuanhao was at a loss of words.

Am I going to die from this never-ending spiral today?

He took in two deep mouthfuls of air, then repeatedly warned himself not to kill anyone. This group of underlings may be inflexible, but they’re loyal to me and carry out all my orders strictly without the slightest deviation.

Killing the underlings would cause others to become disillusioned. Besides, I don’t have many trustworthy subordinates to begin with. If I kill more, there’ll be none left.

“What exactly is the progress with searching for that person? Even if you can't find them, you should at the very least have some clues, right?” Qin Yuanhao stared at the underling. If you dare to say that no clues have been found, you can forget about staying alive today!

Do you really think I don’t dare to kill people?!

The underling muttered softly, “No.” Sensing his boss’ gaze filled with killing intent, he quickly added, “Big Brother, you also know how special the people you’re looking for are. As long as they had revealed their faces in public, they would have attracted attention. However, four days have passed, and our brothers can’t find anything even after running until their feet have grown blisters.

“Putting everything else aside, just based on the traits of being eight feet tall and eight feet wide, we’ve inquired all around and only found one who meets the conditions. However, they either have no pockmarks, don’t eat children, or have a rather pleasant appearance.”

“Who is it?” Qin Yuanhao thought to himself, Let’s not care about whether the appearances are similar. Just like how we slaughter a chicken to scare the monkey, we kill someone with a similar figure first to scare the rest as a warning so that we won’t accidentally be underestimated by people in the shadows.

“It’s the mascot that sells tofu on Qianmen Street.”

“I’m so going to slaughter you!”

1. It’s a Chinese brand of liquor. ☜

2. People burn items and paper money as offerings to the dead. ☜

Chapter 57: Gains

The Luodi Merchant Guild’s business strategy was rather progressive. To broaden their brand recognition, they created the concept of a “brand mascot” and invited a master artist Xuan-Daozi. After three revisions, the decided first draft was a mascot.

This first draft featured a chubby little pig holding a coin.

After the Luodi Merchant Guild introduced their brand mascot, their fame indeed grew significantly. When many other businesses learned of it, they followed suit, creating their own unique mascots.

One such business was the tofu store on Qianmen Street in Yanjiang Commandery.

Qin Yuanhao didn't end up killing his underling. Upon regaining his composure and giving it further thought, he realized that his underlings were down-to-earth with their work and never slipped up. If they said that they couldn't find those people, it really means that they couldn't.

It can't possibly be the tofu store’s mascot running about and starting rumors.

“To have such distinctive features but still untraceable? It looks like my fellow diabolic creed members are framing me!” Qin Yuanhao sneered.

How can I still not figure out that someone has deliberately set me up? But I just don't know who.

This was not uncommon in diabolic creeds. Qin Yuanhao himself had done his fair share of harming his fellow members.

Since there were still no leads after all this time, Qin Yuanhao could only swallow this loss disgruntledly and slowly plan who he should take revenge on. “If you can't find them, then there's no need to keep searching.” Qin Yuanhao took out a stack of papers and a few silvers and tossed them to the underling.

This was also a reason for not killing his underlings. Someone must do the work assigned by the branch leader. If I kill them now, where else am I going to look for a replacement?

“Early the next morning, gather all our brothers and go to the nearest eight commanderies. Secretly disseminate these papers in the black market. These silvers will be your stipend and travel expenses. Do you understand?”

“Yes, yes, I understand.” The underling was frightened by Qin Yuanhao”s last bellow.

“Louder.”

“Understood!” The underling straightened his back and shouted until his neck turned red.

The middle-aged woman from next door yelled angrily, her voice resounding through the wall, “Do you know what time it is now? Why are you shouting?”

She shouted even more loudly than the underling.

Killing intent flashed in Qin Yuanhao’s eyes.

“Big Brother, she is a Foundation Establishment cultivator who is here to live in seclusion,” the underling quickly explained.

Many cultivators liked playing around in the mortal world. Who knew if those selling barbeque skewers on the street were all cultivators?

Qin Yuanhao snorted, saying nothing as he left.

The underling yawned. Boss has finally left. He then fell asleep as soon as his head hit his pillow. There was still work for him tomorrow morning.

Qin Yuanhao’s underlings would often receive some random, incomprehensible tasks from him. To maintain secrecy, he wouldn’t tell his underlings anything, only demanding that they follow his instructions.

It was the same this time around.

After the underling was fast asleep, Lu Yang darted out from the ground. He swiped away three pieces of paper and followed Qin Yuanhao. The latter had only come out to look for his underlings. Once he was done giving his instructions, he went back.

When Qin Yuanhao passed by One More Time Barbeque Shop, he paused for a moment. “I went into seclusion for just four days and a new barbeque shop has already opened up? And it’s already so popular?”

Qin Yuanhao suddenly had the urge to get a meal. It doesn’t matter if there are many people; I can just cut in line. You’re already lucky to have a Foundation Establishment cultivator like me coming to your small place to eat and not making you kneel to receive me. Yet you still want me to wait in line?

However, Qin Yuanhao finally dismissed the idea. Something like barbeque is more enjoyable when there are many people; eating alone is just not as fun.

“I’ll save it for next time.” Qin Yuanhao went home.

Lu Yang returned to the barbeque shop to help out. As soon as he got back, he saw Meng Jingzhou performing xiangsheng comedy. The diners were even applauding and clamoring for an encore, “One More Time!”

Lu Yang took a deep breath. I see that the two of you really want to make this barbeque shop a big success...

Sensing Lu Yang’s knife-cutting gaze, Meng Jingzhou quickly shut his mouth and obediently resumed his role as a waiter, though he would ignore all the diners’ calls.

After a while, the diners gradually left, and the barbeque shop finally regained its peace. The two tiger-henchman ghosts tidied up the grills and utensils and took stock of the ingredients used for the day, estimating the amount of ingredients they needed to buy for the next day. On the other hand, the trio sat on the second floor, discussing their gains for today.

“How much silver did we earn today?” Meng Jingzhou rubbed his hand excitedly. Starting a business from scratch gave him a strong sense of achievement.

“Who’s talking about that kind of gain?!” Lu Yang slammed the table and glared at him. “Did you forget what we came here for?”

“Open a chain store?” Man Gu was still thinking about expanding his family business and taking it to great heights.

Lu Yang stopped paying attention to the two fools. He took out three pieces of paper and recounted the events of the night from following Qin Yuanhao.

“White paper?” Meng Jingzhou took a piece of paper and examined both sides but couldn’t make any sense of it.

Lu Yang also didn’t know how to reveal the content on the paper. “Qin Yuanhao told his people to spread these papers to the black market, so there must be some information on them. It’s just that we don’t know how to identify and decipher them. Is it a special communication method between diabolic creeds?”

Meng Jingzhou nodded, agreeing with Lu Yang’s conjecture. “Very possible; these sneaky fellows often like to use secret codes and the like. This is a paper for all diabolic cultivators, and all of them need to get it. If even we, at the Foundation Establishment Stage, can’t see the text on the paper, it’s all the more impossible for a Qi Training diabolic cultivator to be able to see it.

“So the problem doesn’t lie in the secret code but rather the paper.”

Lu Yang mused over it for a bit, then heated the paper over the charcoal fire.

“What are you doing?” Man Gu was baffled.

Lu Yang carefully heated the paper, casually explaining, “I read in a book that if you write on paper with sugar water, the text will be invisible after it dries. You need high heat to remove the water from the sugar, which then reveals brown-colored text.”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu found this piece of knowledge to be very interesting.

After five minutes of heating, nothing appeared on the paper, so Lu Yang could only abandon this method. He summoned a small ball of water on his palm and suddenly squeezed it until it burst. The mist of water droplets sputtered out and landed on the white paper.

“What are you doing now?”

Lu Yang explained, “Special liquids like body wash and laundry detergent are very water absorbent. When they are used for writing, the text will be invisible after it dries. Only by sprinkling water on the paper and making use of the concept of different absorption rates can the characters be revealed.”

The Central Continent might seem to be similar to historical times, but it actually wasn’t the case. Due to the existence of spells, be it by design or by coincidence, there were many things here that didn't belong to ancient times. Such examples were the body wash and laundry detergent Lu Yang had mentioned.

Unfortunately, there was still nothing on the paper.

Lu Yang wasn’t discouraged. After pondering for a while more, he came up with a new idea. “Since this is a communication method among the diabolic path, perhaps we have to use methods common to them to decipher it?”

Lu Yang bit his thumb and let a few drops of blood fall onto the paper. The blood seemed to have come alive, swimming across the paper’s surface.

“As I thought, this is a method used by the diabolic path for forging paper, so it can’t be judged by normal standards.” Lu Yang heaved a sigh of relief. I’ve finally succeeded.

There seemed to be many invisible grooves on the white paper. Wherever the blood flowed, it would fill these grooves and form characters.

“On the first day of the fourth month, the Everlasting Creed’s Yanjiang Branch will recruit new members. The exact location will be announced the day before the recruitment.”

Chapter 58: This Is Not How Animal Form Fist Is Done

The Everlasting Creed was one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds.

“The Everlasting Creed... I remember that they worship the Everlasting Immortal. They claim that the Everlasting Immortal never dies or perishes, existing for eternity. When one becomes a devout follower, they can avoid the three calamities and five tribulations of cultivation[1] and extend their lifespan,” Meng Jingzhou recounted the information he had.

These were just the most basic details that anyone could obtain with just a bit of effort, but the veracity remained to be uncertain.

“Since the Everlasting Creed is recruiting, this is actually a good opportunity for us. When the time comes, with all sorts of people mixed in, the entry requirements will be much lower, and they won't be too strict when verifying our identities.” Lu Yang was elated.

This is good news! I was just fretting over how the three of us have never practiced legitimate diabolic cultivation techniques and whether we can use the Ghost Commanding Spell to muddle through. But Qin Yuanhao happened to bring us such great news; he's our lucky star!

“Then do we still kill Qin Yuanhao?” Man Gu asked. It seems like there's no need to kill him anymore.

“Regardless, he is still a scourge, so we should kill him if we can, but let's not use his bone tablet,” Lu Yang replied.

No matter whether we can infiltrate the diabolic creed, we still need to kill Qin Yuanhao. For a diabolic cultivator to reach the Intermediate or Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, it's impossible to not have blood on their hands.

Don't be fooled by how Qin Yuanhao didn't kill his underlings. That's not because he is soft-hearted but rather because they were still useful. However, when the underling loses a limb and becomes cumbersome in movement, they'll lose their usefulness to Qin Yuanhao. That's when they'll definitely die.

“Why can't we use the bone tablet?”

Lu Yang called the two tiger-henchman ghosts to serve some skewers, and he explained as he munched on them, “The relationship between diabolic creed members isn't as good as we think. If we frame Qin Yuanhao, he'll investigate and conclude that someone in the diabolic creed has it out for him.

“If we use Qin Yuanhao’s bone tablet to enter the diabolic creed, we'll be marked as Qin Yuanhao’s people. They might make things difficult for us, and it wouldn't be worth it then.”

Realization hit Man Gu.

Lu Yang chuckled. “But the diabolic creed is really prudent. To prevent the location of the base from being leaked, they're only going to announce it at the last minute. Are they afraid that the righteous path will exterminate them after finding out their location?

“We will continue to tail Qin Yuanhao and see if we can find the Yanjiang Branch that way. We can also make the necessary preparations.

“It's getting late. Time to cultivate or rest as you see fit. Let's call it a day.”

~~~

The next morning, Lu Yang yawned after waking up. He got dressed and ate breakfast with the rest. Man Gu had prepared beef offal soup[2].

He had already returned from the market, having pushed back a cart that was loaded with pork, beef, and mutton.

He simmered beef femur bone to make the soup base as well as added a pinch of salt along with other seasoning. After the beef offal bubbled away for a while, a piping hot bowl of beef offal soup was ready.

Lu Yang yelled, “Add more beef tripe.”

“Gotcha.”

After a satisfying breakfast, everyone went about their respective tasks.

Man Gu was supposed to be on monitoring duty today, so he ran to the second floor, planning to sit there for the whole day.

Meng Jingzhou was not one to keep still. Just like an excited rabbit, he had run off somewhere, probably to cause trouble for others.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts worked on butchering a variety of meat, chopping the vegetables, and preparing the skewers. The past four days had allowed them to familiarize themselves with the process. Skewering from morning to evening, they would be just in time for opening the shop and receiving customers at night. Afterward, they'll go to the backyard to heat the charcoal and start the grill, barbecuing for the whole night.

As they worked from morning to night, it could be said that they had a fulfilling time.

Lu Yang also had his own matters to attend to. He took out Animal Form Fist, trying to see if he could grasp the rudiments. As he hadn't practiced martial arts before, he was uncertain deep inside.

“There's a first time for everything.”

Lu Yang set up the simplest Soundproofing Array so that no sound could pass in or out. Sitting cross-legged, he industriously flipped through the book. “Animal Form Fist—a fist technique that mimics the special abilities and form of various animals as well as the combat and living states of humans. It includes the Tiger Fist, Monkey Fist, Eagle Claw Fist, Snake Fist, and more. This book only contains the Tiger Fist.

“The Tiger Fist places emphasis on imitating a tiger’s form, borrowing its techniques, internalizing it with reason, and merging them into a fist intent.

“The Tiger Fist’s sequence is short, concise, and compact, while its foot stance and footwork are smaller with a focus on the three-seven stance.

“To master Tiger Fist, the most dangerous step lies in observing tigers. It is best to have experience in fighting a tiger. Only then can one deeply understand a tiger’s combat stance and better imitate it.”

The hardest step was instead the easiest for Lu Yang; he had already fought against a tiger and won.

He closed his eyes slowly.

The roars, pounces, and tearing movements of the tiger during their battle replayed vividly in Lu Yang’s mind. Although the tiger demon had been killed by him, he couldn’t help but acknowledge that the tiger demon was a formidable opponent and that there were areas he could learn from it.

Of course, it calling its wife for help is something I don’t need to learn; I can’t learn it now either.

The tiger demon’s figure and his own figure gradually overlapped, integrating into one, and his human form now possessed the skills of a tiger.

In Lu Yang’s mind, he repeatedly simulated the movements of Tiger Fist. The originally awkward movements became increasingly fluid, as if a tiger had possessed his body and was roaring in his mind. This was something that could only be done upon reaching the Foundation Establishment Stage. It had high requirements for one’s spiritual consciousness. Mortal martial artists wouldn’t be able to accomplish this.

Lu Yang opened his eyes, revealing a fierce glint and a ferocious tiger hidden in his eyes. Leaping into the air, he landed steadily and assumed a stance. His voice and breathing were full of vigor. As energy surged within him, he stomped the ground in a display of might, exuding a ferocious and intense aura.

Hearing the sounds of Lu Yang’s fist, the two tiger-henchman ghosts skewering inside shuddered. They initially thought that the tiger demon had been resurrected, cautiously peeking out of the door. Only after realizing that it was not the tiger demon did they reassuringly continue preparing the skewers.

After completing a set of moves, Lu Yang found his entire body to be energized, brimming with endless strength that needed to be unleashed. Seizing this opportunity, he practiced a few more sets, each set more fluid than the previous one, and every move of his was firm and powerful.

Regardless of how much of it could be applied in an actual battle, right now, even a Tiger Fist master couldn’t find any flaw with Lu Yang.

“No, there’s still room for improvement.”

Lu Yang’s movements grew increasingly faster, though his heart remained as calm as a lake and a mirror. He had reached a wondrous state; every movement of his revealed his comprehension of the fist technique. As he threw fists and delivered kicks, his comprehension deepened, and a faint phantom image of the tiger demon appeared behind Lu Yang.

“Roar!”

When Lu Yang’s comprehension reached its peak, all of it culminated in this one tiger roar that was utterly satisfying.

“Hmm? Why am I lying prone on the ground?” Lu Yang came back to his senses, finding himself in an inexplicably strange position. When he wanted to stand up, his legs felt weak, and even after teetering and stumbling a few times, he still couldn’t get up.

“What’s going on?”

How could there be a mishap from just practicing fists? My talent in fist techniques is pretty high, so how could there be a problem?

A sense of unease crept over Lu Yang. With both his hands and legs, he crawled to the side of a water vat.

Lu Yang finally saw his current appearance.

He had turned into a tiger.

I have successfully mastered Tiger Fist; how delightful.

“Lu Yang, guess what I saw on the streets? There was a tofu shop with a very interesting mascot.” Meng Jingzhou had just come back from strolling around. Having heard that Lu Yang was practicing fists in the backyard, he wanted to check on his progress.

Then he saw a tiger crouching over the side of the water vat as if looking into a mirror.

“Holy crap, a demon!”

1. The three calamities are likely referring to fire, water, and wind. ☜

2. An example of niuzatang or beef offal soup. ☜

Chapter 59: Lu-Style Animal Form Fist

“Holy crap, a demon!” Meng Jingzhou shrieked, swinging his arms and ready to strike.

Nobody could blame him for having such a reaction. The backyard was originally supposed to be where Lu Yang was practicing his fist techniques, but he had now vanished, and a tiger had appeared instead. It was easy to assume that the tiger demon had revived and devoured Lu Yang.

The “tiger demon” uttered human words, sounding exactly like Lu Yang, “Demon your grandfather; it’s me!”

“It even has the same voice as Lu Yang!” Meng Jingzhou was horrified.

One human and one tiger leaped into the air. Stupefied by the voice of the “tiger demon,” Meng Jingzhou, he couldn't react in time and was swatted to the ground by Lu Yang’s paw.

Lu Yang snorted coldly. There aren't even traces of a struggle here in the courtyard, so how could I have been eaten by the tiger demon? This brat clearly recognizes me but is deliberately playing dumb.

Meng Jingzhou clicked his tongue. Lu Yang hadn’t really hit him just now. Besides, his skin was coarse and thick enough that it didn't hurt at all.

He stood up and dusted himself off, looking at Lu Yang suspiciously. “What on earth is going on here? Weren't you comprehending Animal Form Fist? Why did you learn the Shapeshifting Technique instead?”

“Hold on a bit, let me figure out how to turn myself back.” The “tiger demon” Lu Yang scratched the back of his head but realized that his paw couldn't reach. He had to sit down then use his hind paw to scratch... Forget it, I won't scratch; it's too detrimental to my image.

Lu Yang bared his teeth. He truly hadn't expected that practicing fists could lead to so many bizarre troubles.

Now that I think about it, only my sword technique is considered normal.

Should I say that I live up to the expectations of a Sword Spirit Root?

Meng Jingzhou scampered up the stairs and called Man Gu to come down.

“What’s the deal? I'm monitoring Qin Yuanhao right now.”

“I have something fun to show you.”

Meng Jingzhou dragged the confused Man Gu to the backyard where they saw the familiar “tiger demon.”

“Demon, give my Brother Lu’s life back!” Man Gu bellowed and charged at Lu Yang without any hesitation. As he still hadn't fully processed what was going on, he didn't hold back.

Seeing how the situation had escalated, Meng Jingzhou quickly hugged Man Gu by the waist, imploring the Barbarian Tribe big guy to calm down. “Don't hit, don't hit him! This is Lu Yang.”

The two tiger-henchman ghosts who were skewering heard the commotion in the backyard. Out of curiosity, they secretly ran over to peek at what was happening, only to be frightened out of their wits.

The tiger demon has really revived this time!

“Tiger demon” Lu Yang rolled his eyes, ignoring this group of people. He instead focused on how to turn himself back. Closing his eyes, he silently recited “Return to normal” thrice.

By the time Lu Yang opened his eyes again, he had already regained his original appearance.

After all that chaos, the trio could finally sit down and ponder over what had happened just now.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts also heaved a sigh of relief and went back to skewering. Tonight’s business will definitely be better than yesterday’s; we have to prepare more skewers.

“So, here’s what happened, I was practicing Animal Form Fist just now...” Lu Yang began to elucidate slowly.

When Man Gu heard Lu Yang mention that he was practicing Animal Form Fist, he felt as if he suffered a traumatic blow to his worldview. He blurted out, “Is this Animal Form Fist or Animal Shapeshifting Fist?”[1]

The sages were right—reading ten thousand books isn’t enough, a thousand li of travel is also necessary. Where would you find something like this in a book? I should stick closer to Brother Lu and Meng Jingzhou in their travels.

I have truly broadened my horizons.

Meng Jingzhou’s reaction was not much better than Man Gu’s. He stared at Lu Yang with an odd expression.

I thought you were practicing a spell, yet you’re telling me that you were practicing fists just now? Who on earth can achieve results like yours from practicing martial arts?

Originally, Meng Jingzhou had already found it weird enough that Lu Yang’s ghost commandment technique ended up with his soul leaving his body. He hadn’t expected that something even more peculiar could have happened.

Lu Yang was confident with his words as he shared his unique insights into Animal Form Fist. “Think about it, isn’t the essence of Animal Form Fist imitating animals? Tiger Fist, Monkey Fist, Crane Fist, and so on, don’t they all mimic tigers, monkeys, and cranes?”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu nodded.

Lu Yang pressed on, “Precisely! In that case, the better the imitation, the better the effects and the stronger the power are, am I right?”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu nodded.

“I just had a close exchange with the tiger demon, so I’m the most familiar with Tiger Fist. Naturally, I picked it up the fastest and learned it the best, right?”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu continued to nod.

Lu Yang continued, “With that in mind, I practiced fists, and as I became engrossed in practicing, I suddenly turned into a tiger. That makes perfect sense, right?”

Meng Jingzhou was just about to nod when he caught himself just in time. “What sense?! They’re poles apart!”

Man Gu still nodded dumbly.

Lu Yang spread his hands in exasperation. I’m the one feeling the most helpless here. I was just practicing according to the manual but with a teeny bit of my own comprehension. “Why don’t you two also give it a try? Who knows if you might learn the Shapeshifting Technique this way?”

Excitement sparkled in Meng Jingzhou’s and Man Gu’s eyes. It would be amazing if we could learn the Shapeshifting Technique through practicing fists. Although it’s said that the Shapeshifting Technique is used by those shady cultivators, learning an extra skill can’t possibly hurt. Who knows if it might come in handy one day?

With Lu Yang, the fist technique master, guiding them, the two quickly picked up Tiger Fist, their moves as mighty as a tiger.[2]

However, they just couldn’t figure out the most pivotal shapeshifting aspect.

While the two practiced, Lu Yang didn’t let himself be idle. As he watched their movements, another idea sprouted in his heart.

Animal Form Fist is a fist technique that imitates, so why do we have to limit ourselves to animals? Why can’t we imitate humans?

This unstoppable idea took off like a wild horse free of its reins.

The prerequisite for Animal Form Fist was to be very familiar with the subject of imitation. Lu Yang’s eyes lit up as he saw the two people occupied with practicing fists.

Aren’t they the best examples? I have already mastered the core tenets of Animal Form Fist. It’s time for innovation.

“Only by weeding out the old and bringing forth the new can there be improvement; to advance, one must innovate!”

Lu Yang acted on his thoughts right away. Closing his eyes once more, he recalled Man Gu’s actions, and his body began to move.

In the midst of his practice, Man Gu noticed Lu Yang’s movements, finding them uncannily familiar, but he just couldn’t place a finger to it.

“Isn’t that...me?” Man Gu was swift to realize, but he didn’t understand what Lu Yang was up to.
