The person in question was again immersed in wondrous comprehension. His body changed gradually until he actually turned into Man Gu!

“Haha, I’ve succeeded! I knew my theory was correct.” Lu Yang guffawed with Man Gu’s face, which gave off a very queer and contradictory vibe.

Exclamation marks were shooting out of Man Gu’s head. What just happened? How did he turn into me in the blink of an eye? Why is it different from the Animal Form Fist I know? You can use Animal Form Fist to imitate people too?

“Brother Man Gu, I didn’t know you could laugh like that... Holy crap, two Man Gus?” Meng Jingzhou was in the middle of practicing when he heard a different kind of laughter. Instinctively finding that something was off, he turned to look.

Dang, one real and one fake Man Gus?!

“Wait, the new Man Gu is actually Lu Yang!”

Meng Jingzhou sized up Lu Yang. He does look like Man Gu in terms of appearance, but the expression and demeanor are way different.

It’s obvious at one glance that Man Gu is a straightforward and honest person. The Lu Yang version of him looks like a bad egg with plenty of nasty tricks in his mind.

He had already given up on learning Animal Form Fist. Even if he had originally wanted to learn it to pick up shapeshifting, seeing Lu Yang like this made him realize that he definitely couldn’t master it.

This already has totally nothing to do with Animal Form Fist.

After Lu Yang mastered the technique, he switched from Man Gu to Meng Jingzhou fairly smoothly.

“This is really the Shapeshifting Technique right?”

“This is Lu-Style Animal Form Fist.” Lu Yang clasped his hands behind his back and gazed up at the sky at an angle of forty-five degrees, looking the part of a fist technique expert.

(Don’t ask why Lu Yang still had his clothes on after turning from a tiger demon back into human form—this is a proper novel.)

1. In the original text, the name of the two techniques differ by only one word. I am using “Animal Shapeshifting Fist” here for the effect, but I will be defaulting to only “shapeshifting” hereafter. ☜

2. The original plays on a Chinese idiom that includes the character “tiger.” ☜

Chapter 60: The Constables and the Thieves

“My Lu-Style Animal Form Fist is vast and profound, not something a Single’s Spirit Root like you can comprehend.

“As the saying goes, the heavens are nine layers high, the earth is nine layers deep; the Lu-Style is also divided into nine realms.

“At the moment, I have only reached the first realm. When I have reached the higher realms, I'll be able to obtain the transformation subject's power, spells, and even cultivation. If I attain the ninth realm in the future, becoming a Transcendent Tribulation expert simply requires a single thought, and overpowering Big Senior Sister won't break a sweat!”

Lu Yang was so pleased with himself that Man Gu almost believed him. The latter stealthily asked Meng Jingzhou, “Is Brother Lu telling the truth?”

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. “Truth my ass. It's so obvious that it's all made up. If you are willing to listen, I can fabricate eight different versions for you.”

“Oh,” Man Gu let out. He marveled at Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou's ability to concoct lies on the spot.

~~~

A few days had passed since Lu Yang bestowed a new meaning to Animal Form Fist. Their customers were increasing by the day, and some enjoyed themselves so much that they tipped spirit stones.

“Didn't we raise the prices? Why are there still so many people?” Lu Yang gnawed his teeth. The biggest restaurant in Yanjiang Commandery even offered to buy our recipe yesterday.

That said, he was the only one gnashing his teeth. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were quite delighted.

Man Gu was on duty today to spy on Qin Yuanhao upstairs while Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou worked as waiters downstairs.

While suppressing the urge to start performing xiangsheng comedy, Meng Jingzhou sent an auditory message, “I heard that there was a table of cultivators here a few days ago. After eating, they were full of praise for us, saying that our food tasted better than that of any spirit chef they knew.

“And just like that, word spread from one to ten, ten to a hundred, and now many cultivators know about our restaurant.”

Despite the Dao-Seeking Sect being full of spirit chefs, spirit chefs were actually a very rare cultivator type. In Yanjiang Commandery, they could be counted on one hand, and most of them were at the Qi Training Stage, with only one at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Spirit chefs place particular emphasis on the mutual generation of the Five Elements. The food they made were not only delicious but could also improve one’s cultivation, achieving a union between the two.

On the other hand, Man Gu’s barbeque skewers definitely couldn’t increase one’s cultivation, but they excelled in flavor. The cultivators in Yanjiang Commandery thought that since they couldn’t get to eat spirit chefs’ food to enhance their cultivation, at least they could eat barbeque skewers that tasted better than what the spirit chefs made.

Even though the barbeque skewers were ten times more expensive, they were still considered a bargain in the eyes of cultivators.

“We’ve gained a bit of fame among the middle- and upper-class circles in Yanjiang Commandery. Many commoners whose finances aren’t tight are also following the trend of coming here to eat. I think they also treat it as something to brag about. We are not far away from expanding our business across the continent. Are you excited?”

“Excited your hammer.” Lu Yang rolled his eyes before quickly welcoming a new batch of customers.

“Boss, the first floor is already full; can’t we go to the second floor?” A customer noticed that the lights were on upstairs and thought that it would be a good spot.

“The second floor is currently under renovation and is not open to guests. We kindly seek your understanding.” Even if he didn’t have the intention of growing the barbeque shop, Lu Yang still carried out his role as a waiter assiduously, not having the tiniest bit of intention to slack off.

The customers could only resign themselves to join the queue.

“Haha, it’s finally our turn! Boss, I brought my brothers here again!” A few bailiffs in black plainclothes came to the barbeque shop. Their waist tablets inscribed with their identity and long sabers hung at their waists, exuding an intimidating presence.

The people lining up behind them instinctively kept their distance from them, trepidation gripping their hearts.

“Captain Wei, you’re here.” Lu Yang smiled, as if he was well acquainted with these people.

They were constables from Yanjiang Commandery. Their captain, surnamed Wei, had a full beard and spoke with an air of authority. People gave him the nickname “Iron-Faced Captain.” His cultivation was at the Foundation Establishment Stage, and not just the hooligans but even members of diabolic creeds avoided dealing with them, fearing that they would be targeted and afflicted with endless troubles.

The few constables behind were also not ordinary, with the weakest one at Level Six Qi Training. In a xianxia world, one couldn’t become a constable without some cultivation.

This was already Captain Wei’s fourth time here, so Lu Yang was somewhat familiar with him.

There were initially a few people who thought their cultivation to be a rung above the others and wanted to cut the queue, but as soon as they learned that Captain Wei came here often for supper, they fell back in place.

“We just got off duty and changed shifts, so I brought the brothers here for your skewers. I have to say, your barbeque skewers are really something else. Once I’ve tasted them, I can’t forget them.” Captain Wei smacked his lips, almost salivating at the thought of their barbeque skewers.

“Being a constable is also not easy, eh? You have to work a night shift every two days,” Lu Yang sighed as he led them to a private room.

Once they were inside, the constables took off their outer coats.

”Ugh, speaking of which, it’s been annoying lately. For some reason, many cultivators are streaming into Yanjiang Commandery, and they don’t seem like good people. It’s been putting quite a bit of pressure on public security.

“The commandery governor has issued multiple orders to ensure that nothing goes wrong, so I had no choice but to patrol more often with the brothers. After we’re done with our patrol, I come here to reward them.”

Seeing that Lu Yang was quite busy, Captain Wei didn’t elaborate further and began ordering the dishes.

“Still the same set as the last time?” Lu Yang asked as Captain Wei had ordered the same barbeque skewers the last three times.

“Let’s try something new this time. I already wanted to try it the last time, but the brothers stopped me. Give me ten skewers of roasted eyes, ten skewers of roasted silkworm pupae, and ten skewers of centipede.” Captain Wei hurriedly placed the order, not giving his brothers the chance to react.

They groaned in agony. These things don’t even sound edible.

“Look at all of you, pampered and spoiled. One day, I’ll take all of you to the wilderness and spend half a month there for a mission without Fasting Pills. Let’s see what you eat then!”

After the barbeque skewers and wine arrived, the constables dug into their food, savoring every fragrant bite. As they enjoyed their meals, a few constables began pouring their hearts out, cursing about their unfortunate encounters.

“Damn it, those thieves have been so slippery lately; they didn’t leave any clues behind at all.”

“It must have been the work of cultivators. Otherwise, even a veteran wouldn’t be so adept.”

“I reckon it’s those foreign cultivators.”

“After we catch these bastards, I’m definitely going to whip them a hundred and eighty times, then throw them into the water prison!”

The thieves had been wreaking havoc recently, yet they were still not apprehended, making it look bad for the constables. Captain Wei complained, “The commandery governor even ordered me to solve this case within a month. If he’s so capable, why doesn’t he do it himself?! These thieves even stole from the influential Li and Lü families today. The Li Family is also the commandery governor’s relative. The commandery governor is surely going to put pressure on me again tomorrow.”

In the private room next door, a customer who looked like the leader of a gang placed the day’s loot on the dining table. “Today’s haul was worth it. Old rules apply, I’ll take four-tenth, and the rest is evenly split among the brothers.”

The men were grinning from ear to ear; it had been a big harvest for them today. “Before coming, I heard how formidable Constable Captain Wei is and his nickname ‘Iron-Faced Captain.’ But from what I see, he’s nothing special. He can’t even catch a whiff of our fart!”

“That’s too harsh. He at least gets to catch a whiff of our fart.”

“The Li and Lü families are really wealthy, especially this person surnamed Ma. His cultivation isn’t high, but he has lots of good stuff.”

“Come come come, let’s drink and eat to our heart’s content; my treat today! No one is allowed to sober up. Tonight, we’re not stopping until we’re drunk!”

The thieves heartily drank to their fill. One of them stepped out to use the toilet but accidentally entered the wrong door, walking into Captain Wei’s private room instead.

“Uh...Big Brother, why do you all look different...and also uglier?”

“Where did this drunkard come from? Get lost!” a constable snapped. They were still stressed over where they could arrest the thieves, yet a drunkard was now making a din.

The thief was enraged and tried to start a fight, but how could he be a match for a group of constables? In no time, they threw him out.

Despite discerning that the troublemaker had a bit of cultivation, the constables didn’t think much of it and returned to drinking and complaining.

On the other hand, the thief felt wronged and returned to complain to his boss.

The group of thieves was already drunk. As soon as they heard that their brother had been bullied, the alcohol rushed to the top of their heads. Their leader was even more belligerent about standing up for his brother. Slamming the table, he arrogantly announced, “Damn it, you dare to mess with me? Go tell them next door that if they’ve got the guts, they should come to us! Anyone who doesn’t is a coward of a grandson!”

Chapter 61: Such A Proactive Achievement is Rare

“Who dares bully my brother?!” The leader of the thieves bellowed resoundingly and told his underlings to call the other party over. As their boss, if I don't reclaim some face and stand up for my underlings when they're wronged, how am I going to establish my authority in the future?

Emboldened by their leader backing them up, the thief instantly stood ramrod straight. Kicking the room next door open, he arrogantly hollered, “My boss says that we can't take it lying down after you've bullied me! He wants to talk to you. Whoever doesn't go is a coward of a grandson!”

The constables were flabbergasted. Over their decade of service, they had never encountered anyone so brazen as to outrightly challenge them.

Captain Wei shook his head and chuckled. With his vast experience, he had seen it all. It’s just provocation by a bunch of foolish brats who don’t know their place. Such petty cases that send themselves to my doorsteps are bound to crop up a few times in a constable’s career.

“Who’s scared of whom? Let’s go!”

The thieves cracked their knuckles and rolled their sleeves up for battle, eager to teach the other party a lesson. As they were new to the area, they figured that they couldn’t rely solely on thieving to make a name for themselves before joining a diabolic creed. It’s time for us to make our grand entrance!

All of a sudden, the thieves saw a group of constables burst in with their sabers brandished, their identity waist tablets hanging from their waists.

The constables were astonished to see the tables full of gold, silver, rare medicinal herbs, and spirit stones. Why do these things look so familiar? It seems like someone just reported these items missing?

The constables, “...”

Captain Wei, “...”

The thieves, “...”

“Would you believe me if I say that we picked these up by the roadside?”

Even Captain Wei had never experienced a situation like this before. It was his first time encountering criminals who voluntarily delivered themselves right into his hands.

Meanwhile, the thieves were still clueless about what was happening and were still clamoring for their boss to take action.

“Boss, show them who’s boss!”

The thief in question even talked big, “See my boss’ thinning hair? Every time he kills someone, he plucks out a strand of hair! He’s known as the Scourge of Ghosts in the jianghu!

“See the one with the eyepatch? That’s my second brother. He lost that eye when he fought with an Advanced Foundation Establishment expert. That expert also didn’t fare any better; my second brother blinded him in both eyes, earning the title of Fearless Second Brother in the jianghu!

“See my third brother’s leg? During a heist in the imperial palace, he was surrounded by a hundred guards; he escaped at the cost of his leg! People call him the Grassland Soarer in the jianghu!”

The big boss, second boss, and third boss simultaneously kicked the underling. You talk too much.

Captain Wei smiled sinisterly. “Didn’t you say that whoever doesn’t come is a grandson?” It’s precisely because of you lot that I have to work consecutive night shifts.

“I’m a grandson, I’m a grandson.” The thief’s leader trembled with fear.

The thieves no longer dared to make a move. Noticing that the door was blocked by the constables, they broke through the walls and fled, the noisy group running into the main hall.

Their strength lay in speed, while their abilities in direct combat were average, not to mention that they hadn’t even reached the Foundation Establishment Stage; their big boss was only at the Level Nine Qi Training Stage.

The leader of the thieves commanded his people to scatter as they fled. “The group of you, run out from the front door; the rest of you, follow me through the back door!”

Lu Yang noticed the commotion and quickly figured out the situation, finding it rather amusing. “The thieves and constables are separated by just a wall, yet the thieves dare to provoke the constables?

“Wait, if they escape through the backyard, what if the constables discover the tiger-henchman ghosts?”

Lu Yang was swift in realizing the crux of the problem. If the tiger-henchman ghosts are annihilated, who’s going to barbecue the skewers? How are we going to continue operating the barbeque shop? How are we going to spy on Qin Yuanhao?

The big thief boss was stupefied to see Lu Yang blocking the door and reached out his hand to hurl Lu Yang away. The latter was holding a basin of Dough Drop Soup[1]. When he saw the big thief boss coming at him truculently, his hand trembled, spilling all the soup.

The thief leader didn’t expect such a turn of events. He conjured a layer of spirit energy as a barrier to block the Dough Drop Soup. With this brief delay, Captain Wei took out a snake-like iron chain and coiled it around the leader of the thieves.

“Go, catch the rest and bring them back. This meal is a worthy one.” Captain Wei felt refreshed as if the haze over him had been swept away. The troublesome band of thieves that has plagued us for days is now finally apprehended. What a blessing.

Captain Wei patted Lu Yang’s shoulders and laughed heartily. “If you hadn’t blocked the way, this brat would have really run away. You were a hero in standing up for what is right. Wait for it, I will award you with a silk banner tomorrow!”

Lu Yang hastily waved his hand and said it wasn’t necessary, but it wasn’t enough to change Constable Captain Wei’s mind. The latter was so elated that he insisted on giving Lu Yang the silk banner.

As the scuffle between the constables and thieves had caused quite a ruckus, damaging the walls and turning the main hall into a chaotic mess of smoke and dust, the diners could only leave early. However, they found it worthwhile that they had managed to witness the constables in action.

“One More Time Barbeque Shop is a really great place. The constables can catch people even while sitting.”

“It was worth coming here. You don’t get to see such a good show elsewhere even if you have the money.”

“This must be a place where good fortune accumulates. Their business is already booming in such a short span of time. Even if the food is delicious, this level of popularity is over the top; it definitely involves a certain degree of luck.”

“The fact that the constables could arrest those people today successfully proves this point.”

“It looks like I have to come by more often to have the luck rub off on me.”

“That makes sense. Let’s come together next time.”

Listening to the fading discussions, Lu Yang became pessimistic about the future of the barbeque shop.

It’s destined to become a big thing.

“When I send over the silk banner tomorrow, I’ll also bring the money for repairing the walls!” Constable Captain Wei waved at Lu Yang before taking the unlucky thieves away.

Lu Yang stood at the entrance and sighed. Suddenly, he noticed that Qin Yuanhao had left his estate once again.

“Brother Lu, Qin Yuanhao has left his estate again,” Man Gu transmitted an auditory message from the second floor. He was very conscientious with his task, not caring about everything that happened downstairs and only focusing on watching Qin Yuanhao’s actions.

“I’ve seen it. You and Jingzhou fix the damaged wall. I’ll follow Qin Yuanhao.”

“Understood.”

Lu Yang used Shrinking Earth to follow Qin Yuanhao once more.

Meng Jingzhou remarked from behind, “Lu Yang’s talent in spells is really strong. I tried learning from him for half a day but learned nothing. Besides, I keep feeling that the mantra he taught me has something to do with spatial spells. Is it just my illusion?”

Meng Jingzhou didn’t delve further into this topic. Lu Yang’s talent in spells can only be described as “outrageous.” To hope to learn spells from him is pure daydreaming. If I, a Single’s Spirit Root, can’t even do it, it’s all the more impossible for anyone else.

~~~

Lu Yang was already a distance away and didn’t hear Meng Jingzhou. The former observed that Qin Yuanhao was walking energetically and humming a cheerful tune, as if he was about to do something big.

Qin Yuanhao arrived at a large estate, but instead of knocking, he cast a spell on the door.

Soon, a tall, lanky man emerged. He immediately asked, “The day has come?”

“It’s today.”

“I have prepared for this day for half a month.”

“You make it sound like you’re the only one. This time, we must pull off a big one. There hasn’t been much movement this while, and it’s suffocating me inside! Once this is completed, you’ll have to publicize it well. Let’s see who dares to underestimate me again!” A hint of a cruel smile appeared on Qin Yuanhao’s visage.

“Certainly, certainly.” The tall, lanky man was known for being a big mouth in the Yanjiang Branch.

The two’s conversation was not one others could understand, and their laughter was somewhat cold.

Lu Yang was alert, unsure of what the two men were up to.

The two walked to a bustling district where a building was especially conspicuous due to its vibrant decorations. Qin Yuanhao and the tall, lanky man went inside and were warmly received.

Lu Yang raised his head to look at the wooden plaque.

It was a brothel.

1. Dough Drop and Assorted Vegetable Soup ☜

Chapter 62: Location of the Base

Ten minutes later, Qin Yuanhao and the tall, lanky man left the brothel with their faces devoid of the excitement they had before entering.

Lu Yang scratched his temple. They came out so quickly?

At the entrance, the madam handed Qin Yuanhao and the man each a slip of paper. They opened them, and briefly glanced through the contents before promptly destroying them.

“Brother Qin, the branch leader has something for me to do and wants me to go over, so I’ll make a move first.”

“Mmm, the branch leader also tasked me with something. Let’s part ways here then. Don’t forget to help spread the word about me visiting the brothel.”

“No problem.”

After the two of them parted ways in front of the brothel, Lu Yang suddenly had the idea to follow the tall, lanky man. As the latter’s cultivation was on par with Qin Yuanhao, he didn’t notice Lu Yang lurking underground.

As they walked further, the number of people and houses gradually dwindled. Eventually, they appeared to have arrived in the wilderness with not a single soul in sight. The man seemed to be familiar with the place, walking on the winding mountain path with ease. After about a quarter of an hour, he stopped before a stone wall.

This area was the border between Yanjiang Commandery and another commandery. Technically, it was considered to be a part of Yanjiang Commandery, but due to historical reasons, both parties had grounds to claim jurisdiction.

It was precisely because of this that both parties chose not to take responsibility. After all, there was nothing of value here, so there was no need to fight over it.

The man knocked the wall with three long knocks followed by a short one and chanted something. The wall then became water-like.

Stepping into the wall, the man vanished.

Lu Yang had heard him chant “Everlasting Immortal, rise from the dead, dispel clouds for sunlight, eternal in the world.”

“This is a cave domain?” Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed as astonishment flickered in them.

Cave domains were a separate space created by cultivators proficient in spatial spells. The higher their cultivation, the more complete the space they could create. Generally, a Divine Transfiguration cultivator could already create their own space. Some cultivators liked to use these cave domains to be in solitude, while some cultivators liked to use them as tombs and also be in solitude.

Throughout history, there had been countless Divine Transfiguration cultivators, not to mention the three main stages: Void Refinement, Fusion, and Transcendent Tribulation. Even after a cultivator passed away, their cave domain would be left behind, resulting in the numerous ancient cave ruins across the Central Continent. However, most cultivators didn’t reveal the location or method of entering their cave domains before they died, so people could only rely on their luck to find these relics.

No one knew how many cave domains remained undiscovered.

Big Senior Sister said that as the Great Era approaches, more and more cave domains are being discovered, and many people will obtain fortuitous opportunities to soar to great heights. This cave domain is likely one left behind by a forebear. The diabolic creed discovered it and took it for their own use.

Lu Yang didn’t rashly follow the man. He chose to quietly stay hidden in the ground, waiting for the man to come back out. However, Lu Yang still felt unsafe. This was, after all, the Yanjiang Branch, a diabolic creed’s base. He didn’t know how many experts were inside. Just hiding underground doesn’t feel enough to conceal me.

With this in mind, Lu Yang moved to a spot further away but where he could still see the entrance of the base. He used To Inches to shrink himself and concealed himself with the Barbarian Tribe’s concealment technique Man Gu had provided.

About two hours later, a man wearing a mask walked out from the stone wall with the tall, lanky man following behind. From the looks of it, the masked man was of a higher position.

“Hmm?” The masked man sensed something amiss and released his spiritual consciousness to scan the surroundings, which included beneath the ground.

“Come out, I’ve found you. Don’t think that you’ve hidden yourself very well. If you come out, I can spare your life!” the masked man said coolly.

“Are you still not coming out? Don’t think that I, the branch leader, am benevolent and soft-hearted. I’ll count to three. If you still don’t come out, don’t blame me for not giving you a chance!

“Three!

“Two!

“One!

“Die!”

The branch leader condensed a force in his palm and struck in one direction, producing a thunderous rumbling sound.

“Branch leader, what’s the matter?” the tall, lanky man asked respectfully.

The branch leader shook his head. “I just have a feeling that someone was watching me, so I tried to trick them and lure them out. Maybe it was just my imagination.”

Beads of cold sweat broke out on Lu Yang’s forehead. He had briefly considered bursting out of the ground and exchanging blows with the branch leader, thinking that it might be his only chance for survival. Fortunately, his mental willpower was strong, allowing him to suppress the impulse.

He believed that the Barbarian Tribe Concealment Technique wouldn’t expose himself. Lu Yang sensed that the branch leader’s spiritual consciousness had scanned past him, but the branch leader probably mistook him as a stone and didn’t pay any attention to him. Had the branch leader truly discovered him, he wouldn’t have bothered with a countdown—attacking him directly would be the more logical course of action.

Luckily, the Barbarian Tribe Concealment Technique is brilliant. As long as I don’t move, I won’t be detected. This branch leader is likely at the Golden Core Stage.

“How’s the preparation coming along for the selection trials? It’s in ten days.”

“Everything is ready. We’re just waiting for comrades of the same path to arrive in ten days, pass the selection trials, and join us.”

“That’s great then. I hope we can recruit more diabolic talents this time. That way, the headquarters will value the Yanjiang Branch more.”

The two discussed as they walked, soon disappearing from Lu Yang’s line of sight. Lu Yang stayed still, fearing that he might expose himself.

“Golden Core cultivators are truly something else.”

Lu Yang waited for an hour more, worried that the branch leader might be overly suspicious and suddenly turn back.

One hour passed, and the branch leader didn’t show up.

Time to go. Lu Yang burrowed through the ground as he left.

He had obtained considerable intel this time around. Not only did he learn of the location of the Yanjiang Branch, he even ascertained that it was where the selection trials would be held.

~~~

“Tell me, Scourge of Ghosts, what’s up with your hair? I heard that you pluck a strand every time you kill someone?” Captain Wei interrogated while sitting with one leg over the other. The thieves were lined up, trembling in their seats across from him.

“No...no such thing. It’s hard being the big boss, the team is difficult to manage, and my subordinates cause trouble everywhere, so the sheer stress made my hair fall out.”

“What about you, Fearless Second Brother? I heard that you fought with a Foundation Establishment cultivator. You blinded both of his eyes while he blinded one of yours?”

“My...my eyes are fine. Wearing an eyepatch just makes me look more imposing. When mingling in the jianghu, you need to have something to boast about.”

“And you, Grassland Soarer, I heard that you stole from the imperial palace. At best, you’ll be imprisoned for life; if it’s severe, you’ll be sentenced to lingchi—death by a thousand cuts.”

The third thief cried out in grievance, “It’s a misunderstanding, Your Excellency. I simply didn’t repay the money I owed. My creditor broke a leg of mine before waiving the debt.”

Captain Wei yawned. I thought every one of them bears major crimes, but it turns out to be just like this?

“Brother constable, I confess, I’ll confess everything. I’ve stolen from sixteen houses...”

Captain Wei waved his hand. “No rush on that. First, tell me why the group of you recklessly came to Yanjiang Commandery.”

“Well...” The leader of the thieves was a bit hesitant, weighing the pros and cons of speaking or staying silent.

Captain Wei pointed at the torture chamber behind him. “See those torture equipment behind you? If you don’t talk, I’ll use these tools to help you speak.”

The torture instruments were still stained with remnants of darkened blood, looking particularly creepy. The thieves swallowed their saliva and scrambled to be the first to confess.

“I’ll talk...” The thieves barely uttered two words before suddenly falling silent.

If someone were to go behind them, they would realize that their necks were embedded with needles as thin as cow hair. These needles were laced with deadly poison!

“Assassins!”

Captain Wei was indeed a seasoned constable. He reacted instantly, dashing outside to search for the assassin.

But there was no one outside.

Inside the interrogation room, the shadow seemed to move with a life of its own, letting out a faint chuckle before vanishing.

Chapter 63: Be Careful, the Opponent is Very Freakish

“Captain Wei, you’re here so early. There are no barbeque skewers at this hour,” Lu Yang joked at the entrance.

It was still morning when Captain Wei brought two constables and a silk banner to the barbeque shop.

“Here you go, this is the banner I promised you yesterday.” Captain Wei shook out the silk banner on the street in an attempt to display it. Written on it was “Hero of Courage, Upholder of Justice.”

This action of his indeed drew quite a crowd. The two constables hung the banner on the wall directly facing the main hall, making it extra conspicuous.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts were originally skewering in the hall, but Lu Yang had them move to the backyard in advance to avoid being seen.

Lu Yang brought over three cups of tea and casually asked, “Did those stupid thieves from yesterday reveal anything? Where did these outsiders come from? They even dared to provoke the renowned Iron-Faced Captain?”

“Hai, don’t mention it. We didn’t get anything out of them,” Captain Wei sighed, gulping down the hot tea.

A Foundation Establishment cultivator’s throat was immune to being scalded by boiling water.

“Why is that?”

“Those bunch of stupid thieves are weak in willpower. They wanted to spill the beans after a bit of intimidation, but just as they were about to explain why a group of cultivators had come to Yanjiang Commandery, they were silenced by an unknown assassin. With nine cow hair poisonous needles in their necks, they died instantly. Since the room was sealed, we have no idea how the assassin got in.

“At the time, I instinctively went outside to look for the assassin but to no avail. Later, I realized that the assassin must have used a spell related to shadows, which allowed him to hide in the shadows beforehand. As soon as we started interrogating the thieves, he killed them and escaped through the shadows while I was out searching for him.

“If only I had blocked the door, the assassin wouldn’t have escaped. I can only blame myself for being so overwhelmed with rage that I failed to think of that possibility!” Captain Wei furiously downed the tea meant for the other two constables.

Those two constables stared at Captain Wei in a stupor. We didn’t even get to drink yet.

With a smile, Lu Yang sent off the incensed Captain Wei and the unlucky constables who hadn’t even had a sip of water.

Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message, “Do we kill Qin Yuanhao according to the plan from yesterday?”

After Lu Yang returned last night, he recounted what he had witnessed. Now that they knew the location of the Yanjiang Branch, there was no longer a need to keep Qin Yuanhao alive.

The three of them then spent the night devising a plan to ambush Qin Yuanhao. To be more specific, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were the ones discussing while Man Gu listened by the side.

“No rush. I have a new idea. Let’s prepare a bit more.”

~~~

A figure in black robes lightly knocked on the door to Qin Yuanhao’s estate, but no one answered even after a long time.

The black-robed figure continued waiting.

Finally, the door opened, but there was no one there, as if the door had opened by itself. The door stood open like the gaping maw of a monster, ready to devour the unsuspecting.

The black-robed figure entered the estate calmly. As soon as he stepped inside, the door slammed shut, and a bolt slid into place, essentially trapping him inside.

The black-robed figure took out a bone tablet and announced in a resounding voice, “Is Senior Qin Yuanhao here? I specially came to pay a visit under the order of my master.”

“I was wondering who it was. It turns out that you’re one of Brother Tiger’s tiger-henchman ghosts.” Qin Yuanhao suddenly appeared from behind the tiger-henchman ghost. The latter couldn’t even discern from which direction Qin Yuanhao had come from, as if he had materialized out of thin air.

“Why are you looking for me?”

“My master said that after having ruminated about it for a while, it thinks that you have a point. It’s easier to seek shade when you’re leaning against a large tree. It wishes to join the Yanjiang Branch, but it also has some concerns, so it would like to invite you to Pine Mountain for a discussion.”

Qin Yuanhao looked at the tiger-henchman ghost with interest. “Oh? Brother Tiger hasn’t replied to my letter, so I thought it didn’t have the intention of joining.”

The tiger-henchman ghost smiled meekly. “My master takes a longer time to contemplate.”

Qin Yuanhao’s expression suddenly changed, and he grabbed the tiger-henchman ghost by the neck. “How dare you play tricks in front of me? Tell me, who sent you here? Based on Brother Tiger’s personality, how could he actively want to join the Yanjiang Branch?”

Color drained from the tiger-henchman ghost’s face, and it repeatedly said that no one had sent him.

Qin Yuanhao tightened his grip on the tiger-henchman ghost. Only until it became more faint did it tell the truth.

“A few days ago, several unwitting cultivators entered Pine Mountain and accidentally discovered my master’s whereabouts. My master killed them, and when it was sorting their belongings, it realized that they came from a prestigious sect which had seniors at the Golden Core Stage.

“Worried that the Golden Core cultivators might come knocking on its door, it suddenly recalled your invitation. After convincing the matron, it made up its mind to join the Yanjiang Commandery, so it sent me to invite you over to discuss the details.”

Hearing the answer he was hoping for, Qin Yuanhao tossed the tiger-henchman ghost aside. “That’s more like it.”

No longer suspecting the tiger-henchman ghost, Qin Yuanhao followed him to Pine Mountain.

“Senior Qin, my master is waiting just ahead,” the tiger-henchman ghost said respectfully. “Master doesn’t like people listening in, so please go ahead.”

Qin Yuanhao didn’t bother with the tiger-henchman ghost and walked ahead by himself.

The forest was dense and tranquil, seemingly devoid of human presence for a long time. The bird calls in the distance added a touch of serenity to this dense woodland.

In front of him sat a four-meter-long tiger demon. There were two cups of tea set on a stone table, giving off a hospitable air. Qin Yuanhao subconsciously relaxed his guard and quickened his pace.

Suddenly, his cultivation technique activated automatically. It formed a thin layer of protective film around him that blocked an unknown attack, leaving only a shallow cut on his neck.

“There’s an ambush!” With his wealth of experience, Qin Yuanhao nimbly jumped back. He saw a nearly invisible fine line stretched in the air at the same height as his neck.

“This noodle is quite useful; it nearly cut his head off,” a voice of schadenfreude came from a tree to Qin Yuanhao’s right. It was Meng Jingzhou.

What Qin Yuanhao saw was not a fine line but Dragon Beard noodles[1] Lu Yang had bought from the dining hall. According to the senior male disciple selling the noodles, this type of noodle could kill without a trace and was best for ambushes. Had it not been for Qin Yuanhao’s special cultivation technique which had an automatic defense function, his head would have already been severed.

“How dare you scheme against me!” Qin Yuanhao glowered at the tiger demon. He didn’t invite me to discuss joining the Yanjiang Branch. It was a trap right from the start!

Unexpectedly, the tiger demon had vanished. The ground beneath Qin Yuanhao’s feet became soft, and the Qingfeng Sword struck him right at his crotch.

Fortunately, Qin Yuanhao was swift to react. His right knee clashed with the Qingfeng Sword and deflected it, successfully protecting his family jewels.

Sensing that the situation was not in his favor, he turned and fled. I’m totally unprepared while the other party is totally prepared. How am I supposed to fight back?

“It must be fellow diabolic cultivators!” Qin Yuanhao was sure about his conjecture. That sword’s attack was too wicked; how could any righteous cultivator fight like that?

Man Gu had been waiting behind him for a long time. He swung a tree at Qin Yuanhao, sending him flying far away.

“Hmm, why does it feel like nothing?” Man Gu was perplexed. I had clearly hit the target, but it felt like hitting a piece of paper.

Despite being thrown a distance away, he was unscathed, and his fighting spirit undiminished.

“Watch out for his cultivation technique; it’s very freakish!” Man Gu reminded loudly.

“You're just a few juniors and you think you can deal with me? You’re a hundred years too early!” Qin Yuanhao laughed out loud. As long as they can’t figure out the true purpose of my cultivation technique, no one can catch me.

Lu Yang leaped into the air with composure, aiming his identity jade pendant at Qin Yuanhao. “Capture!”

Qin Yuanhao was momentarily stunned, yet to register what was happening. This jade pendant looks like an alternative storage ring, but a storage ring can’t capture me.

He then noticed that the trio were giving him strange looks. Slowly looking down, he realized that he was naked, not knowing when his clothes had mysteriously disappeared.

Qin Yuanhao’s clothes had been absorbed into the jade pendant, leaving him shivering out in the open in just his underwear.

“F*ck, you guys are the freakish ones!”

1. An example of a dish with Dragon Beard Noodles. ☜

Chapter 64: Shadow

Out of conscience, Lu Yang didn’t take away all of Qin Yuanhao’s clothes, leaving him a piece of underwear to preserve his modesty.

~~~

The storage ring was a widely known magical treasure among cultivators.

The Luodi Merchant Guild had conducted several surveys on the “Most Popular Magical Treasures,” and the storage ring consistently topped the charts with the highest number of votes. Regardless of whether one was out traveling, touring the continent, hiding treasures and their secret money stash, it was an essential household magical treasure.

Moreover, storage rings were very cheap; even Qi Training cultivators could afford it, though their space would be much smaller. Every year, many Qi Training cultivators would purchase storage rings, and the Luodi Merchant Guild would reap tremendous profits, making it a major source of revenue. The Luodi Merchant Guild even released upgraded versions of the storage rings annually, though the improvements mainly focused on enhancing the external aesthetics while the internal space remained unchanged.

For most cultivators, the first magical treasure in their possession would be the storage rings, so it held immense sentimental value. Both righteous and diabolic cultivators would use storage rings, and Qin Yuanhao was naturally no exception.

The aforementioned was Qin Yuanhao’s impression of storage rings.

In his several decades of life, he had never heard of anyone using a storage ring to capture away their enemy’s clothes!

Does this even make sense?!

It actually made perfect sense. Storage rings couldn’t store items possessing spiritual nature, such as living beings, ghosts, and spirit treasures. Clearly, Qin Yuanhao’s clothes didn’t belong to these categories.

Fortunately, as a proud cultivator of the diabolic path, Qin Yuanhao’s sense of shame had long vanished with the wind. Even if he was just wearing his underwear, that didn’t stop him from fighting!

Then he saw Meng Jingzhou take out a recording orb.

“What the hell?! Which creed are you from? What deep enmity do you have toward me?!” Qin Yuanhao was of the firm opinion that Lu Yang and friends were members from the other three diabolic creeds.

Even if they claimed to be from the righteous path now, there was no convincing Qin Yuanhao otherwise.

He just couldn’t understand why. Despite having made enemies, he had always been cautious to not go overboard in making sworn enemies.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were also giving strange looks to Lu Yang, as if they hadn’t expected Lu Yang to come up with such a unique attack method.

“There’s no need to talk about the code of the jianghu when dealing with diabolic crooks! All together!” Lu Yang beckoned the other two.

With all three of them attacking together, even the Half-Step Golden Core Stage tiger demon perished, let alone Qin Yuanhao, who was just at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

They had even considered taking on Qin Yuanhao one-on-one. This was the confidence of geniuses in fighting someone above their level. However, for the sake of not taking any risks, they decided that it would be better for all three to act together.

Casting aside his embarrassment, Qin Yuanhao became embroiled in a battle with the three. The sword was brimming with a heroic aura, flowing like water and unfettered like ink. Qin Yuanhao was repeatedly forced to retreat, not daring to face them head-on!

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu unleashed their fists together like falling mountains, pounding Qin Yuanhao’s chest until he coughed up blood incessantly!

Qin Yuanhao flipped his palm, revealing three cowhair poisonous needles at his fingertips. He pierced all three of their chests.

To his surprise, the trio seemed to be completely unaffected. Their sword and fists showed no signs of weakening, and instead, they fought even more valiantly. Lu Yang had already anticipated that the enemy might use poison, so they had taken Detoxification Pills in advance.

Strictly speaking, it would be more apt to call the Detoxification Pill a Poison Removal Pill. The principle of Detoxification Pills was to encapsulate the poison before it acted up and expel it from the body through sweat. However, if the poison never took effect in the first place, how could it be called “detoxification?”

Qin Yuanhao cursed under his breath. His opponents were too sufficiently prepared. He was unable to unleash his vicious methods. Even if he could unleash them, those methods were no match for his opponents in terms of viciousness.

Meng Jingzhou’s muscles bulged and his veins throbbed. From Qin Yuanhao’s perspective, the fists had grown in size so fast that he could barely react.

Something strange happened once again. Against Meng Jingzhou’s heavy and forceful fist power, an Advanced Foundation Establishment cultivator would be dead or crippled if they were lucky, yet Qin Yuanhao was unaffected.

Qin Yuanhao laughed sinisterly. Like I’ve said, they’re no match for me!

After exchanging blows, Lu Yang finally uncovered the truth behind Qin Yuanhao’s cultivation technique. He swung his sword, and reflected light rays danced about, his sword qi like a rainbow and unstoppable.

This sword struck right at Qin Yuanhao’s shadow!

“Damn it!” Qin Yuanhao howled in pain.

“Just as I thought, you were the one who killed the band of thieves last night. Your weakness is your shadow!”

Lu Yang recalled seeing Qin Yuanhao walking out from the brothel and receiving orders from the branch leader. He was most likely sent to kill those thieves.

With his biggest source of support exposed, Qin Yuanhao no longer wished to fight. His body disappeared from sight, and his shadow moved rapidly across the ground. Even if I can’t defeat them, I am fully confident in my ability to escape. No matter how sharp your sword is, can you possibly kill a shadow?

“I’ve remembered you three juniors! Prepare to suffer from my endless revenge, hahaha...” Feeling victorious, Qin Yuanhao couldn’t control his laughter.

Suddenly, a beam of light shone on the shadow. Instantly, Qin Yuanhao let out a heart-wrenching shriek, as if a piece of flesh had been forcefully torn from his body.

The Light-Gathering Array was a simple array that absorbed and emitted light. It was easy to pick up, but it was considered to be of little value. However, in this particular situation, its effects proved to be remarkable.

With no other choice, Qin Yuanhao’s body emerged from the shadow to block the white light, and the gap in the shadow also disappeared.

His injuries had healed.

“It looks like you came prepared, but so what? Were you so naive as to think that you could hurt me with a mere Light-Gathering Array?” Qin Yuanhao scoffed. “Don’t you know that the stronger the light, the stronger the shadow?”

Lu Yang was unflustered. He hurled out more Light-Gathering Arrays and similarly mocked, “Have you heard of a shadowless lamp?”

Qin Yuanhao hesitated for a moment. He didn’t know what a shadowless lamp was, but hearing it from Lu Yang, an ominous feeling rose from the bottom of his gut.

Lu Yang had no time to explain theories to his opponent in the heat of battle. Dozens of white light rays hit Qin Yuanhao, causing his shadow to sizzle. Regardless of how Qin Yuanhao revealed his body to block the rays or shrink back into his shadow, his efforts were futile in stopping this process.

The shadow grew increasingly faint until it was indistinguishable to the naked eye.

The principle of a shadowless lamp was not to make the shadow disappear but to make it so faint that it was almost imperceptible.

Qin Yuanhao roared as he darted out from the nearly invisible shadow; his physical body could no longer hide within the shadow.

Rays of sword light descended from the sky like a rainbow from beyond the horizon. It was so sudden that it caught Qin Yuanhao off guard, piercing straight through his body.

This was the moment Lu Yang had been waiting for.

“What a close shave, we almost let him escape.” Meng Jingzhou was relieved to see Qin Yuanhao dead. If he had gotten away, their preparations over the past few days would have been in vain. He thought that they were already well-prepared, believing that Qin Yuanhao had no chance of escape even if he grew wings.

Who would have thought that his cultivation technique is related to shadows and that he would be so hard to trap? Meng Jingzhou grinned as he bumped Lu Yang’s shoulder. “Good thing you proposed making the Light-Gathering Arrays before we set off.”

“It was just luck. I suspected that his cultivation technique was related to shadows, but I had no concrete evidence. Anyway, let’s not be happy too early. It’s not too late to celebrate after destroying the corpse and cleaning up the evidence.”

At Lu Yang’s suggestion, the trio burned Qin Yuanhao’s corpse beyond recognition and tossed it into the tiger demon’s lair before destroying the entrance with an explosion. That way, no one would find the place unless they deliberately searched the mountain.

Chapter 65: Examiners

Lu Yang held Qin Yuanhao’s storage ring. After several failed attempts, he shook his head regrettably. “Such a pity. This storage ring can only be opened by Qin Yuanhao himself. There’s no use even if we get our hands on it. Forcefully opening it would only disperse the internal space, making it an impossible challenge to retrieve anything. Let’s go check out his house. Maybe we can find something.” Lu Yang beckoned to the other two to leave.

The tiger-henchman ghost that had tricked Qin Yuanhao followed them from behind. Man Gu thought that it had done a good job and decided to reward it with two lamb skewers. Based on theory, if the lamb skewer is charred until it becomes like an offering, the tiger-henchman ghost will be able to eat it. As for whether the tiger-henchman ghost tastes the proper or charred version, it will have to be tested in practice.

When they arrived at Qin Yuanhao’s estate, they saw that it looked empty with hardly any decorations. One would probably find the place to be lifeless if they lived here alone.

The trio went to the training room. Aside from a jade statue, there were only two bookshelves packed with various secret manuals on cultivation techniques. The jade statue’s face was blurry, and it wore a long robe, making its gender indiscernible.

“This should be the Everlasting Creed’s object of worship, the Everlasting Immortal.” Meng Jingzhou circled the statue twice. The statue’s material was far superior to normal statues, but its craftsmanship left much to be desired. Who wouldn’t want their statues to be lifelike?

“Water-Repelling Mantra, Introduction to Arrays, Countering Sword Moves...they’re all rather common cultivation techniques. You can even find these on the first floor of our scripture library.” Lu Yang’s fingers brushed across the books’ spines, enjoying the feeling of their uneven surfaces.

“Common Methods to Please Your Superior, Human Nature, Schemes and Intrigue...what’s with all this nonsense?” Lu Yang randomly picked a book which happened to be Common Methods to Please Your Superior. Even its corners were worn; it was evident how often Qin Yuanhao had read it.

“Method one: become your superior’s family. Depending on your age and ability, you can set your sights on your superior or their children.”

[Qin Yuanhao’s note:

The branch leader never takes off their mask. Identity unknown. Gender unknown. Unable to approach. Marriage is impossible.]

*

“Method two: offer treasures. Flashy gifts will make the giver seem too ostentatious and unlikable. It is recommended to offer your superior low-key yet expensive gifts.”

[Qin Yuanhao’s note:

Took out a loan to buy a jade chair for the branch leader. Hope it works.]

*

“Method three; develop shared interests. Pay attention to your superior’s hobbies and cultivate the same ones.”

[Qin Yuanhao’s note:

The branch leader’s hobby is fishing. I accompanied them to fish by the river. I caught more fish than they did. Hope they don’t get jealous of my talent.]

“Method four...

“Method five...”

Qin Yuanhao had put in a lot of effort into pleasing the branch leader, but the results were lackluster.

“Looks like life in the diabolic creed is also not easy,” Lu Yang remarked with an amused smile.

However, thanks to Qin Yuanhao’s notes, Lu Yang managed to gain a basic understanding of the branch leader and various administrators. “From bottom to top in the Yanjiang Branch, it goes from ordinary members, Administrators, then the Branch Leader. There are many ordinary members, ranging from the Qi Training to the Foundation Establishment stages, but it’s hard for them to access the Everlasting Creed’s secrets.

“Only by passing the exam can a Foundation Establishment cultivator become an administrator. There are altogether twelve administrators in the Yanjiang Branch. Now that Qin Yuanhao is dead, there are eleven left.

“The branch leader’s identity is a mystery. Their exact cultivation is unknown, but they are at the Golden Core Stage, and they like fishing.”

Apart from that, the trio also found some scattered spirit stones and a few spell books that clearly didn’t look like they were meant for those from the righteous path. For example, there were hypnotism techniques and bedroom techniques. Nothing much worth mentioning.

“Let’s go. We should prepare for the diabolic creed’s selection trials nine days from now.”

~~~

At the border of Yanjiang Commandery, countless silent cultivators traversed through the dense forest. Specks of light dappled their emotionless faces, giving them an eerie vibe. Every cultivator kept their distance from one another, vigilant and ready to strike. The moment they spotted someone relaxing their guard, they would ambush them, striving to reduce their competition as much as they could.

They were all from the diabolic path. Having heard of the examination’s location through different means, they were hurrying to join the Yanjiang Branch.

Under the pressure from the righteous path, their space for survival had been shrinking. If they wanted to attain more resources, they would need to rely on a large organization, and the Yanjiang Branch had become their prime goal.

In the past, one could only join a diabolic creed through the recommendation of an administrator. To achieve that, bribing the administrators was a must. However, it was different this time around—everyone had a chance. It was the best opportunity in thirty years to join a diabolic creed.

Two hours before the trial began, most of the rogue diabolic cultivators had already arrived.

“Look! Isn’t that Chi Xulong, the one who slaughtered an entire family overnight and left not even a rat alive, then nimbly left right under everyone’s noses?”

A burly man was holding the leg bone of an unknown demon beast, looking like a savage. His skin was bronze in color, and his muscles were bulging. His arms were littered with scars, and when he grinned, his teeth looked like protruding wolf fangs.

Chi Xulong was extremely well-known among rogue diabolic cultivators. Known to be arrogant and unbridled, he had survived countless deadly tribulations and even leveled up during battle. It could be said that the more he fought, the more valiant he became—truly an invincible force!

“Chi Xulong, I didn’t expect to see you here,” A pale-faced scholar teased as he fanned himself with a paper fan.

Chi Xulong snorted. “Heh, if it isn’t Shen Jinyi. As a teacher, why aren’t you teaching in school? What did you come here for? No one here needs you to teach them!”

“What? He’s Shen Jinyi, the one who specializes in running schools to teach people how to kill?” Someone gasped and moved away upon hearing how Chi Xulong addressed the pale-faced scholar.

Shen Jinyi was indeed a teacher, but he didn’t teach Confucian classics but rather the most effective and covert methods to kill. It was unknown how many killers he had trained, and he was also a fearsome figure among rogue diabolic cultivators. One shouldn’t be fooled by Shen Jinyi’s smile and frail appearance. If you offended him, you wouldn’t even know how you died!

“Killers? They’re just a bunch of cowards who don’t dare show their faces,” sneered a bladesman who was carrying a wide saber as tall as a person. He didn’t think much of assassins like Shen Jinyi.

Shen Jinyi was just about to retort, but upon seeing the swordsman’s face, he forcefully swallowed his words back, only managing to squeeze a few words through clenched teeth, “One Zhang Red!”

“Why are you calling for your grandfather?” Unfazed by Shen Jinyi’s murderous glare, One Zhang Red even spat in contempt.

Some rogue diabolic cultivators widened their eyes; the people filtering in were all big names. “No way, that’s One Zhang Red? Known for drawing blood within one zhang? Rumors say that he’s unrivaled in close combat and even Half-Step Golden Core experts are unwilling to face him!”

Besides these three people, many other notorious criminals had also arrived. They were on the authorities’ wanted list with huge bounties on their heads, but no one dared to provoke them for fear of being killed instead.

With this group of infamous evil people congregating together, the rest acknowledged their lacking cultivation and stood far away, not even daring to speak loudly.

Suddenly, the arrival of three individuals caught everyone’s attention. The one walking in the middle carried a sword on his back. To his left was seemingly a Confucian cultivator holding Words of Sages, while the person on the left wore a dazzling smile and resembled a madman. The three people walked in silence with a non-negligible aura, their gazes fixed ahead and completely ignoring the rogue diabolic cultivators.

“Who are they? Do you know them?”

“I don’t know them, but they seem like important figures.”

The three passed through the crowd until they reached all the way in front. Chanting something about the “Everlasting Immortal,” they opened the stone wall and pretended to take out tables and benches from the other side when they had in fact retrieved them from their jade pendants.

Chi Xulong and the others thought to themselves, They’re probably from the diabolic creed if they are able to open the stone wall.

After sitting down, the person carrying a sword coughed twice, drawing everyone’s attention. They heard him announce in a loud voice, “I’m Lu Yang, and these two are Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu. The three of us are the examiners for this selection trials. The Everlasting Creed’s selection trials shall now commence. Line up and report your personal information.”

Chapter 66: It Is Not Advisable for the Slow-Witted Ones To Join the Diabolic Creeds

After the “examiners” had given their orders, regardless of whether one was Chi Xulong or another “Long,” they had to stand obediently in line.

If one angered the examiners, could they even think of joining the diabolic creed? No matter how well they had thrived outside, could they compare to the power of the diabolic creeds?

The diabolic creeds have an unfathomable creed leader, numerous powerful members, but what about us? We only have ourselves, and the highest cultivation among us is only at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

None of the candidates recognized the three examiners, but that was understandable. After all, diabolic creeds were an existence far more mysterious than rogue diabolic cultivators; they rarely showed themselves, so it wasn’t surprising that no one had seen them before. Although the selection had begun two hours earlier than announced, nobody raised any questions.

This is probably part of the test—arriving early demonstrates our dedication to the diabolic creed, while those who come right on time are deemed unworthy of joining.

Lu Yang was sitting with one leg crossed over the other. He took out a brush and paper, pointing at the first person. “Tell me, why do you want to join the diabolic creed? What value can you bring to us? What are your personal goals and plans? What are your expectations regarding the stipend?”

“Huh?” The first person was dumbfounded by the sudden barrage of questions. Are these the exam questions for entering the diabolic creed? Shouldn’t they be asking about things like my cultivation, cultivation techniques, and what kind of evil deeds I have done?

Not receiving any response from the man, Lu Yang waved his hand impatiently. “What’s with the ‘huh?’ If you’re tongue-tied when faced with just our questions, are you going to spill everything about the diabolic creed if the authorities catch you in the future?

“You’re disqualified. Go back.”

The second candidate was the leader of a small gang. For the multiple times he had been imprisoned, his gang and wife would be taken by his underlings multiple times, and he would have to reclaim them multiple times. This made him a fairly experienced gang leader.

"I’m Niu Mang, leader of the Qinglong Gang. I want to join the diabolic creed because of the better prospects that are available. My ideals and philosophy for the diabolic path align closely with that of your diabolic creed, and I believe I will be a great fit within the creed. If I am given the opportunity to join your diabolic creed, I will definitely commit myself to doing evil diligently and helping the creed grow stronger. I see a future where we can achieve new heights together!

“My personal plan is simple: I’ll do whatever the diabolic creed needs me to do with no complaints at all. After all, only when the diabolic creed is strong can I be strong!

“The diabolic creed will already be giving me a place to establish myself, so how could I still ask for a stipend? I should be offering tribute to the creed instead!” When Niu Mang reached the climax, he even waved his fists to express that he was determined to surmount obstacles and embrace a brighter future.

He sounded very well-prepared; after all, this was how he taught the Qinglong Gang.

“You’re disqualified. Go back.”

“Why?” Niu Mang was indignant; he thought that his answer was near perfect.

Lu Yang rebuked him harshly, feeling that Niu Mang had let down those from the diabolic path. “What is the diabolic path? It is about selfishness, yet you are so eager to serve the diabolic creed without expecting anything in return. How could someone like you be a diabolic cultivator? As a member of the diabolic creed, you must always be plotting to raise a rebellion and overthrow the leaders! Can a diabolic creed really be called one if there is no internal strife?

“Besides, didn’t you say that you’d do whatever the diabolic creed needs you to do? Well, the diabolic creed needs to disqualify you now. Get lost!”

Niu Mang left dejectedly while those behind him felt as if they had broadened their horizons. So this is the philosophy of the diabolic creed. As expected of the examiners; they have a profound understanding of the diabolic path.

“Next,” Meng Jingzhou called.

“I’m Chi Xulong. My cultivation is at the Foundation Establishment Stage.” Chi Xulong emphasized his cultivation, hoping that the examiners would take him seriously.

“Tell us, what evil deeds have you done?”

Chi Xulong had plenty to say on this topic. “I was taken by wolves as a child and raised by them. When I was ten, I killed those wolves with a bone knife and went down the mountain where I would rob whatever I wanted. I kept this habit even when I got to the city. Whenever I lacked something, I would steal it. The constables would chase me, but I was too fast for anyone to catch, and I would continue to steal while fleeing. As I stole, I would even take hostages and kill anyone who got in my way.” Chi Xulong was proud of his own acts. With all the evil things I’ve done, how could I not qualify for the diabolic creed?

Meng Jingzhou shook his head. “The righteous path has the upper hand now, so we, the diabolic path, have to keep a low profile. Your actions are too ostentatious and will come back to bite you sooner or later. Look at yourself, how many people know who you are? Now, look at the three of us, does anyone recognize us? See, that’s the difference!

“This isn’t cowardice. It’s premeditated concealment. It’s the wisdom of hiding in plain sight!”

Man Gu glanced at Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou curiously. Why do I feel like Brother Lu and Brother Meng are so familiar with the diabolic path?

Chi Xulong was greatly inspired. He realized that he had underestimated the complexities of the diabolic path and left willingly.

“My name is Shen Jinyi.” The pale-faced scholar introduced himself smilingly. After hearing the questions and answers before him, he felt that he had figured out the examiners’ approach.

Man Gu sized up the man’s scholarly appearance. He’s likely a Confucian cultivator too! There was a question that had perplexed him for a long time, and even Fourth Elder couldn’t answer. He asked in excitement, “Since ‘lady’ and ‘granny’ both sound similar and refer to a female, can I call a ‘lady’ ‘granny?’”[1]

The question completely caught Shen Jinyi by surprise. Despite his forty years of life experience, he was still in a stupor. Man Gu hadn’t spoken, and Shen Jinyi had been thinking that this examiner on the left looked simple-minded and ordinary. He hadn’t expected such a curveball right off the bat from Man Gu.

However, Shen Jinyi didn’t directly admit that he didn’t know the answer. “I am a killer, not a Confucian cultivator.”

“Killer? Have you studied criminal law?” Lu Yang asked with interest.

“I have studied it a little,” Shen Jinyi replied humbly. In reality, he had studied criminal law extensively, especially because a killer needed to figure out how to evade the law.

“Then let me ask you something. Criminal law defines murder as ‘intentionally depriving one of life constitutes this offense.’

“So, does suicide constitute intentional murder?”

Shen Jinyi received a second curveball.

Seeing that Shen Jinyi couldn’t come up with a response, Lu Yang waved his hand in disappointment. “You couldn’t even answer the questions in your own area of expertise. Go back.”

In just five minutes, Shen Jinyi had suffered the greatest setback in his life. Are these questions normal people can think of? Could it be that only talents whose brains are wired differently from ordinary people can join the diabolic creed?

~~~

As the selection trial was a consequential matter, the branch leader could only rest assured if they personally oversaw it. For that, they had specially planned to arrive an hour earlier to make preparations.

On the way to the venue, the branch leader saw many fierce-looking individuals leave one by one, muttering things like “The interview was really tough,” “It’s not easy to join the diabolic creed,” “So this is the true essence of the diabolic path,” “I’ll come and try again in thirty years,” as if they had attained nirvana.

The branch leader fell into deep thought. I haven’t even arrived, so who on earth is hosting the selection trial?

Then he saw Lu Yang’s trio passing judgment with all-powerful authority.

1. In the original text, “niang” (ancient way of addressing one’s mother intimately) mean the same thing as “ma,” (a more modern way of addressing one’s mother), the question asks whether a “guniang” (young lady) can be called a “guma” (aunt). The “gu” is taken from “guniang” and combined with “ma,” ending up with “guma.” ☜

Chapter 67: We Are Doing This for the Sake of the Diabolic Creed

Not only did the branch leader have the highest cultivation in the entire branch, he had also undergone systematic training at the headquarters, where he studied the true essence of the diabolic path. He thought that he had already experienced all kinds of situations.

But something like this? I’ve really never encountered this before.

If one were to tell him that the administrators were considerate of their hard work and made preparations beforehand, that would still be understandable, and he would even be gratified. But what’s with these three? From which hole in the ground did they crawl out?

The branch leader soon figured out what was going on, his frosty gaze almost capable of killing. These three people are impersonating examiners and weeding out their competition in advance!

“What a clever trick!” the branch leader exclaimed through gritted teeth.

The three of them were still playing the role of examiners. Lu Yang propped his legs on the table. “You think you can pass without bribing us? Next!”

The next candidate respectfully presented spirit stones to the three examiners. Meng Jingzhou nodded but found the offering to be inadequate. “Do you have any experience in joining a diabolic creed?”

“No.”

“Oh, I’m sorry then. We don’t take in people without experience. Go back.”

He was at a loss for words. These examiners might as well write ‘we refuse to recruit anyone’ on their faces.

The branch leader appeared behind the trio like a specter. Frigid air seeped through their teeth as he fully unleashed their Golden Core aura, sending the three of them flying into a wall with just a smack. Had I arrived any later, everyone would have been gone!

Lu Yang extricated himself from the wall and hurriedly beseeched, “Your Excellency, we’re innocent! We were wholeheartedly thinking in the diabolic creed’s best interests!”

The branch leader found it amusing despite seething with anger. “Then why don’t you explain how you were being considerate of the diabolic creed?”

“Your Excellency, think about it. As diabolic cultivators, we should be skeptical, question everything, and not trust others easily. But look at these people. As soon as the three of us sat down here, they believed that we were the examiners. Not one person raised any questions. If they could fall for the trick so easily, wouldn’t they be just as easily duped by others? If there are smart people from the righteous path, they could just deceive every single one of them.

“Besides, only cultivators of the righteous path believe everything they’re told. I even suspected that there might be spies from the righteous path among these people. Your Excellency, you must investigate their identities thoroughly. We can’t let any righteous cultivators infiltrate the creed!” Lu Yang even shot a suspicious glance at the crowd of candidates, wearing an expression that said, “There’s definitely spies among you.” His heartfelt speech seemed to be a testament to how he had the branch leader’s interests at heart.

The branch leader’s expression relaxed slightly.

Meng Jingzhou was even more sincere than Lu Yang, as if he had directly translated his thoughts into words. “Moreover, diabolic cultivators are selfish and only think of themselves. With so many people here for the selection trials, we naturally needed to find ways to reduce the competition! If they’re not as skilled and get tricked, who can they blame? They can only blame it on themselves for not being experienced enough in deception!”

The branch leader’s brow smoothened out. This should be their genuine thoughts.

They are right. Diabolic cultivators should be wanton, show no regard for the law, be unscrupulous, and use any means possible. Back when I joined the diabolic creed, I also resorted to every trick in the book, which earned me the favor of the higher-ups, and that’s how I managed to achieve my position today.

These three people’s methods are even superior to mine in those days. Is this what they call a student surpassing the teacher?

Man Gu was the most straightforward as he declared, “We truly want to join the diabolic creed, and we guarantee that we won’t do a single good thing!”

The branch leader nodded. Maybe these three can also earn the favor of the higher-ups and improve the Yanjiang Branch’s evaluation.

The crowd glowered at the trio. All of us here are infamous hoodlums, rascals, and swindlers, but even then, none of us are as shameless as these three in deceiving everyone so brutally! These bastards!

If the branch leader weren’t around, they would have charged at the trio and shred them to pieces!

The branch leader didn’t care about the opinions of the people beneath him. Just a mediocre bunch. How can they compare to the value of these three?

“The three of you, what is your cultivation?”

Lu Yang replied deferentially, “We are all at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage. The three of us brothers are not from this region. We came to Yanjiang Commandery one month ago and happened to hear that the diabolic creed was recruiting, so we thought we’d give it a try. When we saw that there were too many competitors, we came up with this plan.”

“Well done.” The branch leader grew more pleased with the trio the more he looked at them. Such good fledglings. These are all part of my accomplishments.

With how I had casually waved my hand earlier, ordinary Basic Foundation Establishment cultivators would have gotten injured. In contrast, these three people were unscathed. This goes to show that they are the cream of the crop even among people at their level.

If these three perform decently well during the trials, it’s not impossible to promote them to administrators.

The people who had been “disqualified” gradually came back. The branch leader had called them back when he arrived. These people bore even greater resentment toward the trio. Lu Yang felt that if they were killed right now, they could likely turn into vengeful spirits.

The branch leader opened the stone wall and told everyone, “All of you, come in.”

Behind the stone wall was a vast yet dim space. Giant boulders were floating and connected by chains, forming a rather magnificent sight.

Lu Yang’s speculation had hit home—the Yanjiang Branch was located in a cave domain.

The branch leader’s attitude toward the trio was distinctly different compared to his attitude toward the rest. “Your idea was a good one, and you did well in eliminating the competition, but your direction was wrong from the start. Even if you eliminate these people or only the three of you had participated in the trials, it doesn’t mean that you’d pass.”

“What do you mean?” Lu Yang and the other two were bewildered.

The branch leader smiled underneath his mask. Stepping on the floating rocks, he led everyone to the most massive one.

It was a platform whose surface was carved with intricate and elegant patterns. Four ancient stone pillars stood at the four cardinal directions, and eleven respective black-robed administrators were stationed at the periphery of the platform.

“Spread yourselves out and have a seat; relax your minds.”

Everyone followed his instructions. The branch leader went to the center of the platform where a dark green stone hovered. The stone was engraved with dense, mysterious symbols.

As the branch leader infused the stone with spirit qi, the array beneath him activated. It expanded as it spun and replicated, covering the entire platform in an instant. The platform resembled an ancient colossal beast that was awakening, using mysterious powers from ancient times to send everyone to an unknown space.

In a pristinely white space, shadowy figures stood with blank expressions, unaware of what had happened. When Lu Yang saw the white space, he kept imagining that a Tofu Heavenly Sovereign might suddenly emerge from the crowd. He also noticed that neither Meng Jingzhou nor Man Gu was beside him; he was completely surrounded by strangers.

“Brother, where are you from?” Lu Yang tried to strike up a friendly conversation, but the person didn’t seem comfortable with Lu Yang’s enthusiasm.

However, the person also thought that it would be impolite to remain silent, so he replied, “From Huangyue City.”

Lu Yang continued asking a few more people. They came from different bases of the diabolic creed, yet they were all transported here with the gigantic array. He roughly understood what the branch leader’s intentions were. This selection trial isn’t conducted by each base but rather the headquarters; all rogue diabolic cultivators will be participating simultaneously.

“This feels like having the soul leave the body, but that’s not exactly it either,” Lu Yang mumbled to himself. He thought that the platform hadn’t transported their physical bodies but something similar to their consciousness instead. “This is pretty interesting. I wonder whether Big Senior Sister can...” Lu Yang stopped himself from thinking further. If I’m in a form of consciousness now, maybe the Everlasting Creed can detect what I am thinking.

Best to be cautious.

Suddenly, the whole space darkened. A figure emitting a white halo appeared in the air and announced without much emotion, “I am the Vice Creed Leader of the Everlasting Creed. I have set three rounds of trials for all of you. Those who pass all three trials may join our creed.”

Chapter 68: The Correct Method to Pass

The crowd became restless. They hadn’t expected the Everlasting Creed to take this selection so seriously; even the vice creed leader had turned up.

The vice creed leaders of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds were among the most notable personages on the Central Continent. Being able to meet one was considered a luxury.

On the other hand, Lu Yang was indifferent about it. They’re just at the same level as the elders in the Dao-Seeking Sect. It’s not like I’ve never seen such figures before.

“Your current state is a form of your consciousness; your real bodies are still where they originally were. After the official trials begin, your cultivation and memories will all be wiped out so that everyone will be at the same starting point.”

The creed leader placed great importance on this selection. Talents and geniuses matter most in the battle of the Great Era! If we find Single Spirit Roots, innate Celestial Physiques, and innate Diabolic Spawns, we’ll have the assets and leverage to contend with the righteous path!

To this end, they had the vice creed leader specially design the three rounds of tests to ensure that true geniuses would be selected! In order to prevent cheating, they would use one of the creed’s secret spells to erase the candidates’ cultivation and memories. That way, their true abilities could be reflected.

The vice creed leader announced, “The first round officially begins now. The passing criterion is to defeat the Liang Kingdom’s army.”

Everyone suddenly felt as if the world was spinning around them, and they couldn't distinguish the cardinal directions. By the time they regained their senses, they couldn't remember anything.

~~~

“Where am I?” Man Gu was still feeling dizzy as he came to his senses.

His hair was disheveled, the sword in his hand was broken, and his armor was stained with blood and dirt.

He took two steps forward, staggering as he almost fell down. His personal guard hastily supported him. “General, quickly get onto your horse! Now is not the time for maintaining righteousness and pride. The Liang Kingdom’s army is closing in!”

As Man Gu escaped on horseback, the details of the trial gradually flowed into Man Gu’s mind.

“There are two kingdoms: the Liang Kingdom and Jin Kingdom. There's a deep-seated enmity between them, and both wish to defeat the other party. The Jin Kingdom isn't as strong as the Liang Kingdom. I am the Jin Kingdom’s general, in charge of commanding the entire army.

“I was careless this time around and fell for the enemy’s trap. I must get my act together, make a comeback, and defeat the Liang Kingdom!”
