Man Gu had forgotten that this was a test. He only remembered that he was the victorious general of the Jin Kingdom, and his mission was to defeat the Liang Kingdom and protect his own kingdom.

Apart from memories regarding the background of the situation, war and combat experience also gushed into his mind. Man Gu had now completely become the Jin Kingdom’s victorious general.

Unfortunately, Man Gu might be very experienced, but that was also the case for the Liang Kingdom’s general. As the two parties clashed, Man Gu faced repeated defeats.

Man Gu was a venerable figure among the army, and the soldiers placed great trust in him. They believed that their setbacks were temporary and that their general, Man Gu, would ultimately lead them to victory.

Man Gu lost yet again. As he had an honest character, although he had experience in warfare, he couldn't apply it effectively in practice, and he would often fall for the traps set by the Liang Kingdom’s general.

“Whew, whew, whew...” Man Gu fled into a mountain cave in a sorry condition. He had suffered an utter defeat and lost his armor this time. It was the disgrace of his life.

The plaintive winds and rains outside rattled his heart, increasing the bleakness of the whole situation.

He thought about the trust his soldiers had in him. He thought about the repeated failures he suffered. He looked down at the sword in his hand. It was riddled with holes and jagged edges. He wished he could use it to end his life right now and then!

Everything will be resolved with death. Defeat? Jin Kingdom? They all have nothing to do with me!

Suddenly, a spider caught his attention. It bore a strange appearance, one that Man Gu had never seen before.

The spider was weaving a web, though the wind and rain outside the cave would blow in and tear it apart several times. Every time it was destroyed, the spider would start over again without being discouraged. Watching the spider fail again and again, yet continuing to try again and again, Man Gu saw a striking resemblance to his own plight.

“You will succeed!” Man Gu stared intently at the spider, hope slowly reigniting in his eyes. If even a spider can persist like this, as a person, how can my willpower be weaker than that of a spider?

Finally, after countless failures, the spider succeeded in weaving its web.

Man Gu sprung up to his feet, a fighting spirit burning inside him. The spider succeeded, so I will succeed too! I have to rally my forces again and strike back against the Liang Kingdom!

“Hmm?” Man Gu glanced at the spider, wanting to thank it for its encouragement, but he didn't expect a mantis to suddenly appear and kill the spider.

Consumed by rage, Man Gu initially wanted to stomp the mantis to death, but he recalled how similar the spider's circumstances were to his own. It became complacent after succeeding and forgot about the dangers lurking in the dark.

He pondered about it. “That’s right! Determination is important, but so is strategy. Striking when the enemy has become complacent can catch them by surprise and lead to unexpected results!”

In the end, Man Gu gave the Liang Kingdom small tastes of victories to numb them before commanding his troops to lie in ambush for attack. They broke through the main forces of the Liang Kingdom in one decisive strike and achieved an overwhelming victory.

Man Gu passed.

~~~

At the Everlasting Creed's headquarters, a calm water surface displayed everyone's appearance in the first round. The vice creed leader observed their performance and gave his evaluation.

“How did it go? Any prospective talents?” The space warped as the creed leader appeared. “This first round of yours is not easy. When faced with continuous setbacks, not only must one learn perseverance from the spider, but they also need to understand the principle of striking when the opponent least expects it from the mantis.”

The vice creed leader shook his head. “That is necessary. With the righteous sect oppressing us and the diabolic creeds facing repeated defeats, there are already people in the creed thinking of retreating. Our experiences and the Jin Kingdom's are so alike. Through this trial, I want to identify future members with strong willpower and nurture them so that they can fight against the righteous path! This requires not only determination but also technique. If they don’t learn the techniques from the spider and mantis, how can they achieve victory?”

The creed leader nodded. “Well said, this was also the reason I chose you to organize the selection trials this time. We have to prioritize training them; they will all be our backup forces in resisting the righteous path!”

The vice creed leader pointed at one of the scenes. “I have high hopes for this Man Gu. His method of passing perfectly fits how I intended it to be. This child is destined for greatness in the future!”

The creed leader eyed Man Gu and found him quite satisfactory. “Then let’s also see how the others perform.”

The creed leader and vice creed leader stood together and observed for a while when the creed leader suddenly asked, “Say, do you think it’s possible for there to be other methods to pass the trial?”

The vice creed leader firmly repudiated it without hesitation, “Absolutely impossible!

“The first round is a segment I’ve extracted from history. The Liang Kingdom and Jin Kingdom were a corner of the world’s chaos one hundred thousand years ago. At that time, cultivators were in fewer numbers, and they were even fewer in either of the two kingdoms. I have used this as a reference in my adaptation to ensure the highest degree of authenticity.”

For the sake of extracting the historical segment, the Everlasting Creed had poured in a substantial amount of resources, so much so that the vice creed leader’s heart ached.

“In history, the Jin Kingdom’s general gained enlightenment in the mountain cave and defeated the Liang Kingdom’s army! This was already a miracle. I refuse to believe that there are other methods!”

The creed leader nodded; he thought the same. He had asked the question earlier simply because he found the silence awkward and wanted to start a conversation.

Then, they saw how Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang passed.

Chapter 69: The Wrong Methods to Pass

After the Jin Kingdom’s army failed too many times, even Meng Jingzhou spiraled into despondence, thinking that victory was just a pipe dream.

“Can I really win?” Meng Jingzhou asked himself in the mountain cave, but he found the answer in his heart too bitter to utter it out loud.

“Hmm, a spider?” Meng Jingzhou noticed a spider weaving a web.

Watching the spider fail repeatedly but never stop trying greatly astonished him.

“The spider rises again after every failure. I can’t be worse than a spider, right?”

Meng Jingzhou’s morale was boosted, and he planned to rally his forces again to battle the Liang Kingdom once more!

“The Liang Kingdom’s army is stronger than ours, but it is not an insurmountable gulf between us. Besides, how could I give up just because of a few defeats? If I give up, what is the Jin Kingdom behind me supposed to do? I believe that with the appropriate stratagem this time, we have a chance at victory!” Meng Jingzhou clenched his fists, a plan already formulated in his mind.

After failing several times, he was now familiar with the Liang Kingdom’s general’s tactics.

Having won numerous times, the Liang Kingdom’s general’s ego must have inflated. I can make use of his mentality to my advantage. I’ll first feign defeat and scurry away like a sorry loser, then lure the Liang Kingdom’s army into a canyon, turning the tables on them and encircling them. This time, we’ll definitely strike with the element of surprise and not let down the expectations of our elders!

“Thank you for the guidance,” Meng Jingzhou cupped his fists at the spider.

If it weren’t for the spider’s edification, I would have remained demoralized and not been able to bounce back. Victory would have really been a lost cause then.

There were many mosquitoes and insects in the cave. To express his gratitude, Meng Jingzhou caught an insect and placed it beside the spider. However, the spider didn’t seem to understand Meng Jingzhou’s actions. It treated him as an enemy and bit him.

“It’s a venomous spider...” Meng Jingzhou fainted.

It was unclear how much time had passed; it was perhaps a few minutes or more than ten minutes. In any case, it wasn’t long. Meng Jingzhou woke up and found himself brimming with strength. “What happened to me?”

Meng Jingzhou felt that his body had undergone some change. His vision, hearing, and senses were all enhanced, and his body was flexible and agile like never before, as if he had been born again. Suddenly, his right hand subconsciously moved, and his middle and ring fingers bent, as white silk spurted forth.

“What the hell is this?!!!”

The white silk adhered to the wall. Meng Jingzhou pulled them with force and found them to be unusually tough and durable.

“Why do they look like spider silk?”

Meng Jingzhou pressed both of his hands against the wall and was shocked that they could also stick. Leaping across roofs and vaulting over walls will be a cinch.

“I remember that I was bitten by a spider... wait a minute, where’s the spider?”

By the time Meng Jingzhou found the spider, it had already been killed by a mantis. He stomped the mantis to death to avenge the spider. Inheriting the spider’s final wishes and legacy, he regrouped his army and battled it out with the Liang Kingdom’s army again.

On the night before the final battle, wearing a night stealth attire and relying on his newly obtained powers, he carried out a decapitation operation by himself, directly beheading the Liang Kingdom’s general. Although the general had bodyguards who were cultivators, they weren’t as nimble as Meng Jingzhou, allowing Meng Jingzhou to kill the general successfully.

Before dying, the Liang Kingdom’s general had been dumbfounded. As generals, shouldn’t both our armies meet on the battlefield with weapons and engage in some kind of final battle? Yet you’re here skipping through all the steps and having a general kill another general?

The Liang Kingdom’s general was a rare military genius. After he died, his army was left without a leader and thrown into disarray. As there was no one who could rise up to the occasion and take charge, Meng Jingzhou led the Jin Kingdom’s army to crush the Liang Kingdom’s army.

Meng Jingzhou passed.

~~~

At the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, the creed leader and vice creed leader didn’t speak for a long time after watching the way Meng Jingzhou passed.

A second method of passing has really emerged.

The creed leader massaged his brow. “What’s the deal with the spider? Why could it grant someone spider-like abilities with just a bite? Don’t tell me that if I bite the spider, it can turn into human form?”

The vice creed leader was also dumbstruck. After pondering for a while, it seemed like a revelation had hit him. He took out an ancient book from his storage ring and pointed to a passage. “I’ve found it. Look, the ancient texts record that there once was a type of peculiar spider on the Central Continent. Its strength was the same as ordinary spiders, and it never bit people, but anyone who was bitten by it would undergo a mutation.

“This type of spider had become extinct tens of thousands of years ago.” The vice creed leader reasoned, “The events of the Jin Kingdom and Liang Kingdom took place one hundred thousand years ago. Since we perfectly recreated the scenes from that time, from a theoretical viewpoint, it is possible for such a spider to appear in the cave.”

The creed leader nodded. “Looks like this Meng Jingzhou not only has resolve and a quick-witted mind but also good fortune.”

However, the topic of luck was elusive. Perhaps only the Qi-Gazing Technique from the legends could truly assess one’s fortune. Nonetheless, it could be reflected in other aspects. Meng Jingzhou was one example. Among the plethora of people going through the trial, he was the only one who got bitten by the spider and mutated. This exemplified how his luck was exceptional, unlike others.

A person with great fortune will find their cultivation to be on a flatland, and their accomplishments in the future will be very impressive.

“Let’s continue to check out the others. I refuse to believe that there is a third method of passing.”

~~~

Lu Yang watched the spider continuously weaving its web yet constantly failing, causing him to sink into deep thought.

“If spider webs can capture prey, why did waiting idly for a rabbit to crash into a tree fail?[1] Aren’t they all waiting for prey to come to their doorstep? What’s the difference between the two?

“Is it because the insects aren’t smart, so they could only foolishly bump into the web? On the other hand, the rabbit is smarter and knows how to avoid the tree? If bugs aren’t smart, that means that spiders also aren’t smart. The spider experiences repeated setbacks but doesn’t stop weaving the web—does that reflect strong determination or a fool’s persistence? Even the rabbit knows not to crash into trees, so why are there still people stubbornly insisting on crashing into a wall?” Lu Yang’s thoughts wandered far. Despite experiencing failures, he wasn’t discouraged. He simply sought shelter from the rain in the cave and took the chance to come up with methods to defeat the enemy. Now that he saw the spider weaving its web, he thought of many questions that seemed profound but were actually useless.

Suddenly, a mantis appeared, ambushing the spider while it had its guard down. The spider desperately resisted with its web, but the mantis was deft and intense. After a few rounds, it killed the spider.

Having witnessed the whole process, Lu Yang fell deep in thought. He stood up and recalled the mantis’ movements. For the hand movements, he learned how the mantis skillfully used its agile forelimbs, and for the leg movements, he learned how it deftly leaped in all directions.

“Imagine myself as a mantis...” Lu Yang murmured to himself. He felt as if he had learned something similar before and was extremely talented in this area.

Lu Yang was like a human-form mantis, bold and swift with the coalescence of firmness and flexibility. Any opponent would fall under his fist technique.

The general of the Jin Kingdom in history was at the Intermediate Qi Training Stage, which Lu Yang had inherited.

Toward the end of his training, he transformed into a large mantis. One swift fist from his forelimb caused the cave to collapse.

Lu Yang marveled, “So is this the legendary Mantis Fist in the wulin? It has such formidable power, but a problem is that ordinary people can’t learn it.”

Lu Yang simplified Mantis Fist so that it was easy to pick up. He widely propagated it throughout the Jin Kingdom’s army, allowing their military power to surpass that of the Liang Kingdom. There was no need for any stratagem. They simply marched forward, sweeping through the enemy lines effortlessly.

Lu Yang passed.

~~~

“Who on earth passes like this?!” the vice creed leader roared in rage.

1. The idiom of the rabbit waiting idly by the tree is a classic story advising people to not just sit back and leave things to chance but take the initiative instead. ☜

Chapter 70: The Second Round of the Selection Trials

“Who practices Mantis Fist like this?!” The vice creed leader’s eyes widened. He had heard of Mantis Fist before—it was a fist technique that imitated the movements of a mantis.

It’s supposed to imitate a mantis, not turn into one!

To ensure that the selection trials would meet expectations, he had simulated it repeatedly and even asked a few sharp-minded higher-ups to test it out. With that, he ascertained that aside from his intended solution, it was impossible to derive a second solution. Even if two other unexpected solutions had just emerged, I can’t accept it!

The creed leader was not too hung up about it and accepted it more calmly. “If you think about it from another perspective, it merely took him a few glances at the mantis to comprehend Mantis Fist. The Jin Kingdom’s general from history was also not talented in martial Dao, which all the more implies that this person called Lu Yang possesses extremely high aptitude! In the end, he even attained the Dao through martial arts, achieving the advanced realm of transforming martial techniques into spell techniques. We’ve stumbled across a rare genius!”

The vice creed leader was dumbstruck for a bit before turning to look at the creed leader with a serious expression. “Are you being serious?”

The creed leader thought, Of course, I made that up. Actually, I also couldn’t tell how he transformed from a human into a mantis. But as the creed leader, I can’t show my ignorance in front of my subordinates.

The creed leader proceeded to nod. “Of course, I’m serious.”

The vice creed leader’s mood slightly improved after hearing the creed leader’s words. Since he is a rare genius that is hard to come by, it’s also not a stretch that he accidentally found an unconventional way to turn the tide.

I can force myself to accept this.

“Everyone who could pass has passed by now, so let’s end the first round here,” the vice creed leader said.

There were hundreds of thousands of scenes displayed on the water surface, each one of them recording the performance of every candidate. Only a selected few could comprehend perseverance from the spider, and even fewer comprehended strategy from the mantis. Most people didn’t bounce back on their feet and became an army deserter. They were killed by the Liang Kingdom’s soldiers in the chaos of war and perished in a nameless death. The soldiers from the Liang Kingdom didn’t even know that the person they killed was once full of spirit and ambition.

“The second round begins.”

~~~

“The second round tests whether you can make the examiner sincerely want to let you stay.” This sentence suddenly popped up in everyone’s mind. They had forgotten everything else, only remembering that they had to come up with a way to pass the second round.

Yan Wangsun was feeling a bit dizzy. He had no recollection of what had previously transpired, except for a vague memory of a sociable person asking him where he was from, to which he replied with “Huangyue City.”

“I’m Yan Wangsun. I am currently interviewing for a position in the Luodi Merchant Guild. The interview rule states that I can’t share the interview questions with others.” Yan Wangsun organized the information he currently had. Even if this wasn’t a requirement, I wouldn’t have told others about the interview questions either. Helping others in this case brings no benefit to myself.

He then noticed that he was sitting in the first position, and next to him was a burly man donned in Confucian robes.

“I’m Man Gu. What about you?”

Yan Wangsun didn’t answer because the examiner happened to call his name then.

Upon entering the room, Yan Wangsun noticed a ball of paper on the ground. He casually tossed it into a trashcan before preparing for the interview.

The examiner was plump with clothes barely fitting and wore a permanent smile. “You’re Yan Wangsun, right? Go to the marketplace now and see if anyone’s selling potatoes.”

Yan Wangsun obediently left for the marketplace and made his round. There was only one shop selling potatoes, and he came back, replying, “Yes.”

The plump examiner posed another question, “How many potatoes?”

Yan Wangsun had no choice but to run out again. When he came back, he answered, “There are eighty jin[1] of potatoes.”

"And what about the price?”

Yan Wangsun cursed inside his heart, Why didn’t you say so earlier, fatty? He ran out a third time and came back with the price. “Three copper coins for one jin.”

“How’s the quality of the potatoes? Does it match the price?”

Suppressing his burning fury, Yan Wangsun ran out for the fourth time to examine the potatoes’ quality and returned with an answer. “The quality of the potatoes is average and looks to be about three to four copper coins, so the selling price isn’t very high.”

The plump examiner smilingly said, “You’re disqualified.”

“Based on what?!” Yan Wangsun was furious. He felt like he was a leashed dog forced to be walked four times by the plump examiner. Every single time I would run out and run back, but after all that hard work, you’re telling me that I’ve failed?!

Are you toying with me?!

The plump examiner spread his hands. “You had to go out four times just for a trivial matter like answering questions about potatoes. How can I trust you to handle the job?”

“Then you could have asked all the questions in one go!”

The plump examiner shook his head. “You were not meticulous and thorough with your work, so how can you blame me for not asking the questions at once? Young man, you need to anticipate the intentions from above in the workplace.”

“Pfft, intentions from above? You think you’re the emperor?”

The plump examiner was not offended. “Although you have failed, you can still stay behind.”

Yan Wangsun looked at the plump examiner suspiciously, worried that he was being played with again. “Really?”

“Do you still remember the ball of paper you picked up right when you stepped in? I had purposely thrown that on the floor so that I could see who would pick it up.”

Yan Wangsun was overjoyed. Is this testing my sense of responsibility and observation skills?

“We happen to be short on a janitor. You can stay behind and be in charge of maintaining hygiene and sanitation.”

Yan Wangsun, “...”

He really wanted to lash out at him, but none of the words came out. No matter what, being able to stay means that I’ve passed the trial, which is a good thing.

“Next,” the plump examiner called.

Man Gu walked into the room. Upon seeing Man Gu’s honest demeanor, Yan Wangsun was somewhat disdainful. This person will definitely be toyed with by the examiner just like I was.

“Go and see if there’s anyone selling potatoes in the marketplace,” the plump examiner asked the same question.

Man Gu simply responded with an affirmative and left. It took him more than ten minutes to return.

“There’s an old man pushing a cart of potatoes in the marketplace. There are eighty jin of potatoes, and one jin is worth three copper coins. The price and quality match, and the old man even said that if we buy in bulk, he can lower the price further by ten percent...” Man Gu’s answer was extremely detailed, even covering questions the plump examiner hadn’t considered. At the side, Yan Wangsun was completely dazed.

Although Man Gu might not look like it with his burly appearance, he was an attentive person inside. He was adept at being humble in learning, especially when learning from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, though judging based on his current progress in this aspect, he still had a long way to go before graduation.

“Congratulations, you may stay.”

~~~

“See? I said that Man Gu is a prospective talent.” The vice creed leader was elated to see Man Gu passing once again. This proves that my thought process in designing the questions is correct.

Among the other candidates, there were some who answered four of the examiner’s questions in two trips, which allowed them to barely pass.

Only Man Gu perfectly fits my expectations.

The creed leader nodded. “Looks like this second round tests whether one is thorough and capable of considering their superior's point of view.”

The diabolic path has to be cautious and not leave any incriminating traces to avoid the righteous path getting a hold on them. Moreover, by taking into account their superior’s perspective, it demonstrated that one had the potential for advancement, prompting the higher-ups to promote them.

It was out of such considerations that the vice creed leader had come up with the second trial.

The vice creed leader smiled smugly. “There shouldn’t be other methods this time.”

The creed leader didn’t speak, simply turning his gaze to the two people with excellent performance in the first round.

His instincts told him that there might be other methods.

1. 1 jin is 500g. In this case, it’ll be 40kg. ☜

Chapter 71: Sincerely

“The second trial is to make the examiner sincerely want to let me stay?” Meng Jingzhou read through the passing condition again.

“What a strange test. It doesn't sound difficult. Anyway, where am I?” Meng Jingzhou was sitting on a bench. He was sitting in the middle with four people in front of him and five behind.

“Oh, I'm interviewing for the merchant guild.” The identity and setting assigned by the Everlasting Creed popped up in his mind.

Facing the immaculately white wall in front of him, Meng Jingzhou’s hand subconsciously moved, his middle and ring fingers bending.

Nothing is spurting out.

“Hmm? Why am I doing such a strange action?” Meng Jingzhou was perplexed, not remembering that he had such a habit. “Forget it, I shall focus on the interview.”

He noticed the first person entering the examination room then hastily running out before dashing back in again, repeating this three to four times.

Meng Jingzhou called out enthusiastically, “Hey, brother, why are you running? Is the examiner testing your running speed? If that's the case, I'll recommend that you change your shoes. A pair of good-quality shoes can greatly boost your speed. Your starting posture also matters. You should crouch down and arch your back with your hands on the ground as support. That will help you run much faster. Trust me, I'm very experienced...”

The person looked at Meng Jingzhou as if the latter was an idiot. Ignoring Meng Jingzhou, they ran out to check the quality of the potatoes.

The rules had clearly stated that candidates were not allowed to leak the questions to other candidates.

This went on for the second person, third person, and fourth person; everyone was very diligent in running, but they also didn't pass. However, regardless of whether one passed, they would disappear right after their interview ended. That way, the people lining up behind them wouldn't be able to distinguish whether making more or fewer trips was the key to passing.

“Next, Meng Jingzhou!” the plump examiner shouted from inside.

“Coming.” Meng Jingzhou was in high spirits as he sauntered inside.

The plump examiner wore a smile as usual. “Meng Jingzhou, go to the marketplace and see if there's anyone selling potatoes.”

Meng Jingzhou didn't move.

The plump examiner mistook it as them not relaying the instructions clearly, so they repeated the question, enunciating every word.

This time, Meng Jingzhou spoke, “Why?”

“What do you mean why?” The plump examiner couldn't follow Meng Jingzhou’s line of thought.

“I'm asking why I have to go to the marketplace and see if there's anyone selling potatoes. Do you know what we are doing now?”

“An interview,” the plump examiner replied in a matter-of-fact tone.

“Exactly, you said it yourself—this is an interview, not a time for you to get people to run your errands. By the way, did you also ask the four people in front this same question? You’re still not satisfied after asking four times, and now you still want to ask it a fifth time?!”

The plump examiner patiently explained, “This is the exam question.”

Meng Jingzhou replied with a simple “oh” and obediently made a trip to the marketplace.

“There's someone selling potatoes,” answered Meng Jingzhou when he returned.

“How many jin of potatoes are there?”

Meng Jingzhou didn't know the answer, so he stood up and walked toward the door.

A sliver of a sneer appeared on the plump examiner’s visage. Kid, you talk the most nonsense. Come back one more time, and I'll announce that you've failed.

To his surprise, when Meng Jingzhou opened the door, it revealed an old man standing outside.

Meng Jingzhou asked the old man, “How many potatoes do you have in your cart?”

“Eighty jin,” replied the old man.

Meng Jingzhou turned his head back. “He said there’s eighty jin of potatoes. Do you also want to ask how much each jin costs?”

The plump examiner opened his mouth but couldn’t bring himself to ask “How much does one jin of potatoes cost?” Even if he had asked it out loud, the old man at the door would have answered immediately.

What’s the point of asking now?!

The plump examiner questioned in ire, “Why did you bring the potato seller over here?” How am I going to test the remaining candidates?

Meng Jingzhou shrugged. “I asked him whether a few people had come by to ask about the potatoes, and he complained that these few people had run over, taken a glimpse of his potatoes, run back, then run over, asked him for the total jin of potatoes, run back, then run over again to ask how much each jin costs. However, they all only asked and didn’t buy anything.

“Then, I asked him if he wanted to meet the main culprit behind all this, and he said yes, so I brought him over here.”

The plump examiner, “...”

What am I supposed to do for the rest of the tests? No one told me that I’d encounter a situation like this...

Recalling Meng Jingzhou’s disrespect, the plump examiner steeled himself and yelled, “You weren’t able to anticipate the intentions from above and have been disqualified...”

Before he could finish, Meng Jingzhou gave him a kick. “To hell with intentions from above! Who are you to say that? I’ve been too respectful to you!” Meng Jingzhou ran outside.

The plump examiner smashed the table into pieces. “Stop right there!”

Since the examiner sincerely wanted to let Meng Jingzhou stay, Meng Jingzhou passed.

~~~

The vice creed leader massaged his knitted brow. What is this strange method of passing? I set the requirement that the examiner must sincerely want to let the interviewee stay because I was worried that someone may try to take a shortcut and bribe the examiner. I thought I was already meticulous enough, but I didn’t expect there to still be another way to pass.

How on earth is this young fellow’s brain wired? Or am I the one without a brain wired?

“O undying and indestructible Everlasting Immortal, please give me an answer,” the vice creed leader muttered a prayer to the Everlasting Immortal, hoping that he would receive a response.

The creed leader interrupted the vice creed leader’s prayers, “If only the Everlasting Immortal could hear your words.”

The vice creed leader didn’t think that the creed leader was being blasphemous. He knew that the creed leader was the most pious follower in the Everlasting Creed. He sighed, “How many times have we tried? But they all failed. We still can’t resurrect the Everlasting Immortal. If we could, regardless of whether it’s the Great Xia Dynasty or the righteous path, they’re no match for the Everlasting Immortal!

“Only with blood as sacrifice can the Everlasting Immortal be resurrected.”

The two didn’t linger on this topic, and the vice creed leader soon changed the subject. “What do you think of Meng Jingzhou?”

The creed leader clicked his tongue in praise. “One who takes the road less traveled. A true talent.” Luckily I didn’t agree with the vice creed leader that there wouldn’t be other methods to passing. Otherwise, my reputation as the creed leader would’ve gone down the drain!

“Are you sure this young fellow can also be considered a talent?”

“Of course, I feel that what our Everlasting Creed needs is precisely such talents with unorthodox thinking. Look at the Dao-Seeking Sect from the righteous path. Why have they lasted so long? I’ve summarized a few reasons, and the most important one is that they possess wisdom beyond the understanding of people in this world.”

The corner of the vice creed leader’s mouth twitched. As expected of the creed leader, describing madness in such a refined manner.

The creed leader continued, “Who knows if this Meng Jingzhou can become the backbone of our Everlasting Creed?! Speaking of Meng Jingzhou, there was another young fellow who left quite the impression in the first round. If I remember correctly, his name seems to be Lu Yang. How did he do?”

~~~

“Make the examiner sincerely want to let me stay?”

Lu Yang ruminated over it. What’s so difficult about that? I just have to give the examiner a kick. Best is if I can also spit on him. I’m sure that will anger the examiner so much that he won’t want just me to stay; he might even want my life to stay with him.

However, this method was too barbaric. Only a crude person like Meng Jingzhou would use such a method. Lu Yang couldn't be like him. He was a civilized person.

Chapter 72: Three Heroes of the Diabolic Creed

Lu Yang was sixth in the line of ten interviewees. He had also noticed that the people in front of him would run out at the speed of a hundred-meter sprint after entering the examiner’s room, after which they would run back again, repeating this process a few times.

“What kind of strange interview question is this?”

Lu Yang was not one to sit still. Although the rules forbid him from asking the other interviewees about the contents of the interview, there was no rule about going out to take a look.

He asked a rogue diabolic cultivator next to him who was resting with his eyes closed, “Do you want to go out and take a look?”

The rogue diabolic cultivator glimpsed at Lu Yang in contempt and said nothing. How could diabolic cultivators act in groups? This guy must be trying to trick me. No way. Not going.

Not receiving a response from the other party, Lu Yang became sympathetic. He’s handsome, but it’s a pity that he’s deaf. What is he going to do when he can’t hear the examiner speak during the interview later?

Seeing no one pay any attention to himself, Lu Yang headed outside, where he was greeted by a bustling marketplace. One could find vendors selling fruits, eggs, pork, and all common types of food here. The hawkers would set up stalls or push small carts and peddle their goods.

“I’ll have an apple.” Lu Yang bought an apple and rubbed it before eating. As he munched on the apple, he observed the actions of the interviewees.

The third person happened to run out to see if there was anyone selling potatoes. Upon spotting a potato vendor, they immediately ran back to report to the examiner.

In less than three minutes, this person came running out again. They asked the old man selling potatoes how many jin of potatoes there were in total and how much each jin cost.

Another three minutes passed. It was still the same person. They had run out to inspect the quality of the potatoes.

Afterward, the fourth person came. Their process was practically identical to the third person’s. The only difference was that he made four trips as he wasn’t as quick-witted as the third person.

Lu Yang continued to chew on his apple, deep in thought.

~~~

“Next, Fang Hao,” the plump examiner called.

Fang Hao was the person Lu Yang had invited to go out together with earlier.

“Here!” To Lu Yang’s surprise, Fang Hao was actually not deaf.

“Go to the marketplace and see if there’s anyone selling potatoes.” The plump examiner repeated his usual trick.

Fang Hao hastily dashed out. He was taking quite the time to come back, something the plump examiner found puzzling.

Just as the plump examiner was getting impatient, Fang Hao returned. “There’s no one selling potatoes in the marketplace.”

“How many jin of potatoes...wait, what did you just say? There’s no one selling potatoes?”

Fang Hao didn’t understand why the plump examiner had such a huge reaction, but he still nodded. “That’s right. I ran around the marketplace twice to make sure that there was nobody selling potatoes.”

“That’s impossible!” The plump examiner thought that Fang Hao was lying to him. He hurriedly ran out with Fang Hao following closely behind.

As soon as the plump examiner stepped outside, he saw Lu Yang pushing a cart of potatoes. The cart read “potatoes not for sale.”

Meanwhile, the old man who was supposed to be selling potatoes was happily counting his silvers.

Seeing the plump examiner, Lu Yang ran with the cart of potatoes.

The plump examiner was furious. What am I going to do with the remaining interviews with the potatoes gone?

“Stop right there!!”

Lu Yang passed.

~~~

“This is preposterous!” The vice creed leader flew into a rage, wild and frightening aura waves emitting from him. The whole hall shook, and ripples formed on the water surface, obscuring the scenes of the live broadcast.

The exam I’ve meticulously designed is riddled with flaws in front of these two scourges! It’s an absolute disgrace!

The creed leader calmly intervened to suppress the vice creed leader’s aura waves. It wasn’t easy for us to find a place to build this hall. If we get discovered by the righteous path because of a mere matter like this, that would totally be a joke.

The creed leader advised, “Don’t get angry so easily. Their current selves have forgotten everything else except for their task to find a way to pass the trials. As a diabolic creed, what we’re particular about is killing people to revive the Everlasting Immortal. How can we kill people because of something like this? Besides, these two people are rare talents who can blaze a new trail. Ever since the inception of the Everlasting Creed, there haven’t been major breakthroughs. I feel that these two people are our hope.”

The vice creed leader thought to himself, That means that there is no hope left for the Everlasting Creed.

The creed leader said with slight excitement, “Speaking of which, Man Gu, as well as Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang, they’re all from Yanjiang Commandery, right? I didn’t expect three talents to appear in a small place like Yanjiang Commandery. It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to call them the Three Heroes of the Diabolic Creed. With these Three Heroes, our sect will be stronger than ever like a tiger that has grown wings!”

The vice creed leader muttered softly, “Like a tiger that has grown wings? Isn’t that a qiongqi[1]? Even a qiongqi can’t defeat the righteous sect.”

The creed leader glared at him. “Shut up, you didn’t have to show off that you’re cultured.”

The vice creed leader obediently shut his mouth.

~~~

At Yanjiang Commandery, eleven administrators were trying their best to maintain the great array. Close to a hundred rogue diabolic cultivators stood rooted to the spot, their eyes vacant and in a daze. Their consciousness was undergoing the trials on behalf of their physical body.

Maintaining the great array was too boring, so the administrators began to chat while ingesting Qi Restoration Pills. “Qin Yuanhao has disappeared for so long that he’s probably dead.”

“He’s definitely dead. We just don’t know how he died. I’ve said a long time ago that with this fellow constantly scheming and thinking that everything was under his control, it was only a matter of time that he would offend an enemy, and they would find a dark, windy night to get rid of him.”

“Qin Yuanhao’s body hasn’t been found either.”

“Did one of his enemies kill him?”

“What else then? It can’t possibly be his benefactor turning on him and killing him, right? Those in our line of work have no benefactors.”

“Why did I hear that the night Qin Yuanhao died, he went to have a whale of a time in the brothel with Big Mouth Wang?”

The administrators chuckled.

Just as Qin Yuanhao had wished, Big Mouth Wang had gone around spreading rumors of how he and Qin Yuanhao were a force to be reckoned with, battling it out all night long with no mercy in the brothel.

Then, Qin Yuanhao died.

Hence, rumors of Qin Yuanhao dying from exhausting his energy spread in Yanjiang Commandery. Qin Yuanhao could probably rest in peace if he learned about this in the underworld.

“I wonder how many people in this batch will pass the trials.”

Although there were many people participating in the initiation ceremony, those who could pass the trials and successfully join the creed were a different matter. Having one out of ten make it was already a decent number.

To become administrators, they had all passed similar trials, so they understood the difficulty within.

With the vice creed leader personally organizing it this time, the difficulty level will definitely go down in history!

“Only the branch leader knows the results.” The eleven people turned to look at the branch leader who was in a meditative state.

The branch leader had made use of the great array constructed by the Everlasting Creed to enter the mysterious space. All branch leaders were able to view their respective branch’s performance.

As Lu Yang and the other two displayed exemplary performance, the branch leader was so thrilled that it seemed like a chrysanthemum had bloomed on his face. However, he was wearing a mask, so no one could see how ecstatic he was.

He excitedly mumbled, “If these three people can successfully pass and earn high praise from the higher-ups, the Yanjiang Branch’s year-end performance will definitely be among the top! If I push it a bit more and improve my cultivation, maybe I can be transferred to a wealthier place as branch leader, or I may even be directly promoted to Hall Leader!”

After the three rounds of trials ended, the vice creed leader and creed leader assessed the new members with outstanding performance. For example, their evaluation of Qin Yuanhao was “diabolic nature to the bone.”

The branch leader believed that Lu Yang and the other two would receive a much higher appraisal than Qin Yuanhao.

It’s so obvious at a glance that these three aren’t any good eggs!

1. Just in case, here’s a refresher: Qiongqi is one of the Four Fearsome Beasts. I suppose it does somewhat resemble a tiger with wings. The tiger demon in earlier chapters was said to have some Qiongqi blood in them. ☜

Chapter 73: Spy From the Righteous Path

“Hmm? We’re back here again?” Lu Yang opened his eyes, finding himself back in the mysterious white space.

There were many familiar people around him, including Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, Chi Xulong, and Shen Jinyi.

Only ten people from the Yanjiang Branch successfully passed the first two rounds. Lu Yang recognized half of them. As for the other half, he didn’t get the chance to trick them for their personal information when he was impersonating an examiner.

The memories from the first two rounds gradually flowed into his mind. Mantis Fist in the first round. Pushing the cart of potatoes in the second round...

“It looks like the Everlasting Creed’s trials aren’t all that hard either.” Lu Yang felt that his performance was average. Anyone with a brain can do it.

“I think so too,” Meng Jingzhou agreed. “Just get bitten by the spider in the first round and deliver a punch to that fat guy in the second round.”

Lu Yang looked at Meng Jingzhou, slightly astounded. “Hmm? Why are our methods of passing different?”

Meng Jingzhou waved his hand confidently. “Do you even have to ask? My answer is definitely the correct one. Yours was just a fluke.”

Lu Yang scoffed at Meng Jingzhou’s confidence. “Ridiculous! In the first round, my comprehension of Mantis Fist demonstrates my proficiency in martial Dao. What can your performance in the first round show? Luck? Is that what matters for a member of the Everlasting Creed? It’s clear that my answer is the correct one!”

“I advise you to face reality.”

As Man Gu watched the two’s intense argument by the side, he silently recalled how he had passed. In the first round, I learned perseverance from the spider, then learned to act with strategy from the mantis. In the second round, I practiced perspective-taking and made sure to be thorough in my work.

“Now that I think about it, my method of passing does seem a little too ordinary. It looks like Brother Lu and Brother Meng are correct. I just don’t know whose method is the most correct,” Man Gu mumbled to himself. He felt that he had once again learned something new.

There was still no conclusion to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s squabble. As a clear-headed bystander, Man Gu stepped in to stop them. “Is it possible that both of your methods are correct? The diabolic creed emphasizes acting unscrupulously and doing whatever one wishes to. Perhaps there is no correct answer, or perhaps any method that works is a correct answer.”

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou stared at Man Gu in astonishment. They felt that he made a lot of sense.

Lu Yang marveled, “I didn’t expect the diabolic creed’s trials to be so open-ended in style.”

Meng Jingzhou nodded.

“Speaking of which, we’ve only passed two rounds. Why are we back here? What about the third round?” The trio suddenly recalled they had proper things to do.

The vice creed leader’s figure appeared in the sky once again. He held an orb the size of his palm with a small slit in the middle. Taking a step in mid-air, the mysterious white space immediately changed. With him as the center, buildings began to emerge like tides surging. City walls, palaces, courtyards, small pavilions, towering mountains, rivers that traversed through the whole city, pedestrians in a rush, hawkers peddling, cultivators moving mountains and seas... It looked just like a grand cultivation city!

Once again, the vice creed leader split everyone up by branch. The ten people from the Yanjiang Branch sat in a small pavilion where they could see the scenery outside.

The vice creed leader’s emotionless voice sounded in everyone’s ears. “Congratulations on passing the first two rounds of the trials. We will now proceed to the third round.

“This is a city I have simulated. In a little while, I will unleash your inherent nature. It will make you believe that this is the real world and let you do the bad things you genuinely want to do. The more destruction you bring about, the higher our evaluation of you. The time limit is one day and one night.”

The vice creed leader raised the orb in his hand. The orb’s slit widened, revealing a black pupil.

This wasn’t an orb but a gigantic eye!

As the eye opened, strange rays of purple light enveloped the entire city.

~~~

When the vice creed leader’s consciousness returned to the headquarters, he was still holding the giant eye. “As expected of the Immortal Eye crafted by the Everlasting Immortal. Human nature is the most complex. Only an immortal treasure is capable of releasing people’s inherent natures and drawing out their deepest, darkest side.”

The vice creed leader was reluctant as he returned the Immortal Eye to the creed leader. There aren’t many opportunities to use an immortal’s treasure.

In theory, he didn’t have the authority to use the Immortal Eye. However, for the purpose of starting the third round, the creed leader had temporarily lent it to him.

The creed leader stressed, “The third round of the trials is extremely crucial. It concerns whether spies from the righteous path have infiltrated the diabolic path. Since the Immortal Eye can let loose a person’s inherent nature, with how kind the righteous cultivators are, they wouldn’t cause much destruction. Under the light of the Immortal Eye, those righteous cultivators won’t have a chance to go against their true nature and commit murder and arson! Furthermore, if the righteous cultivators witness acts of injustice, they would even lend a helping hand. That way, we’ll be able to filter out those righteous cultivators who have tried to infiltrate our ranks!”

To become a member of the Everlasting Creed, the first requirement is that one mustn’t be a spy from the righteous path.

The vice creed leader smiled. “Besides, this Immortal Eye can also automatically assess the level of destruction based on one’s cultivation. With the Immortal Eye around, both you and I just have to wait for the results.”

~~~

Squelch!

A pedestrian was pierced through the heart by a sword. The other passers-by shrieked and fled in terror. Behind them was a rogue diabolic cultivator cackling out loud while hacking at those around him, causing their heads to roll to the ground. Corpses were littered everywhere.

“Refreshing, it feels good!” The rogue diabolic cultivator was elated to let their inherent nature run wild. They never had a chance to kill to their heart’s content before. “Today, I will use your corpses to establish my footing in the Everlasting Creed!”

I’m going to make use of this opportunity to kill as much as I like!

“Stop!” A large spear suddenly appeared, deflecting the rogue diabolic cultivator’s sword.

The rogue diabolic cultivator was slightly stunned to see the new joiner. “I was wondering who it was. Isn’t this Fang Hao? You usually put on such a cold facade that I thought you were a true evil diabolic path cultivator. Turns out you’re from the righteous path.”

Fang Hao tried his best to keep his composure, reminding himself that it was a critical moment and that he mustn't expose his identity as a righteous path cultivator. Otherwise, all my previous efforts would have been in vain!

Unfortunately, under the glow of the Immortal Eye’s purple light, any disguise was useless.

I can’t stand the rogue diabolic cultivator’s wanton slaughter! I want to do everything I can to stop it!

This was an impulse from the bottom of his heart that couldn’t be restrained.

Fang Hao clashed with the rogue diabolic cultivator, crossing their sword and spear. For now, it wasn’t clear who would prevail.

~~~

“As I thought, someone from the righteous path has tried to infiltrate us!” the vice creed leader exclaimed irately. If not for the third round, this Fang Hao would have joined the Everlasting Creed!

The creed leader’s gaze was frosty. “You should know what to do without me saying anything.”

The vice creed leader nodded. “I’ll get the Huangyue Branch Leader to kill him now!”

“Kill him my ass! Quickly inform the Huangyue Branch Leader that the location of their base has been exposed and that they need to quickly escape!”

“Ah?” The vice creed leader was not keeping up.

The creed leader was disappointed with the vice creed leader as he explained, “What ah? If Fang Hao could sneak into the trials, it means that the righteous path already knows about the Huangyue Branch’s location. Shouldn’t they be packing up and fleeing right away?”

“Then what about Fang Hao?”

“We can’t kill him. The righteous path definitely has Fang Hao’s soul lamp. Once Fang Hao is killed, the righteous path would know that his identity as a spy has been exposed, and they would all then charge right toward the Huangyue Branch without a second thought. How would they have the time to escape then?”

“Oh.”

Chapter 74: The Ultimate Technique of Animal Form Fist

“This is a little tricky.” Lu Yang clicked his tongue, finding something to be amiss.

The other people from the Yanjiang Branch had already left in a hurry to commit evil deeds, leaving behind only the three of them. If the three of them were to act without restraint, they could even turn the entire flying immortal city upside down. However, their inherent nature didn’t allow them to do so. They were here to infiltrate the diabolic creed, and they were surrounded by many real diabolic cultivators.

“No wonder I’ve never heard of anyone infiltrating the Everlasting Creed as spies. Turns out it’s because there is such a test.” Meng Jingzhou also found the situation to be very sticky.

“What’s the worst bad thing you guys want to do?” Lu Yang asked.

After pondering for a long while, Meng Jingzhou replied uncertainly, “Does going to a brothel count?”

Since he was young, his clan had forbidden him from going to places like brothels. His uncles who had visited the brothels all told him that brothels were terrifying places that were not meant for children.

When Meng Jingzhou saw the wretched state of these uncles kneeling on washboards after going back home, he believed that brothels were indeed terrifying places.

As I now have a Single’s...oh wait, Pure Yang Spirit Root, all the more I can’t go.

To Meng Jingzhou, a rebellious act like visiting a brothel was the worst bad thing.

Man Gu simply couldn’t think of one.

“Never mind, we still have one whole day. Let’s go to the brothel to relax first then,” Lu Yang proposed. You must be kidding! I already have an idea. Do you expect rules like this to restrict me?

Since there is still time, we don’t have to do it now. This opportunity is hard to come by, so we might as well satisfy Meng Jingzhou’s wish first.

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. That’s right! We’re not in our true bodies here. Going just once won’t hurt.

“Come on, let’s go, let’s go,” Meng Jingzhou urged, dragging the other two along with him.

Going to places like this alone makes me guilty.

The brothel was in a conspicuous place, and the trio located it easily.

Ravishingly dressed women stood at the entrance waving their handkerchiefs to attract customers. Whenever they beckoned with their petite hands, the souls of passers-by were easily sucked in.

Upon arriving at the brothel’s entrance, Man Gu started to have thoughts of backing out and staggered a few steps back. “I’m a scholar. This isn’t a place a scholar should go to. The sages said that ‘beautiful women are skeletons, femme fatale are bones’—no matter how gorgeous a woman is, she will eventually turn into nothing but a pile of white bones. I mustn’t do the wrong thing.”

The other two exhausted their saliva in persuading Man Gu but to no avail, so they could only give up.

Lu Yang decided to be loyal to his friends. “Since you’re not willing to go to the brothel, I’ll go on your behalf.”

Man Gu heaved a sigh of relief. Brother Lu is still the most reliable.

Then, he saw Lu Yang unleash a set of Animal Form Fist and turn into Man Gu’s appearance right before his very eyes.

Man Gu was screaming inside his heart.

Lu Yang patted the dazed Man Gu reassuringly, “I’m going now.”

Man Gu hastily grabbed his “other self.” “You can’t go! Even if you go, you can’t be using my appearance!”

“I’m being kind to go in your stead. It’s such a pity that you’re not going.” Lu Yang’s tone sounded very heartfelt.

Man Gu was steadfast in refusing him.

“Don’t be shy,” Lu Yang encouraged.

In reality, Lu Yang was also very nervous. I’ve never visited a place like this before. What if I mess up? Wouldn’t Meng Jingzhou laugh at me for the rest of my life?

If I turn into Man Gu, even if something embarrassing happens, I won’t be the embarrassed one.

But I definitely cannot say something like that out loud.

While the three of them were about to squabble, they heard a rumbling sound from the brothel, followed by a woman’s high-pitched screech and a man’s savage laughter.

The trio immediately turned around, noticing dozens of cultivators ravaging the brothel wantonly. In their arms were innocent women they had seized. These cultivators didn’t even bother with concealing their cultivation. They were all at the Foundation Establishment Stage, with two or three of them having aura waves that were no weaker than the tiger demon’s!

These were all cultivators who were participating in the trials.

“Bastards!” Flames of wrath burned in the trio’s hearts, and they wanted to stop these people.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were just about to intervene when Lu Yang stopped them.

“Let’s not be reckless. There are only the three of us here. We can’t possibly defeat them.”

“What should we do then?” Meng Jingzhou asked anxiously.

Lu Yang waved his hand. “I have a way to temporarily boost my combat power. You two wait for me.”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were curious. We don’t have any Ten-Buffalo Strength Pills on us. Could Lu Yang have learned a secret spell that temporarily elevates his cultivation?

That was when they saw Lu Yang taking a deep breath. His movements became more gentle, his animated gaze turned cold, his face became devoid of expression, and his aura turned aloof and icy.

Meng Jingzhou narrowed his eyes, then widened his eyes.

These movements almost look like they belong to Big Senior Sister Yun Zhi!

Lu Yang was using the Lu-Style Animal Form Fist to transform into Yun Zhi.

He had previously joked that there were nine layers to his Lu-Style Animal Form Fist. When one reached the ninth layer, they could turn into a Transcendent Tribulation expert with a single thought. The reason for saying so was because he had discovered that when he turned into Man Gu, his physical body became stronger than his own.

It dawned upon him that the Lu-Style Animal Form Fist could allow him to obtain part of the transformation subject’s power! There were certainly limits to such power; one couldn’t become stronger infinitely. However, this was already formidable.

Lu Yang wanted to turn into Yun Zhi and see how much power he could gain and whether he could defeat these people!

Sorry, Big Senior Sister.

A breathtakingly beautiful woman appeared. Her gaze was vivid and radiant, and an eternal frost lingered between her brows.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu subconsciously held their breath at the sight of this beautiful woman, their legs trembling.

Lu Yang has successfully transformed into Big Senior Sister!

Lu Yang felt a surge of powerful energy descend from above and gush into his body!

~~~

At the Dao-Seeking Sect on Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi was sitting cross-legged at the summit. She was gazing up at the sky, as if she could see the boundless sea of stars beyond. She had restrained her aura to an extreme to the point that anyone who saw her would think that she was a mortal. However, a mortal wouldn’t be hovering atop a mountain peak, and neither would their eyes be filled with a galaxy of stars.

“Hmm? Who borrowed my power?” Yun Zhi withdrew her gaze as she detected that a sliver of her power had been separated and flown into the distance. “Let’s see who has such guts!” I’ve never encountered such an audacious thief before!

Removing her mortal state, aura waves exuded from her like fierce war halberds piercing through the clouds, her demeanor as the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Big Senior Sister on full display! Her soul left her body, transforming into a streak of light that followed the sliver of power that had split off from her body.

~~~

“Cough!” Lu Yang couldn’t withstand even a fraction of Yun Zhi’s power and reverted to his original form.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu also breathed a sigh of relief. The pressure of Lu Yang in Yun Zhi’s form was too overwhelming.

Crack! A crisp sound came from above.

Be it the rogue diabolic cultivators who were wreaking havoc and committing all kinds of atrocities or the heroic trio who were preparing to stand up for justice, everyone froze, staring upward with their eyes wide and mouths agape.

A crack had appeared in the infinitely large space, as if something had bumped into it.

Creak, creak, creak...

The crack was like a dried river bed that kept splitting larger. Crash! It was as if a gaping hole had formed in the firmament.

A dazzling figure appeared at the opening, her brows slightly furrowed.

“This aura...a diabolic creed?”

Chapter 75: Flee For One’s Life!

At the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, a bronze ancient cauldron was flowing with white mist. The consciousness of the rogue diabolic cultivators were right inside this cauldron. As the Immortal Eye opened, it projected a light screen that displayed the rankings.

The creed leader and vice creed leader were paying attention to the top few performers.

“Look, this person from Kunlun City is not bad. He would chant the Rebirth Requiem before killing. That’s quite the ritual. I heard that he was once a monk at a temple. He was of the notion that killing was a means to enlightenment and secretly killed many people. When the abbot found out, he wanted to flog him to death with the plank. Having exposed himself, this person smashed a Buddha statue and escaped in advance. He came to our Everlasting Creed because he wanted to see if the Everlasting Immortal would support his notion.”

“That little fellow from Quhe Commandery is also one with ideas. He likes to have family members killing one another. He controlled the child to kill the father and the grandson to kill his grandfather. After they died, he would turn them into puppets.”

“Oh, this one is interesting. He smashed a load-bearing wall, causing the building to collapse and crush many people to death.”

The two fervently commented on the cultivators in the top few positions. To have achieved such results, they were surely ruthless individuals, and they had a high probability of being promoted to the upper ranks in the future.

“What about those three outstanding young fellows from the first two rounds?”

The two people scrolled through the screen for a long time before finding their names, finding out that the trio was discussing whether to visit a brothel.

The vice creed leader was very displeased with their low ranking. “They’re ranked so far behind. Could they be spies from the righteous path and don’t know how to commit evil deeds?”

The creed leader shook his head with experience. “You shouldn’t think of it in that way. From what I have seen, this Lu Yang is someone with many ideas. He probably has a big plan to suddenly amaze everyone with one feat. You must understand that committing evil deeds doesn’t necessarily have to be about making haste in the present; planning for the long-term is the far superior option.”

Without much progress from Lu Yang’s side, they switched the screen back to the top to check in on what evil things the person in first place had done.

“The first place uses poison. He poisoned the well, killing the entire street. He also poisoned the cows so that they would go mad on the streets, trampling many people to death. Excellent, this is how poison should be used.

“What strange method is this? Acquiring numerous shops then firing all the staff?

“The one below is similar to him. After purchasing the shops, they forced the employees to work overtime without pay? Does this also count as an evil deed?”

The vice creed leader felt that he wasn’t keeping up with the times.

Suddenly, an incredibly powerful soul descended from the sky, breaking through the various arrays set up in the headquarters and dashing straight toward the bronze ancient cauldron shrouded in primal chaos aura waves!

The bronze ancient cauldron seemed to be unable to withstand such a forceful impact, and a tiny crack appeared on its surface!

“Oh no, my cauldron!” the creed leader cried out.

The bronze ancient cauldron was named the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron. It was capable of containing all things. He had devoted half of his life to refining his life-bound magical treasure, and it was only a fine line away from becoming an immortal treasure!

“An expert from the righteous path has discovered this place!” The creed leader was in disbelief.

What on earth happened? Why did a righteous expert find us in the blink of an eye?!

“This aura wave...it’s Yun Zhi from the Dao-Seeking Sect?!” Sensing familiar aura waves, a chill ran down the creed leader’s spine as he recalled some terrifying past events.

A fierce expression clouded the vice creed leader’s face as he took out his weapon, preparing to kill whoever it was. “Yun Zhi? Isn’t she just a disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect? In any case, it’s only one person. We just have to gather everyone and attack her together. Can’t we take her down then?”

As Yun Zhi rarely acted, she wasn’t very well-known across the Central Continent. The Dao-Seeking Sect’s sect leader, eight elders, and even Dai Bufan were more famous than her. However, having a low profile didn’t signify that she was weak. Anyone who had seen her in action would have their understanding of cultivation completely overturned!

The creed leader happened to have the chance to witness Yun Zhi in action. She plucked the stars, grabbed the moon, reversed yin and yang, and casually suppressed strong foes. I really feel that my three thousand years of cultivation has been for naught, all transferred to a dog.

The creed leader sent the vice creed leader tumbling across the ground with a kick. Is this the time to be fighting with your lives?

“That’s because you haven’t seen her in action. You don’t know how scary she is. Listen to me, run now! If you’re too slow, even the Everlasting Immortal won’t be able to save you!”

He was able to become the Everlasting Creed’s creed leader not just because he was the most devout to the Everlasting Immortal and possessed the highest cultivation. The most important reason was his prudence. He knew when to fight with his life, when to flee for his life, and when to resign himself to his life.[1]

Going head-on with Yun Zhi is not fighting with our lives; it’s called resigning ourselves to our lives!

The creed leader cast ancient mysterious sigils on the Mountain and Rivers Cauldron one after another to prevent Yun Zhi from charging forth right away.

It was the vice creed leader’s first time seeing the creed leader lose his bearings like this. He also realized the gravity of the situation and transmitted an auditory message to all the other higher-ups, issuing a highest-priority order to immediately escape to the alternate headquarters.

Taking precautions against ambush from the righteous path, the Everlasting Creed had designed detailed procedures and escape routes, even going as far as to carry out multiple evacuation drills, so the higher-ups were very familiar with the steps.

In the blink of an eye, the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed seemed to have vanished into thin air.

Unleashing his mighty ability of Three Heads Six Arms, two of his hands cast sigils and continued strengthening the seals on the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron, while four of his hands returned the people’s consciousness in the cauldron to their original bodies.

The cracks on the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron were only increasing. The speed of sealing could not keep up with the rate at which cracks were forming.

Seeing that everyone had successfully escaped, the creed leader heaved a sigh of relief and severed his connection to the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron. He vomited a mouthful of essence blood, a backlash from his life-bound magical treasure. His aura waves subsided rapidly, and his face became as pallid as paper.

However, there was no time for him to bother. He turned around and immediately fled!

Boom!

The Mountains and Rivers Cauldron shattered, its explosion causing the entire headquarters to shake violently.

Yun Zhi walked out from the cauldron expressionlessly, just like a martial goddess from the legends, sacred and inviolable. She bent down, the tips of her fingers brushing the essence blood left behind by the creed leader. With a snap of her finger, she had made a divination, coldness glinting in her eyes.

“In that direction.”

A blazing white light gathered in her hand, like brilliant heavenly lightning that eradicated all evil.

The white heavenly lightning shot toward the creed leader. He hadn’t expected that Yun Zhi could still locate him in spite of all he had done. He wanted to dodge, but it was too late. Blood burst forth from his shoulder.

“Cicada Sheds Its Carapace!” The creed leader had multiple life-saving tricks.

By the time Yun Zhi caught up, she was left with only a remnant body.

~~~

The creed leader staggered back to the alternate headquarters. He stuffed life-extending pills into his mouth as if they didn’t cost anything. After forcefully cutting off the connection with the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron and using the secret spell of Cicada Sheds Its Carapace, it would take at least several hundred years of peaceful cultivation for him to recover.

That’s still manageable. The biggest blow is the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron! That was a precious cauldron forged with the power of the whole creed, and the amount of treasures it expended can match the Great Xia Dynasty’s ten years of tax revenue!

Yet this priceless treasure has fallen into the hands of the Dao-Seeking Sect just like that!

“How are you feeling?” the vice creed leader asked in concern. Having just seen Yun Zhi in action, he was still overwhelmed with fear. If it were me, my body would have long turned cold. It’s only because of how capable the creed leader is that he’s still alive.

“I won’t die.” The creed leader was still shaken. “Fortunately, we had prepared contingency plans and prepared a hiding place in advance. By disconnecting the causal relationship, Yun Zhi wouldn’t be able to find us. Otherwise, the Four Great Diabolic Creeds would have to become the Three Great Diabolic Creeds.

“Since the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron has shattered, we’ll just end the third trial here. Let’s see who’s currently in first place.”

The Immortal Eye projected a light screen, a name prominently displayed at the top.

First Place: Lu Yang.

“Hmm?”

1. There's supposed to be wordplay done by the author here. I tried to translate it too, but here's an explanation just in case it's not done well. The first expression means putting everything on the line and fighting desperately with all they have, while the last expression means resigning themselves to their fate. ☜

Chapter 76: Evaluation

“Who on earth borrowed my power?” Yun Zhi was perplexed. Every single person from the Everlasting Creed had fled, only leaving behind the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron that could purchase an entire first-class sect.

Now I can’t find who the culprit was.

There was a type of spell called the Divine Descent Technique that allowed one to borrow another’s power with their permission. However, the spell was not only extremely challenging to master, but it was also on the verge of being lost through the generations. It had been a long time since Yun Zhi had seen such spells.

Besides, who can borrow my power without my permission? Yun Zhi had sensed no malicious intentions from the other party, which was why she instinctively didn’t hinder her power from flowing out.

I can roughly guess who it was.

“But where did he learn the Divine Descent Technique?” Yun Zhi didn’t recall teaching Lu Yang such spells.

~~~

First Place: Lu Yang

“Hmm? Someone else has taken first place?” The vice creed leader was bewildered.

As they were busy fleeing for their lives, they didn’t have a chance to pay attention to what Lu Yang had done. Since the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron was also shattered, they couldn’t watch the playback.

“The Immortal Eye never makes mistakes. These three people must have caused the most destruction!” asserted the creed leader despite also being unable to guess what Lu Yang had done.

The previous first-place had killed several hundreds of people in a short time and brought deleterious impacts to the lives of several thousands more. Yet Lu Yang could surpass this person in such a short time! That’s unbelievably remarkable!

There’s no need for me to speculate either. The Immortal Eye is an immortal’s precious treasure and of a higher tier than the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron; it definitely won’t go wrong.

Indeed, as Lu Yang had summoned Yun Zhi over, which led to the destruction of the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron and the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, the destruction he brought to the creed could go down as one of the top three in history.

Just the amount of damage he inflicted upon the creed leader alone could earn him the first position.

The creed leader was so proud that he forgot the pain he felt. “See, I told you so. This Lu Yang possesses great wisdom. Even if he was lagging behind, when you're not paying attention, he can pull a big move any moment. Look, he's now risen to first place.

“Don't be fooled by the average performance of Meng Jingzhou and the Man Gu you favor. That's because they didn't have time. With enough time, I guarantee they'll make it to second and third.”

The vice creed leader admitted his defeat graciously. As expected of the creed leader! Not only is he prudent, he also has a sharp eye. No wonder I'm only a vice creed leader while he's the legitimate creed leader.

“What's your evaluation of Lu Yang?”

After contemplating for a bit, the creed leader slowly said, “In the first round, Lu Yang went for an unconventional gambit, revealing his talent in martial Dao and a rare display of entering the Dao through martial arts. In the second round, with attentive observation, he inferred a pattern and leveraged it to buy the potatoes, preventing those behind him from taking part in the trial. This is evidence of how destructive he is, and it is especially prominent in the third round. It's not an exaggeration to call him an Innate Diabolic Spawn.

The vice creed leader was astonished. I've known the creed leader for so long, but I've never heard him give someone such a high appraisal.

“What about Meng Jingzhou?”

“In the first round, he obtained powers after getting bitten by the spider, a manifestation of his good fortune. He is probably a Dao Spawn whose birth was ordained by the heavens. In the second round, he meticulously studied the question and analyzed it from multiple angles. He might have seemed arrogant and domineering, but in fact, every step was calculated. With his strategy, he eventually broke through the examiner’s psychological defense and successfully passed. Unfortunately, he didn't have the chance to showcase his strengths in the third round before it ended, falling slightly short of Lu Yang. I suppose he can be considered a Descended Dao Diabolic.”

The assessment “Descended Dao Diabolic” was also extremely hard to come by. Hardly anyone in the younger generation had attained such high praise from the creed leader. Looks like this Meng Jingzhou has a bright future ahead of him.

“What about Man Gu?”

“In the first round, he possessed abilities to comprehend, persevere, and strategize. In the second round, he was thorough in thinking through the question. It's just that he didn't have much of an opinion in the third round. In the past trials, his performance would be considered stellar, but unfortunately, when comparing him to the illustrious pearls in front of him, I can only rate him as Diabolism in Heart.”

Diabolism in Heart... judging based on past experience, as long as they didn't meet their demise, they could all join the upper ranks of the Everlasting Creed.

“Shall we transfer them to the headquarters to groom them?” the vice creed leader asked.

The creed leader shook his head, tapping on his experience as he explained, “No rush, they can start from the bottom so that they minimally have two years of foundational experience. Trust me, experience at the grassroots level will be beneficial for them in the long run. This was how I made my way up.

“Furthermore, I have another plan. Lu Yang is imaginative and uninhibited while possessing much destructive force. When he matures, let’s see if he can infiltrate a righteous sect like the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

The vice creed leader couldn’t stop himself from laughing. The creed leader thinks too highly of them. If we’re talking about other righteous sects, there’s still a chance, but the Dao-Seeking Sect is too enormous of a challenge. Just keeping up with their disciples’ line of thought alone is already a hurdle for almost anyone. Assuming they really infiltrate the sect, it won’t be long before they get exposed for not fitting in.

Infiltrating the Dao-Seeking Sect is easier said than done.

“I’ll go tend to my wounds first.” The sect leader went to a secret chamber to go into seclusion and recuperate.

Up until now, the vice creed leader had never harbored thoughts of usurping power. Today was a prime example of that. Although killing the creed leader can let me move one step up, what comes after that? What if the righteous path attacks us again? Can I make the right decisions then?

As soon as I make a wrong judgment, I’ll definitely die under the righteous path’s attacks. It’ll be too late to regret usurping power then.

~~~

At the Yanjiang Branch, the branch leader had just received word from a messenger sent by the creed leader. “A total of ten people passed the trials, and three of them received the evaluations of Innate Diabolic Spawn, Descended Dao Diabolic, and Diabolism in Heart?!” The branch leader was over the moon, his eyebrows raising in joy. The results are even better than I had expected! My opportunity at promotion is right before my eyes!

As for the rogue diabolic cultivators who didn’t pass the first and second rounds, the eleven administrators would split up to dump them at various places while they were still unconscious. After they wake up, they would forget the location of the Yanjiang Branch and think that everything was just a dream.

The most foolproof method was to kill them to ensure that they wouldn’t leak the location of the Yanjiang Branch. However, for the sake of the greater picture, the Everlasting Creed didn’t do so. With these rogue diabolic cultivators wreaking havoc in their respective territories, they could draw the attention of the righteous path. Amid the chaos, the righteous path wouldn’t be able to distinguish which acts were committed by rogue diabolic cultivators and which were by the diabolic creeds, thereby achieving the effect of confusing the righteous path.

Lu Yang and the other two slowly woke up, their minds muddled after the many events that had just transpired.

What did I see before passing out... Big Senior Sister descending from the sky?!

Lu Yang broke into cold sweat. Big Senior Sister didn’t see me transforming into her, right? If she did, she’s surely going to skin me.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu also recalled what happened. Lu Yang’s Animal Form Fist had summoned the real Big Senior Sister.

Lu Yang’s gaze warned the two of them to keep it a secret, and the two tactfully nodded.

The branch leader suppressed the delight in their heart and tried their best to speak in a neutral tone, “From today onward, the ten of you will be a part of the Everlasting Creed.

“Usually, we should first go through with an initiation ceremony, but the three rounds of trials today have already exhausted everyone, myself included. Visiting the Everlasting Immortal in such a state would be disrespectful. We will assemble here again tomorrow and officially hold the initiation ceremony.”

Lu Yang could discern that when the Everlasting Immortal was mentioned, the branch leader’s tone as well as the expressions of the eleven administrators would change. This means that they truly believe in the Everlasting Immortal’s existence.

No wonder they call themselves a creed.

He then heard the branch leader say, “However, since there are new members joining us today, it also wouldn’t be right to not celebrate. I’ll tell you what, let’s go out and have a meal. I heard that a new barbeque shop has opened in the commandery. It’s called ‘One More Time.’ The taste is pretty good, and it has many positive reviews. We’ll gather there in a short while; my treat.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Man Gu, “...”

Not letting us rest, huh?

Chapter 77: Where’s the Shop Owner? Come Out!

“I’m so exhausted, I don’t feel like doing anything at all.” The trio was yawning, their eyelids struggling to keep open.

Why did the branch leader have to propose this rotten idea to come here and eat?

They were currently on their way to the barbeque shop. After one whole day of battling with wits and valor, they had finally infiltrated the enemy. All they wanted to do now was dig into a hearty meal and enjoy their beauty sleep.

As the Everlasting Creed had congregated everyone’s consciousness inside the Mountains and Rivers Cauldron, it would result in significant fatigue.

“Fortunately, I had the tiger-henchman ghosts prepare the skewers beforehand. We can open the shop right away.” Man Gu felt glad.

Upon arriving at the entrance of the barbeque shop, Lu Yang noticed a familiar person.

“Captain Wei? What are you doing here? Is anything the matter?”
