Captain Wei had knocked on the barbeque shop’s door for a while but to no avail, to which he thought there was not a person inside.

He was right—there was not a person inside but rather two tiger-henchman ghosts that were busy skewering. When they heard the knocking, they were almost frightened to death and didn’t dare to open the door.

Just as Captain Wei was about to give up, Lu Yang and his gang arrived.

Captain Wei’s eyebrows arched upward in joy. “Manager Lu, all of you are finally back.”

Lu Yang nodded, casually spouting some lies, “I saw that the weather was not bad this morning, so the three of us decided that it was a good day for an outing. We just got back.”

“Are you still opening for business today then?”

Lu Yang pondered for a bit. The branch leader and the rest are coming, making that around twenty people. That should count as opening. “Yes, we’re opening.”

Constable Captain Wei spoke in his gentlest tone possible, “Manager Lu, here’s the thing. Your barbeque shop is quite famous around the area, so I often bring a few brothers along to eat here. I know that you only enjoy running the barbeque shop and have no intentions of expanding or having others advertise for you.”

Lu Yang nodded.

Captain Wei continued in a remorseful manner, “That few brothers of mine aren’t good at keeping their mouths shut. After eating, they went back and raved about how delicious the food here was. Naturally, the others also began drooling, and they agreed that they’ll come here to have a meal together after their shift today. The brothers on the night shift in the yamen even asked us to bring some food back after we’re done eating.”

Judging by Captain Wei’s expression, his brothers are probably not the only ones who did that. You spread the word too, didn’t you?

“So?”

“There are quite a few constables in Yanjiang Commandery. We could probably take up all your tables. The chief constable is also coming, so I was wondering if we could book the entire place tonight.”

Understanding his intentions, Lu Yang soon showed a troubled expression. “But I also have a few good friends coming over tonight, I’m afraid...”

Captain Wei hurriedly said, “That’s not a problem at all! A few people won’t make much of a difference. All of us can eat together. It’ll also be livelier with more people.” Before coming, he had slapped his chest confidently and promised his colleagues that they would be able to get a meal today. If they don’t, that would be a slap to my face.

Lu Yang agreed, “Alright then. We’ll get things ready and open in an hour.”

Hearing an affirmative answer from the other party, Captain Wei was pleased as he left.

~~~

When it was almost time for the meetup arranged by the branch leader, people from various directions gathered in front of the barbeque shop. They included the branch leader, eleven administrators, and seven new members.

Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi were even thoughtful enough to be carrying a few jars of wine. ”We’re afraid that the liquor provided by a small shop like this wouldn’t be strong enough, so we specially brought a few jars of thirty-year-old spirit wine, Nü’er Hong.”[1]

This type of spirit wine was extremely strong; even a Foundation Establishment cultivator couldn’t neutralize its effects.

The other five new members also had the idea of presenting wine out of respect, but they were all at the Qi Training Stage and unable to offer anything decent.

For the sake of the meal, the branch leader had even changed his mask into one that had the lower half exposed.

Lu Yang and the other two walked out of the barbeque shop and invited everyone in. “Come on in, everything’s ready! The place was originally booked for the night, but after much persuasion, we managed to convince the other party to leave us one table.”

The branch leader nodded. He was originally worried that the trio would be a problematic bunch to deal with and refuse to listen to orders, so he had hoped to show off his authority and put them in their place. Now it looks like these three are on the ball. They know how to reserve a table in advance.

“Don’t just stand there, let’s head inside,” the branch leader beckoned everyone.

As the barbeque shop was empty, the branch leader very naturally sat at the table in the center. This table is the largest and has the best position—fitting for my position.

Lu Yang softly reminded him, “Branch Leader, this table has been reserved.”

Before the branch leader could say anything, Chi Xulong cut in, “Get them to move to the side! Who do they think they are? They dare to snatch our seats?”

Seeing no objection from the branch leader, he said nothing more.

After everyone sat down, Man Gu took out the menu. “What shall we eat?”

Shen Jinyi passed the menu to the branch leader. “Branch Leader, please choose.”

The branch leader waved his hand. “Order whatever you like.”

“You are treating, so it’s only right that you choose.”

“No need, just order whatever.”

They went back and forth until the menu ended up back in Man Gu’s hands. His mouth twitched. This bunch of people sure are troublesome. They have to dilly-dally even with just ordering skewers.

Man Gu didn’t have the habit of declining out of respect. After he finished ordering, he took the menu to the backyard and instructed the two tiger-henchman ghosts to start the grill.

Not long after, Man Gu carried plates of mouthwatering barbeque skewers. The aroma alone was enough for everyone to know that it wouldn’t disappoint.

“Come come come, the skewers are here! Pour the wine!” The branch leader smiled, signaling for everyone to pour some wine.

Meng Jingzhou said with a smile, “I’ll do without wine. I don’t like it and I’m used to drinking tea."

The branch leader chuckled. “Little Meng, how can you not drink when roaming the jianghu? There will be plenty of occasions in the future where you have to drink. Get used to it by drinking three cups first.”

Meng Jingzhou still refused.

The branch leader felt that it was an affront to his authority, and his brow slightly knitted.

Chi Xulong took the chance to berate, “What’s wrong with you? The branch leader told you to drink and you reject it? Are you trying to disrespect the branch leader’s authority?”

Meng Jingzhou’s mouth twitched. “It’s just drinking wine. How did you link that with respect? Does that mean that if the branch leader insists that I drink, he’s not giving me respect?”

Chi Xulong just wanted to retort with “Look at yourself in the mirror, who are you to talk about respect in front of the branch leader?” Before he could voice it out loud, the branch leader stopped him.

The branch leader knew that Meng Jingzhou had a bright future ahead of him and didn’t want to start a conflict with him. Only the branch leader was aware of the creed leader’s evaluation of the trio.

“There’s no need to be so particular during our welcoming meal. I’ll introduce myself first. My surname is Chu, you can call me Branch Leader Chu.”

The next person after the branch leader was the tall, lanky man who had gone to the brothel with Qin Yuanhao. “I’m Wang He. Those familiar with me like to call me Big Mouth Wang.”

“Bai Zifang.”

“Peng Shuo.”

One by one, the eleven administrators introduced themselves, but calling it an introduction might not be apt as they were simply reporting their names, cultivation, hobbies, and nothing else of note.

Trust was rare within diabolic creeds. One would conceal information about themselves where possible.

It was a harmonious sight as everyone enjoyed their meals, as if a dispute hadn’t occurred.

“These skewers taste really good.” Chi Xulong was extremely surprised after eating a few skewers. These are the best barbeque skewers I’ve ever eaten.

Greed grew in his heart, and he quietly asked the branch leader, “Should we force the shop owner to hand over the recipe? Even if we price these barbeque skewers with spirit stones, there will still be a market for it. We could make a fortune!”

The branch leader was tempted. I’ve killed, robbed, scammed, and extorted people many times before. One more doesn’t make a difference.

Lu Yang asked by the side, “What if the shop owner doesn’t hand over the recipe?”

Coldness gleamed in Chi Xulong’s eyes as he smiled sinisterly. “Then let’s see if he wants to keep his life or the recipe!” He slammed the table, ready to cause trouble as he yelled angrily, “Where’s the shop owner? Come out! The skewers are already all served, yet you still haven’t shown your face. Don’t you know the rules?!”

Right afterward, Captain Wei’s voice could be heard from outside. “Haha, where’s the shop owner? I’ve brought my brothers here.”

A swarm of constables streamed in, including the chief constable who was at the Golden Core Stage, surrounding the table the branch leader and the rest were at.

1. A traditional Chinese wine from Shaoxing, Zhejiang. It is also common in wuxia and xianxia novels. ☜

Chapter 78: Righteous and Diabolic Paths as One Family

The constables spread themselves out and sat down. Captain Wei wasn’t exaggerating when he claimed that they could take up all their tables.

With the branch leader’s table in the center surrounded by constables, it was a scene of harmony, the righteous and diabolic paths coming together as “one family.”

Chi Xulong was so terrified that he hastily lowered his head. One shouldn’t be fooled by the rumors of his arrogance; that was just an image he built for himself. Whenever he did something bad, he would either be in disguise or cover his face. If he encountered someone from the authorities, he would hide away as far as possible.

Now that he had nowhere to hide, he could only lower his head and pretend to be an ostrich.

“Captain Wei, I’m here.” Lu Yang smilingly stood up and greeted Captain Wei.

Chi Xulong widened his eyes as he stared at Lu Yang in disbelief. So you are the shop owner!

“You've already started eating.” Captain Wei was a bit embarrassed.

“It’s fine. What would all of you like to eat?”

Captain Wei waved his hand. “There’s too many people here to be ordering. Just serve whatever you have.”

“Alright,” Lu Yang agreed, already guessing Captain Wei’s response beforehand.

As the constables sniffed in the delectable aroma from the branch leader’s table, they subconsciously swallowed their saliva. It was mealtime now, and they were already hungry, so the fragrance only made them hungrier.

Fortunately, Lu Yang had made preparations in advance, getting the tiger-henchman ghosts to work at full steam before the constables came. They would grill some of the portions first so that food could be served once the constables arrived.

Soon, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu brought out plates of skewers to let the constables fill their stomachs for the time being.

Despite not voicing it out, Captain Wei was very grateful to Lu Yang for saving him from the complaints of his colleagues.

“Let me introduce to you, this is our chief constable, Fang Qingyun!”

Fang Qingyun politely shook hands with Lu Yang. As a Golden Core cultivator himself, he could discern that Lu Yang was a fellow cultivator. And not just Lu Yang. He could also tell that the branch leader’s table was made up of only cultivators.

He made no comment since plenty of cultivators ran businesses. As long as they don’t break the law, what does that have to do with me? It’s not like running a barbeque shop is illegal.

So what if the table is occupied? As chief constable, I can’t abuse my authority to bully others. That wouldn’t be good for my reputation if rumors get out.

After Lu Yang sat down with a smile, Chi Xulong cursed silently before complaining so that the branch leader could hear him. “You bastard, you have ill intentions! Why didn’t you tell us earlier that the constables are coming?!”

Lu Yang pretended to feel wronged. “That’s because I want to let all of you build a good relationship with the constables. You should grab hold of this opportunity.” Lu Yang pointed at the silk banner on the wall. “Do you see that? Captain Wei gave me that silk banner.”

He randomly made something up. “Before I joined the creed, I had specially found a base beforehand so that I could lay the foundation to establish connections with the authorities. That way, no matter what I do, the authorities won’t suspect me. When they come here to drink, I can even eavesdrop on their intel.”

The branch leader nodded. What Lu Yang said makes a lot of sense. He is worthy of the creed leader’s appraisal. The creed leader had mentioned that although these three may seem to be messing around wilfully, there’s actually a deeper layer to their actions. We can’t judge them just by what we see on the surface.

Just based on how they have proactively built connections with the authorities, the courage and ideas they’ve showcased have already surpassed most of the people within the creed!

“Come, drink.”

After eating a few skewers to temporarily satiate their hunger, the constables began to drink. As they consumed more and more skewers, the constables drank to their hearts’ content. They drank round after round and exchanged toasts, a lively atmosphere to behold.

In stark contrast to the buzz in the surroundings, those at the branch leader’s table in the center were drinking very cautiously, afraid that they might spill some secrets by accident if they had too much to drink.

Toward the end, they even stopped drinking wine altogether and switched to tea instead.

Captain Wei noticed that the branch leader’s table was lacking a lively mood, and he felt that his presence might have been the culprit. Feeling guilty inside, he picked up his wine cup and walked over.

“Come come come, don’t mind us. We’re just ordinary people when we’re off duty. We should be eating and drinking happily when we’re at a barbeque shop!!

“Come on, let’s have a drink!” Captain Wei called out to Chi Xulong.

Chi Xulong gingerly lifted his teacup. Captain Wei was displeased, his face stern. “What’s with drinking tea? Are you not giving me respect? Pour wine!”

Chi Xulong had no choice but to brace himself to down the thirty-year-old spirit wine he brought along.

Captain Wei was spinning in circles as he drank, while the other constables were clearly drunk. They followed him and started to drink at the branch leader’s table, enjoying themselves to the fullest.

No one looked for Lu Yang and the other two to drink. There was a tacit consensus that they shouldn’t be getting the boss of the shop drunk.

The strength of a thirty-year-old spirit wine was not something a Foundation Establishment cultivator could tolerate. Chi Xulong and the others ended up intoxicated. Seeing that they already had their fill, the branch leader found an excuse to leave.

With their boss gone, under the influence of alcohol, the people gradually became less restrained. Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi put their arms over each other, determined to unite and make a name for themselves in the Everlasting Creed.

“Chi Xulong, the biggest weakness you have is that you’re too impatient and flamboyant. You should tone it down a little!” Shen Jinyi advised Chi Xulong.

However, Chi Xulong was not happy to hear that. He was a free soul and wasn’t willing to accept criticism. “Oh, please. You’re saying that I’m flamboyant? Then should I be a coward like you? Someone who doesn’t dare act by themselves and teach a bunch of students to do the work for them? You’re always hiding behind others like a girl!”

Shen Jinyi flared up. “Chi Xulong, don’t mistake my kindness for weakness! I’m looking out for you, yet you tried to bite me back?”

Chi Xulong was even more irate. “Who are you calling a dog?!”

He sent a punch right into Shen Jinyi’s face.

How could Shen Jinyi take something like this lying down? If I swallow my anger now, based on Chi Xulong’s character, he’ll definitely push his luck further. He picked up his wine cup and splashed it at Chi Xulong. Although the latter was drunk, his reflexes were still nimble enough to dodge. The wine ended up splashing onto Bai Zifang, who was just watching the commotion from the side.

Bai Zifang was also not one to be trifled with. He was insistent on getting payback for being implicated in something he had no part in, so he splashed wine all over Shen Jinyi to give him a taste of his own medicine. That wasn’t enough. He even smashed a plate right into Shen Jinyi’s face.

The three of them became embroiled in a brawl. The others who tried to intervene were instead accidentally injured in the process, which fueled their anger.

I was kind enough to help you all avoid embarrassment, yet this is how you repay me? It’s fine if you don’t appreciate it, but how dare you hit me?!

I was being too nice!

The spirit wine was so strong that it addled everyone’s mind. Without even caring that they were surrounded by constables, they launched an all-out fight.

Crash!

Someone had flipped a table, sending things flying to neighboring tables.

It was the constables’ first time encountering such brazen people and witnessing cultivators in a public brawl.

Moreover, it was with the constables right at the side. If we aren’t around, who knows how much worse it could have been!

A public brawl among cultivators could inadvertently kill innocent bystanders. This is extremely evil and must be punished!

The chief constable, Fang Qingyun, released an oppressive pressure to suppress the diabolic creed members.

“Take them away. Let them sober up in prison!”

The creed members instantly became sober. Upon realizing what had happened, cold sweat streamed down their backs.

Too many people had come this time, overwhelming the two tiger-henchman ghosts who were so busy that they became fainter. Man Gu stepped in to personally help out. Lu Yang and Man Meng Jingzhou kept shuttling between the backyard and the main hall. The skewers they had prepared were decreasing at a rapid speed.

Lu Yang lifted the curtain and apologized, “I’m sorry, everyone, the skewers are all finished... What’s going on here?”

Lu Yang saw the arrogant and domineering diabolic creed members sitting obediently in the main hall while the constables watched them with mocking smiles.

Captain Wei whispered, “Sorry, Manager Lu, your friends were involved in a public brawl. The chief constable hates it the most when cultivators do something like this. The commotion they caused was so big that even passers-by outside had noticed. It wouldn’t be right to not punish them.”

Lu Yang didn’t know what to say to that. To be honest, I did have the intention of playing with them by arranging the creed members and constables to sit together. But I honestly didn’t expect this group of people to be so audacious as to fight right in front of constables.

Meng Jingzhou’s mouth twitched. “I told you, don’t drink wine. Nothing good ever comes from drinking.”

~~~

On the day of the welcome party, Chi Xulong and gang were detained for ten days for engaging in a public brawl.

When Branch Leader Chu learned of the news, it took him quite a while to register it.

Chapter 79: Everlasting Immortal

Fortunately for Chi Xulong and the others, they were crafty veterans who wouldn’t disclose the diabolic creed’s secrets just because they were locked up. Otherwise, Branch Leader Chu would have considered silencing them.

Branch Leader Chu sent word for Lu Yang and the other two to head to the Yanjiang Branch for their initiation ceremony.

As for those dim-witted bunch of fools, let them sit in prison for ten days first to cool off.

Branch Leader Chu was sitting lazily on a jade chair. Looking up at the three people standing in front of him, he complimented, “Your idea of opening a barbeque shop is a good one; keep it up. This is a channel for us to establish connections with the authorities.”

Branch Leader Chu dismissed the attendants. As they were entry-level members of the creed and hadn’t gone through trials, they weren’t qualified to be privy to the diabolic creed’s secrets.

“Let’s go, I’ll take you all to pay your respects to the Everlasting Immortal.”

Branch Leader Chu led them to another place with a floating stone. On it were buildings from an unknown era. Eroded by the tide of time, they had already collapsed. The ambient light made it look oppressive and stifling. Treading through the ruins gave a heavy feeling of walking through history.

Even the erudite Meng Jingzhou couldn’t discern which era the buildings had been constructed. They definitely don’t belong to these one hundred thousand years ruled by the Great Xia Dynasty! Meng Jingzhou was secretly stunned. Could they be from the Great Yu Dynasty?

Historical books recorded that the last emperor of the Great Yu Dynasty led a debauched lifestyle. The court fell into pieces and the world was plunged into chaos. That was when the Meng Family’s ancestor and the Great Xia Emperor’s ancestor rose in revolt and sought to vie for dominion over the Central Plains.

The Dao-Seeking was established 120,000 years ago during the Great Yu Dynasty, but that was at its peak, when its position was unshakable.

At the end of the buildings was a statue about four meters tall. It looked similar to the one in Qin Yuanhao’s house. Its face was blurred, and it was clad in long robes, making its gender indiscernible.

It was none other than the Everlasting Immortal.

Branch Leader Chu held up three lit incense sticks and bowed to the Everlasting Immortal. He turned to the trio and told them, “Sit in meditation for an hour to dispel any adulterated thoughts.”

The three incense sticks weren’t ordinary goods. After inhaling the scent, their restless hearts surprisingly calmed down.

Dispelling adulterated thoughts was basic for the three of them. Branch Leader Chu nodded slightly upon seeing how fast they settled their hearts.

Even with the help of the precious incense, their speed is still amazing. Most diabolic cultivators are impatient and irascible, cultivating just their bodies but not their hearts. These three are indeed hard to come by. They probably encountered a fortuitous opportunity somewhere before.

If it had been in the past, Branch Leader Chu would have stopped at nothing to get his hands on their fortuitous opportunity. However, these three people were different. They were of key interest to the creed leader. He didn’t have the courage to make a move.

An hour later, the three of them woke up and followed Branch Leader Chu’s instructions to pay their respects to the Everlasting Immortal. After completing the elaborate steps, the three of them were now officially followers of the Everlasting Creed.

Branch Leader Chu said with his hands behind his back, “Before joining our creed, you might have only known that we Everlasting Creed worship the Everlasting Immortal and that becoming followers could extend your lifespan. You probably know little about the Everlasting Immortal.”

The three nodded. They had no clue about the Everlasting Immortal; this was, in fact, the only immortal they had ever heard of.

Branch Leader Chu reverently went into detail, “The existence of the Everlasting Immortal is a taboo. He has lived through the ages alongside heaven and earth, witnessing the ups and downs of this world. Even if his physical body perishes, his immortal soul decays, and only a sliver of his spirit light lingers in the mundane world, as long as someone still remembers him, he can come back to life, everlasting for eternity!”

The trio’s hearts were thunderstruck. They didn’t know how much of what Branch Leader Chu had said was true.

As long as someone still remembers the Everlasting Immortal, he will be undying and imperishable? This has never appeared even in the legends! To have such divine wonders, he truly deserves the title of “immortal.”

Branch Leader Chu continued, “Having attained enlightenment and become an immortal in ancient times, he is cognizant of ancient secrets through the ages, and the power he possesses is far beyond what us plebeians can oppose.

“Now that the Great Era is upon us, the old monsters buried in the wilderness are crawling out of their coffins. If we want to survive in this Great Era, we can only resurrect the Everlasting Immortal to protect us!”

Lu Yang hesitated for a bit before asking, “So how are we resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal?”

“The Everlasting Immortal attained enlightenment through battles and became an immortal through slaughter, something he delights in. We have to stir up war in this world and please him through the death of millions. This is just the first step. The subsequent steps are not what someone at your position can have access to.”

“Millions of deaths?!” Meng Jingzhou was flabbergasted. How many lives would that be? You can’t even use “corpses strewn across the ground” to describe the carnage!

“Is that a lot? Not at all.” Branch Leader Chu shook his head. Most people would have similar reactions upon hearing this number, but after regaining their composure, they would change their minds. With how expansive and boundless the Central Continent was, millions of people might seem like a lot, but when they averaged it out, they would realize that it was just one death in every few thousand people.

“Do you know how many people die from exhaustion every year? How many people die from suicide after being driven to their wits’ end? How many people die from illnesses? How many people die due to medical treatment by quacks? How many unclaimed corpses does the Great Xia Dynasty discover every year?”

Branch Leader Chu sneered. “Do you know? Of course not! That’s because the Great Xia Dynasty doesn’t dare to announce the real numbers!

“If we don’t revive the Everlasting Immortal, who’s going to protect the vast Central Continent? When the old cultivation monsters awaken one after another, the death toll won’t be just this number of people.”

“Is the Ancient Great Era really so terrifying?” A chill seeped into the depths of Lu Yang’s heart.

Branch Leader Chu didn’t answer, simply signaling for the three to follow him. He went around the Everlasting Immortal’s statue and passed through an area of ruins, explaining as they walked, “These ruins date back to ancient times. Through the corrosion of time, they have crumbled and become dilapidated.

“Ten thousand years ago, the creed founder discovered this place by chance and learned of the Everlasting Immortal’s existence. The era of the Everlasting Immortal is so distant in the past that people have forgotten about the immortal who once protected the world. It was the creed founder who brought the Everlasting Immortal back into this world! The creed founder replicated the ruins and preserved them at the various bases. This is one of them. It has since been ten thousand years.”

Meng Jingzhou thought to himself, No wonder I couldn’t tell. Turns out it’s a replica of ancient ruins. Only legends from ancient times have been passed down to the present; very few things have survived until now.

Branch Leader Chu stopped at a stone wall. “It’s right here. This is the scene of a sacrificial ritual from ancient times.”

The first thing they took in from the stone wall was the Everlasting Immortal, who had his arms wide open. There were countless orbs of myriad sizes at his chest. Some of them even had ring-shaped objects around them, though their purpose remained unknown. Each orb had a small figure kneeling on it, holding up tributes to be offered to the Everlasting Immortal.

“What are these orbs? And why are the people standing on them?” Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were bewildered.

Lu Yang’s pupils dilated upon seeing the mural. These orbs resemble the celestial bodies from the previous era, and the ring-like objects should be meteor dust.

Branch Leader Chu slowly explained, “These are called planets. In ancient times, there was no Central Continent. All races lived on planets.

“At the end of the ancient era, an unfathomable existence refined all the planets into what is now the Central Continent!”

His words sent shock waves through the trio!

Chapter 80: Stars and Continent

Branch Leader Chu’s words stunned the three of them, especially Lu Yang, who began to draw many associations.

Back when I joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, they had given me a rough map of the sect, and it stated that the Dao-Seeking Sect spanned one million li. What's one million li? That's even larger than putting ten Earths together and unfurling them!

But then again, if I think of the Void Refinement and Fusion experts described in the books, it does seem reasonable. Only such an enormous place can allow them to unleash their wondrous abilities without restraint.

There are many forbidden areas in the sect, and most of them are used for battles between cultivation experts. Even going close to the periphery can be deadly for those with low cultivation.

When I joined the sect, Big Senior Sister had said ‘Everything about the sect can't be explained in a few sentences. You will gradually explore and find out in the future.’ It's not because she was too lazy to introduce the sect to me but because the Dao-Seeking is so huge that one needs to explore slowly.

Now that I think about it, the Dao-Seeking Sect could have been formed from planets! But the land it occupies is only a corner of the Central Continent. It's hard to imagine how vast the Central Continent actually is!

Branch Leader Chu continued, “In ancient times, stars with life existed in the tens of thousands or even more than that. We can no longer verify the exact number.

“The cultivators didn't have to rely on magical treasures to reach the Divine Transfiguration Stage, and they could fly from one star to another. At the time, one could see damaged stars throughout the universe, which were the aftermath of battles between cultivators!

“The splendor of ancient times is truly fascinating. Numerous legends were born, and many formidable cultivators were fostered. Back then, when the cultivation experts compared their strength, they would see how many stars one could destroy in one strike. When they compared their influence, they would see how many living stars one controlled.

“At the peak of their prosperity, a certain entity acted. They refined the universe of stars into one gargantuan continent. Regardless of whether a star was living, none of them could escape from his grasp.

“The reason for the vibrant life on the Central Continent is because this used to be a living celestial body, a place best suited for cultivation! To the east of the Central Continent, the vast ocean was once a celestial body covered by seawater. To the west of the Central Continent, the Golden Buddhist Kingdom was once a bleak, uninhabitable celestial body. The same logic applies to the Demon Region in the south and the Extreme North.”

Branch Leader Chu had undoubtedly overturned the trio’s understanding of the world. They had never imagined that the land beneath their feet was once a star that had been refined!

“Who exactly refined the stars?” Lu Yang asked.

Branch Leader Chu shook his head, not because Lu Yang’s position wasn’t high enough but because he truly didn’t know the answer. “There’s no way to verify their true identity, but one thing is certain: That Entity was definitely an immortal!”

Such extraordinary power is beyond something a Transcendent Cultivator is capable of!

“Why That Entity wanted to refine the stars into a continent and what methods were used remain a mystery. However, we can be sure of one thing: That Entity’s methods in refining the stars were extremely brutal and lacked benevolence. With their manipulation of the stars, how many of those living on them could have survived? Even ordinary cultivators found it a struggle to stay alive. For those who managed to survive, it’s not because of their high cultivation but due to sheer luck!

“When the proud geniuses and formidable figures rose up to resist, they were all beaten into a bloody fog and forced into the cycle of reincarnation. Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal intervened and saved most of the human race, preventing the extinction of humankind.

“The flourishing Great Era that was at its pinnacle was annihilated and crumbled away. For the longest time ever, not a single talent could be seen.

“There is no way to find out where That Entity is now, but they are certainly not dead. Who knows if That Entity would suddenly appear? If they unleashed an all-out massacre then, who can stop them?

“Only the Everlasting Immortal!

“That is why for both public and personal reasons, we have to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal! Reviving the Everlasting Immortal will only cause the death of a small number of people, but if we don’t revive the Everlasting Immortal, maybe the entire human race will be wiped out!

“Those detestable people from the righteous path think they're on the side of justice, but they don't know that the Everlasting Creed is the one sacrificing ourselves for the sake of the human race!” Branch Leader Chu’s tone was firm, his eyes glinting with resolve.

From the standpoint of the greater good, we kill people to save everyone else. From a personal standpoint, we have a justifiable reason for killing people, so we can kill without qualms. The reason the Everlasting Creed only recruits those from the diabolic path is precisely because this philosophy can resonate the most with the mindsets of diabolic cultivators.

Lu Yang was astonished. Just listening to what Branch Leader Chu said can really make a person madly believe in the Everlasting Immortal and pray for the immortal’s salvation.

But what he said may not be true, or perhaps they’re only part of the truth. Lu Yang didn’t believe that the Dao-Seeking Sect was completely oblivious to the matters of ancient times, and neither did he believe that Yun Zhi was completely unprepared.

Meng Jingzhou asked, “If that’s the case, why not cooperate with the righteous path? Wouldn’t it be easier to succeed with everyone working together?”

Branch Leader Chu sneered. “Who can guarantee that the entity who refined the stars isn’t hiding within the righteous path? After a series of investigations, the creed founder thinks that That Entity is within the righteous path, either among the Five Great Immortal Sects or within the Great Xia Dynasty.

“Why does the righteous path advocate for order? Isn’t it to allow more people to cultivate and for the Central Continent to flourish more? But what comes after prosperity? Don’t forget the painful history from the end of the ancient era. Maybe That Entity likes to harvest lives and they’re waiting for life to thrive again to make their move once more!” Branch Leader Chu voiced the mainstream view of the Everlasting Creed.

He added, “The stars above us may seem to be hanging in the sky, but if you reach a certain cultivation and fly to the universe to take a look, you’ll find that they are merely remnant shadows from ancient times. In theory, there should be some stars that slipped through the net, but they will certainly be rare.” Branch Leader Chu had told them so much because he hoped that the trio would sincerely believe in the Everlasting Immortal.

Seeing how astounded they are, there should be no problem.

“Alright, I know this information has been overwhelming. Go back and digest them.

“In addition, you three performed well in the three rounds of trial. The branch is currently in need of people. However, most people are resting in the prison cells. Since you have reached the Foundation Establishment Stage and meet the requirements to become an administrator, after some consideration, I have decided to promote you to administrators.”

Branch Leader Chu gave each of them a tablet, representing their status as an administrator.

In fact, Branch Leader Chu had intended for the trio to become administrators from the beginning. Only administrators were qualified to learn what he had shared with them earlier. He advised, “If you have the time, you can visit your fellow members. I heard that the food in prison isn’t good. Bringing them some food can help with building rapport.”

The diabolic path only cares about self-interest but also makes clear distinctions between favors and grudges. If those beneath me get too tangled up in internal strife and schemes, I won’t have an easy time as branch leader.

However, what Branch Leader Chu was worried about was not the subordinates scheming against the trio but rather that they would be tormented to death by the trio.

Lu Yang’s face was wreathed in smiles. “We are all brothers from the same creed. We will definitely unite as one and work together to resurrect the Everlasting Immortal. Please rest assured, Branch Leader.”

For some reason, Branch Leader Chu felt even more uneasy after hearing that.

Chapter 81: Stone Covert Weapon

“By the way, Branch Leader, you left without paying the bill for our previous meal. Are you going to hold it off or settle it now?” Man Gu asked right before he was about to leave.

Lu Yang hastily interjected Man Gu, “Shush! As part of the diabolic path, it is only right and proper of us to dine and dash. How could the branch leader be the type of good person who pays for their meals?!”

Meng Jingzhou concurred, “Exactly! What the branch leader said was that he would treat us, not settle the bill. How could you not even make such a simple distinction?!”

Branch Leader Chu, “...”

I must admit that when it comes to making sarcastic jabs at people, I’m no match for these three.

He gritted his teeth, resisting the urge to hit them, and threw a gold ingot to Man Gu. “Keep the change. You three, get out of here right now!”

Man Gu’s face was one of bewilderment. I’m just asking for money like a normal person would, but why do Brother Lu and Brother Meng sound strange? They seem to be speaking for me and the branch leader at the same time.

By the time the trio left, it was already late at night. Lu Yang gazed up at the resplendent starry sky and remarked, “Who would have thought that the stars in the sky are all fake? That was totally unexpected, truly unexpected.”

Meng Jingzhou scratched his head. “It’s not that unexpected right? Since I was young, my grandfather has told me that he’d get anything I wanted, including the stars in the sky. I was about seven or eight when I pointed at a star and said that I wanted it. My grandfather then traveled to the universe. When he returned, he placed a speck of light the size of a fingernail in my hands, saying that it was a star. Coincidentally, there was also one less star in the sky. I gestured to my grandfather, telling him that stars should be very big, even bigger than our courtyard. He just smiled mysteriously and claimed that stars were indeed this small.”

“What happened after that?” Lu Yang was intrigued.

“After that? After that, someone who seemed to be a high-ranking official from the Ministry of Justice came. They said that my grandfather was guilty of stealing natural resources and demanded that he return the star. My grandfather returned that speck of light, and a star appeared in the night sky again.

“At the time, I already felt that something was fishy, but I couldn’t figure out what it was. Over time, I forgot about it. Hearing about all this today, I realized that what I held in my hand then was really a star.”

“As expected of someone from the Meng Family. Your childhood experience is already very different from ours.” Lu Yang shook his head, trying to recall what he was doing during his own childhood.

Oh, I’ve remembered. When I was young, I was reminiscing about my life before transmigration and the classical poems I had to memorize, such as “The lofty tower stands a hundred chi high; I could pluck the stars with my hand. I dare not speak in a loud voice, lest I disturb those up in the sky.” [1]

I could only pluck stars in poems while Meng Jingzhou could pluck stars in reality. This is truly what disparity looks like.

Recently, Lu Yang had been contemplating whether he should write a novel like The Drifting Earth, but in the context of this world, it was probably not planets pushing the Earth but rather a formidable cultivator.

The trio didn’t continue dwelling on the issues of the stars and continent any longer. Such matters were too distant for them. With their current cultivation, they even struggled with lifting huge rocks, much less moving stars.

“Rest early. Tomorrow, we will visit our fellow creed members in prison.”

The three yawned. At the Foundation Establishment Stage, they could sit in meditation in place of sleeping. Although the effects were the same, the three of them still preferred to sleep.

Sit in meditation? We’ll leave it for the Golden Core Stage.

~~~

Early the next morning, Lu Yang found Constable Captain Wei, who readily approved his request to visit the prison and handed him a slip of paper.

Right as Lu Yang stepped inside, he felt as if his spirit energy was shackled, unable to manipulate any of it. Even his body became sluggish.

“Is this the Spirit Energy Disabling Array?” Lu Yang was surprised. He hadn’t expected the Spirit Energy Disabling Array to be as powerful as what Captain Wei had described.

When Captain Wei approved of Lu Yang’s visit to the prison, he had cautioned him to be careful of the Spirit Energy Disabling Array in the prison. It was specifically designed with cultivators in mind. Within the range of the array, cultivators’ cultivation will be frozen, preventing them from using any spells. This was to thwart prison breaks and escapes.

As the Spirit Energy Disabling Array was of a high tier, even Golden Core cultivators would be restricted. There were no exceptions.

Lu Yang had arrived just as the prison wardens were changing shifts. The prison wardens from the day shift yawned with tears in their eyes, their eyes in a daze as if they hadn’t woken up. As for the night shift wardens who were about to get off, they were in good spirits and teased, “Old Zhou, aren’t you usually the most energetic? Why are you so tired today? You didn’t do something shameful or secretive last night, right?”

Old Zhou’s mouth opened wide as he finished yawning before saying, “I don’t know what's been going on recently. I just can’t seem to wake up. It’s hard to get up in the morning. And it’s not just me, the same goes for my wife. Before coming here, I even washed my face, but I’m still sleepy.”

The night shift prison warden smiled. “It must be because you did something at night that kept you from sleeping well. Look at me, I’m not tired.”

Old Zhou’s mouth twitched. “You’re a cultivator; you’re different from me.”

The night shift prison warden waved dismissively, “I’m just at the Level One Qi Training Stage. Whether I’ll even reach Level Two is totally up in the air. I’m not really a cultivator.”

The prison’s rule was that the wardens in the day shift would be mortals while the wardens in the night shift would be Level One Qi Training Cultivators as the latter could ensure that they stay awake and vigilant during the night.

Cultivators were unwilling to be suppressed by the Spirit Energy Disabling Array and be no different from mortals. However, it was clearly inadequate to only have Level One Qi Training prison wards on guard, so there were covert sentinels posted outside to keep watch as cultivators.

After the change of shift, Lu Yang used the slip of paper to find Old Zhou. After glancing at Lu Yang and searching him, Old Zhou saw that he brought nothing else but a lunchbox, so he allowed him to pass.

~~~

Chi Xulong was infamous for his ruthlessness among the rogue diabolic cultivators in nearby commanderies. He thought that after he joined the diabolic creed, he would realize his grand ambitions, carve out his own territory, and become the local tyrant. Even imprisonment couldn’t change his aspirations.

Since I’m in prison, I’ll become the prison tyrant first!

The first hurdle standing in front of me is that I’m unable to intimidate others.

Chi Xulong was currently confined in a cage where even Foundation Establishment cultivators couldn’t break free. He didn’t even have a weapon at hand. The people in the neighboring cells were relentless with their insults or sarcasm. Chi Xulong could only grind his teeth in rage.

At this moment, his cellmate Shen Jinyi came up with an idea. He held a small stone in his mouth and spit it out. The stone shot out like a bullet with incredible power. One could only imagine the impact if it struck a person. As a killer, Shen Jinyi was well-versed in using various items as covert weapons.

“As brothers in the same dire straits, we should all the more cooperate sincerely and forge a way out together!” Shen Jinyi said with the code of brotherhood. “Once you learn this technique from me, you’ll be invincible in prison. Let’s conquer the prison together!”

Greatly spurred on by his words, Chi Xulong woke up early and slept late just so that he could diligently learn to use his mouth to shoot stone covert weapons with his mouth.

Unfortunately, Chi Xulong lacked the talent. Despite his brute strength, he couldn’t master the technique at all.

“You have to do it this way. Hold air in your mouth, then spit it out. Speed is key!” Shen Jinyi demonstrated, trying hard to teach Chi Xulong.

“I know, it’s just spitting it out.” Chi Xulong was getting impatient.

“No, no, that’s wrong, you’re not pouting enough. It should be like this.”

“Like this?”

Lu Yang stood outside, looking at both Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi pouting, wondering if he should remind them that such a scene could be easily misunderstood.

Let me capture this with a recording orb first.

1. This is a famous poem “A Night’s Lodging at a Mountain Temple” by famous poet Li Bai. The original poem has each stanza at five characters, so I translated it to eight words per stanza for the English version. ☜

Chapter 82: Faithfully Reported

“Long time no see, I’ve brought you some food.” Lu Yang’s attitude was amiable, a result of his training at the barbeque shop.

After more than a month of practice, Lu Yang’s fake smile was so convincing that Meng Jingzhou praised his smile for being as genuine as his own.

Chi Xulong was in the middle of pouting when he heard Lu Yang’s voice. He rapidly turned his head, malice in his eyes. If it weren’t for you calling the constables over to eat, how would I have ended up in this mess?

“Why are you here?” Chi Xulong’s tone was harsh. The first time I saw this fellow, he tricked me by pretending to be an examiner. During the meal a few days ago, he even set me up. He’s full of evil ideas. And now he’s being a hypocrite by bringing food? He’s definitely up to no good!

Compared to a ruthless murderer like himself, Chi Xulong felt that Lu Yang was even more despicable and shameless!

Lu Yang had no intention of playing with Chi Xulong in prison. All of us still have to help each other out in the future. There’s no point in straining our relationship. This is also the branch leader’s wish.

However, Lu Yang’s hearing might not have been the best, and he misheard Chi Xulong asking him whether he had become an administrator. “What? How did you know that I’ve been promoted to an administrator? But don’t be too agitated. As long as you perform well, you can also become an administrator.”

I didn’t expect Chi Xulong to be so well-informed even in prison.

Lu Yang even took out his waist tablet to flaunt, the characters for “administrator” extremely striking. Chi Xulong almost had fumes emitting from his head. “The heavens must be blind!”

Lu Yang tried to comfort him, “Don’t be angry. The branch leader also sent me here with a message for you.”

Hearing that Branch Leader Chu had a message for him, Chi Xulong calmed down a little. The branch leader still values me greatly to personally send a message. “What did he say?”

“He said that it’s best that you try to build rapport with me.”

Chi Xulong flew into a rage. The branch leader really thinks highly of this fellow. “I’d rather die than get along with you!”

Seeing how Chi Xulong blatantly disobeyed the branch leader’s instructions, Lu Yang sighed and left the food before leaving.

The prisoners drooled when they caught a whiff of the food’s aroma. They couldn’t get such delicious food in prison.

Lu Yang was much kinder to the others, encouraging them to reform themselves properly in prison and strive to turn over a new leaf after their release so that they could benefit the Central Continent. His words were filled with so much concern that people might have misunderstood that the prisoners would be staying in prison for at least ten years.

After leaving the prison, Lu Yang faithfully reported to Branch Leader Chu about his work updates. “I brought food to visit Chi Xulong in prison and said that there have been some misunderstandings between us. All of us are fellow companions, and we’ll be working with each other in the future, so building rapport would make our work more convenient. I stressed that this was your instruction, and I even mentioned that as long as he performs well, he can also become an administrator just like me.

“I didn’t expect Chi Xulong to fly into a rage and start cursing, claiming that the reason I became an administrator was that someone was blind. He declared that he’d rather die than get along with me. I don’t remember his exact words, but this was the general gist.”

Branch Leader Chu’s gaze immediately turned frigid. “Who did he say was blind?!”

Lu Yang hurriedly bowed. He gingerly raised his head to look at Branch Leader Chu and replied in trepidation, “That person’s position is too high, and it’ll be too disrespectful. I don’t dare to say.”

Branch Leader Chu had already formed an answer in his heart. “Alright, I got it. You may go back.”

Lu Yang sighed. Chi Xulong really doesn’t have a filter. “Branch Leader, please don’t say that you heard this from me. I might have remembered wrongly.”

Branch Leader Chu waved his hand impatiently. That’s a given.

After Lu Yang left, Branch Leader Chu tapped on his jade chair and snorted coldly. “Chi Xulong, how dare you say that I’m blind!”

~~~

Things were as usual that day. Meng Jingzhou strolled around the streets. Man Gu exercised and tempered his body in the backyard. The tiger-henchman ghosts skewered in the main hall. Lu Yang did his laundry.

As Lu Yang’s clothes were ordinary, they couldn’t be spotless.

“Damn it, why can’t I master the Garment-Cleansing Incantation?” Lu Yang grumbled as he scrubbed his clothes. He was the only one among the three who needed to wash his clothes. “When I have the money, I definitely have to buy a set of clothes that doesn’t need washing.”

A while ago, he had consulted Meng Jingzhou to learn the Garment-Cleansing Incantation. Meng Jingzhou didn’t know the spell personally, but he had a book titled Minor Spells for Everyday Life. His younger sister had secretly slipped it to him before he left.

This book recorded a spell called “Garment-Cleansing Incantation.” As the name suggested, it was an incantation that could make one’s clothes clean. It was simple and easy to pick up.

The three of them gathered together to learn it. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were the first to master it. As a refreshing burst of spirit energy descended from above, their filthy clothes instantly became pristine, as if they were brand new.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were elated. Working in the barbeque shop meant that it was easy for them to soil their clothes, which was very troublesome. Given Meng Jingzhou’s wealth, he naturally had a set of specially refined clothes that was a magical artifact that automatically kept itself clean and needed no washing. However, the clothes’ quality was too high that it would reveal his background, and that would not be advantageous for staying hidden in the diabolic creed.

Lu Yang’s high aptitude for spells was well-recognized. He did learn the spell, but the results were somewhat unexpected.

After casting the Garment-Cleansing Incantation, space distorted, and a brand new set of clothes appeared out of nowhere.

When it happened, Lu Yang had fallen silent for a long time. He wanted to curse but didn’t know where to start.

In terms of sequence, this was the first spatial spell Lu Yang had learned, holding much significance for him.

In terms of innovation, this was a novel transformation of the Garment-Cleansing Incantation, equivalent to creating a new spatial spell.

In terms of logic, there was no logic.

Lu Yang stared at the collar labeled “For So-and-So” and realized that the clothing was likely a custom-made garment from a tailor store. Before the customer could collect their clothes, he had summoned it with his spatial spell.

“Why does the Garment-Cleansing Incantation I cast summon a brand-new set of clothes instead?! What would happen if I cast the Body-Cleansing Incantation?!” Lu Yang was furious, thinking that the heavens probably found him too brilliant and had to purposely restrict his talent in spells.

He naturally couldn’t wear the clothes since they belonged to someone else. However, Lu Yang didn’t know who the owner was, so he couldn’t return them even if he wanted to.

Meng Jingzhou even kindly offered to perform the real Garment-Cleansing Incantation to help Lu Yang wash his clothes. After several attempts, it ended in failure.

The Garment-Cleansing Incantation could only be used for clothes worn by oneself. Lu Yang couldn’t possibly remove his clothes and let Meng Jingzhou wear them just so that he could let Meng Jingzhou clean the clothes before removing them again and passing them back to him.

Oh well, I can only wash the clothes manually by myself.

After Lu Yang was done with his laundry, he wanted to hang the clothes outside the window but accidentally caused the laundry drying pole to slip, and it was aimed straight at a passer-by.

“Be careful!”

Unexpectedly, the passer-by had excellent reflexes and sidestepped the laundry drying pole.

Lu Yang hurried downstairs and realized that the passer-by was a new acquaintance. It was Lan Ting, the disciple from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace who had helped them with fighting the tiger demon on Pine Mountain.

Lu Yang was puzzled. It’s been more than one month since then. Why is she still here?

Lan Ting lowered her head and stared at the laundry drying pole on the ground in silence, her brow slightly furrowed as if she was ruminating about a problem.

Lu Yang asked curiously, “What are you thinking about?”

Lan Ting blurted out, “I was wondering why the laundry drying pole doesn’t fall up toward the sky instead of falling down to the ground. Could there be an invisible force pulling at everything in the world?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Chapter 83: Lan Ting’s Secret Mission

Lu Yang complained by the side, “Since this invisible force makes everything gravitate to it everywhere, why don’t we call it gravity?[1]”

Finding the voice familiar, Lan Ting raised her head to look at Lu Yang. “Oh, it’s you.”

“Come in and talk.” Lu Yang was afraid that Lan Ting would reveal their true identities.

Lan Ting was extremely beautiful, her charming demeanor as she stood at the door very eye-catching. It would be easy for someone with ill intentions to eavesdrop on their conversation by the entrance.

As soon as Lan Ting stepped in, she saw the tiger-henchman ghosts hard at work and realized that they were the ones left behind by the tiger demon.

Upon noticing Lu Yang and Lan Ting walk in together, the two tiger-henchman ghosts silently picked up a bowl of meat and skewers and continued skewering at a table in the corner. Seeing how practiced their movements were, Lan Ting thought that this was what they did when they were alive.

Man Gu was training in the backyard when he heard the commotion. He took a pause and came to the main hall.

Meng Jingzhou had just finished a day of strolling around. He was shouting as soon as he entered, “Have you heard? Yanjiang Commandery has its own festival called the Spring Harvest Festival which is in half a month’s time. People go out for walks and scenic tours in spring, and at night, there will be a poetry gala with poetry recitations and music; it’ll be quite lively. People from nearby commanderies will come too, while the locals in Yanjiang Commandery get three days off.

“I even found out that the brothels would raise their prices during those few days every year, and they would make a fortune. Should we take advantage of this opportunity to organize a big promotion, something like a bargain sale to celebrate the two-month anniversary of our shop’s opening?”

Meng Jingzhou proved that he wasn’t going out just to play but was also gathering intelligence, though this piece of information wasn’t helpful to the three of them.

Man Gu’s eyes lit up. He was about to say something when he noticed Lu Yang’s emotionless gaze and silently kept his mouth closed.

Meng Jingzhou was surprised to see Lan Ting. “I remember you. You’re Lan Ting from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace?”

In order to open a barbeque shop, oh wait, I mean, to infiltrate the diabolic creed, we have stayed here for over a month. But why is Lan Ting here?

“That’s right,” Lan Ting replied softly.

Lan Ting found the three of them interesting. As she had stayed in Yanjiang Commandery for more than a month, she had naturally heard of One More Time Barbeque Shop’s fame. However, she preferred the peace and quiet, so she hadn’t come to visit the bustling shop. It was only because she happened to pass by today did she realize that the barbeque shop was run by someone she knew and disciples from an immortal sect at that.

It looks like the three of them have really achieved something great in Yanjiang Commandery through their hard work. Could it be that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s missions don’t just include vanquishing demons and devils but also running a business to earn money?

Considering the Dao-Seeking Sect’s reputation, that’s still plausible.

Lan Ting had heard from her senior sisters that one could exchange for the prize “Sect Leader One-Day Experience” on the rewards boards with their contribution points in the Dao-Seeking Sect. This is something not available in the other four immortal sects.

“You’re still here in Yanjiang Commandery; are you on a mission? If you need help, feel free to let us know. We have connections with constables and people in prison,” Lu Yang kindly offered. As fellow members of the Five Great Immortal Sects, we should help one another.

It wouldn’t be a stretch to say that Lu Yang’s trio was powerful to the extent they could almost cover the sky with one hand. On the surface, they were warm-hearted civilians who had helped Captain Wei catch criminals, and the constables frequently patronized them and gathered for meals. Under the table, they were promising diabolic spawns the Yanjiang Branch Leader valued. Meanwhile, their true identities were core disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Who could beat them in terms of their background?

Lan Ting fell silent. She had come here on a secret mission and shouldn’t be interacting with outsiders. Otherwise, after helping Lu Yang to defeat the tiger demon, she wouldn’t have perfunctorily asked for two tiger hides and simply left.

More than a month’s time had passed since then, yet there was still no progress, so she was getting anxious.

These three before me are my chance! Maybe they’ll be able to help me!

She took two deep breaths and steadied her breathing before solemnly replying to the three of them, “I am executing a secret mission, so what I’m about to tell you must be kept a secret. This concerns my safety! Don’t be shocked when you hear it!”

The three of them straightened their backs upon seeing how serious Lan Ting was.

“I plan to infiltrate the Everlasting Creed as a spy!”

The three of them blinked, thinking they were hearing things.

Lan Ting continued, “This is reliable information the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace obtained through special means. Recently, the Four Great Diabolic Creeds are planning to organize a large-scale recruitment of followers. The Radiant Sun Creed has finished their recruitment, while the other three diabolic creeds are still recruiting.

“In Yanjiang Commandery, there is a branch of the Everlasting Creed called the Yanjiang Branch. The branch leader is mysterious, their identity and even their surname unknown. Among all the branches of the Everlasting Creed, the Yanjiang Branch is ranked closer to the bottom, and the cultivation of its members are on the lower side, so it’s the most suitable for a Foundation Establishment cultivator like me to infiltrate them. With proper planning, it’s possible to even join the upper ranks.

“My senior sisters’ cultivation is too high and conspicuous. Moreover, they’re very reputable in the outside world, so it would not be ideal for them to be the ones infiltrating. After some discussion, the mission fell to me.”

When Lan Ting mentioned that her senior sisters were “very reputable,” she was referring to how they were so beautiful that they had previously appeared in some forbidden books to satisfy the fantasies of some men.

Lan Ting sighed, “But I’ve stayed in Yanjiang Commandery for over a month and still haven’t found the Yanjiang Branch’s location. I don’t even know if the selection trials have ended. I just hope that I’m not too late!” Lan Ting gazed at the three of them with hopeful eyes, especially toward Lu Yang who she found especially reliable, wishing that they could provide some help.

The trio silently took out the waist tablets from the branch leader, the characters for “Administrator” extremely prominent.

“Sorry, we’re already members of the Everlasting Creed.”

Exclamation marks were popping out from above Lan Ting’s head.

“Oh, don’t be alarmed. What we meant was that we have successfully infiltrated the Everlasting Creed,” Lu Yang added.

Lan Ting relaxed. I thought that the three of them had betrayed us, but it turns out that they’re just spies... Wait a minute, that doesn’t sound right either.

“How did you infiltrate the Everlasting Creed?!”

Lu Yang was placed in a tough spot. How should I say this? We simply participated in the selection trials and successfully passed.

Meng Jingzhou said proudly, “Our performance in the selection trials was stellar, and the Everlasting Creed found us to be very suitable for joining the diabolic creed, so they chose us.”

Man Gu didn’t understand what Meng Jingzhou was proud of.

Lu Yang tried to explain in simple terms that they had found Qin Yuanhao’s letter in the tiger demon’s lair, traced it to Qin Yuanhao, and learned about the diabolic creed’s recruitment and the location of the Yanjiang Branch.

Regret wrecked Lan Ting. Had I known, I would have joined Lu Yang and the others. Not only have I wasted more than a month’s time, I still haven’t even found the entrance to the Yanjiang Branch, while they have already become one of the higher-ups in the branch.

“Just like Qin Yuanhao, you can recruit ordinary creed members, right? Could you bring me in?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “Ordinary followers don’t have access to the Everlasting Creed’s secrets. To do that, you must undergo the trials from the headquarters. To be honest, I don’t think you can pass the trials. It’s quite likely that you’ll expose your identity.”

Lan Ting lowered her gaze in disappointment.

Lu Yang continued, “However, we can forge a false identity for you. We’ll say that you’re a distant relative of mine who has come looking for me to seek refuge, so you can stay with us. On the surface, you’ll be working at the barbeque shop, and during our operations, you can also support us. This way, it can count as fulfilling part of your mission.”

“Is that really possible?” Lan Ting hadn’t expected such great news.

Man Gu also hadn’t expected that the barbeque shop had finally recruited a new worker.

Lu Yang nodded. “Of course. As a Foundation Establishment cultivator, you'll be of considerable help to us. The only thing is that you stand out too much, so you’ll need to disguise yourself. By the way, do you know shapeshifting techniques? If you don’t, I can teach you.”

1. The Chinese term for gravity translates directly to something like “universal pulling force.” ☜

Chapter 84: The Tofu Shop on Qianmen Street

After Lan Ting witnessed the whole process of Lu Yang performing Animal Form Fist to transform into Man Gu, she silently took out a yellow talisman.

I think it’s best that I draw a Shapeshifting Talisman myself.

As expected of the immortal sect renowned for their fanciful imagination and spells to be disguising the Shapeshifting Technique as a fist technique. This is something only achievable with a profound comprehension of spells. Fellow Daoist Lu Yang must have reached the level where his comprehension of spells transcends spells and traces them to their origins.

Lan Ting believed that Lu Yang’s talent in spells was unrivaled among those at the same cultivation realm.

Lu Yang recalled that Lan Ting had also asked for the tiger hide previously to create talismans. It looks like she has quite the talent for talismans.

Lan Ting pointed at her own eyes. “My eyes are imbued with a divine wonder that makes them sensitive to patterns, allowing me to discern the core essence of runes and the focal point of arrays, so I’m naturally adept at crafting talismans and drawing arrays. However, I have limited capacity, so I have directed most of my energy to crafting talismans; I only have a very rudimentary understanding of arrays.”

Despite Lan Ting’s humility, the talent she possessed was actually an exceptional one that many talisman and array masters were envious of. Her talent was fated to take her far in the field of talismans and arrays

Soon, Lan Ting finished drawing a Shapeshifting Talisman and pasted it on herself. It was fascinating watching her stunning features change into ordinary ones right before their eyes.

Just like that, the barbeque shop welcomed its new staff.

~~~

After Lan Ting had joined the barbeque shop for two days, the trio’s workload had become much lighter although the shop was still busy as usual.

Lu Yang noticed that Man Gu appeared to be a little unhappy and used his spiritual consciousness to ask him while serving the customers, “Did something happen? You don’t seem very happy.”

Man Gu nodded. “I don’t know if you have noticed, Brother Lu, but the number of customers has decreased recently. I calculated our revenue for the past few days and confirmed that it’s indeed true.”

Lu Yang was taken aback as he hadn’t paid attention to this detail. “Because of Lan Ting?” But shouldn’t business be better with the addition of a female staff?

“No, the numbers have already been reducing before Lan Ting joined. I still haven’t figured out the problem.” Man Gu had been ruminating about this problem.

Lu Yang didn’t make much of it. He wished that there would be less business for the barbeque shop. “You can think about it first. I’ll go deliver the food.”

A month ago, at Meng Jingzhou’s suggestion, the barbeque shop had introduced a delivery service. A box would be placed at the entrance in the day, and those who wanted food delivery would deposit a piece of paper written with their desired barbeque skewers, delivery time, and address. At night, one of the three would be responsible for handling the deliveries.

It was Lu Yang’s turn today.

Lu Yang hadn’t gone out for the past few nights, and he noticed that there were considerably fewer pedestrians on the streets. Perhaps this is the reason for the barbeque shop’s lower customer traffic.

“Let me see where I should deliver this to...the tofu shop on Qianmen Street?”

~~~

Wen Xiangyu had long heard about the popular barbeque shop that opened recently. She was interested in giving it a try, wondering if it was really as delicious as in the rumors. However, ever since her husband passed away and she took over his tofu shop, she had hardly gone out at night.

She was not trying to brag, but with her beautiful appearance, she didn’t know how many people hungered after her, so going out alone would be very dangerous. Subsequently, she heard that the barbeque shop offered a food delivery service, so she wrote what she wanted to eat on a piece of paper and dropped it in the box outside the shop.

She had been very sleepy the past few days, and it was even worse today. Before the skewers could arrive, she had already succumbed to her sleepiness and lain on the bed.

The barbeque shop’s staff should probably be able to wake me up.

~~~

Lu Zhi was a thief who had been giving the constables a headache recently. He would sneak into people’s homes at night and steal their valuables while they were asleep, then he would swiftly depart, leaving behind negligible traces. When the constables questioned the neighbors, the answers were always something along the lines of them being too deep asleep to notice anything outside.

This time, Lu Zhi had set his sights on the tofu shop on Qianmen Street. The lady boss was a well-known pretty widow, and her tofu’s reputation reached far and wide. The money she earned the past few years caused the neighboring proprietors’ eyes to go red with envy.

Lu Zhi was agile like a monkey as he stealthily climbed to a rooftop. Twisting his body, he opened the window to the second floor.

“She should be asleep by now.”

He was extremely confident as he had happened to come across a yellow talisman that was capable of inducing deep slumber. He had pasted it outside the house, and everyone within fifty meters would sleep like a log. This trick of his had never failed him.

Holding his breath and slinking over cautiously, Lu Zhi saw the beauty lying in bed, and a sly smirk of triumph morphed onto his face. He then turned around to rummage through the cupboards for valuables. Based on my experience, women like to keep things here.

“Nothing?” Lu Zhi frowned and turned his gaze to where the tofu shop’s lady boss was.

Since there’s nothing here, the stuff should be under the bed.

He gingerly crouched down and peered under the bed. That was when his heart almost stopped beating.

There’s actually a human face underneath the bed!

“Ahhh, ghost!”

~~~

Zheng Shouhe was a rapist who had been giving the constables a headache recently. He often hid under the beds of single women beforehand, waiting for them to fall asleep before emerging to defile them. However, there were occasions where he would bump into women in the midst of an affair. In those cases, he could only force himself to wait patiently under the bed.

This time, he had set his sights on the tofu shop on Qianmen Street. The lady boss was a well-known pretty widow, and it was unclear how many souls she had captivated.

As usual, Zheng Shouhe had hid under the bed in advance, waiting for nightfall to have his way with the lady boss.

“I'm so sleepy.” Zheng Shouhe had never felt so sleepy. In the past, the more he waited, the more excited he would become. However, for some reason, sleepiness kept coming over him today. His eyelids were fighting with each other. After trying to open his eyes a few times, he ultimately succumbed to his sleepiness.

A shrill scream woke him up. He seems to be shouting “ghost” or something.

Zheng Shouhe suddenly opened his eyes and saw Lu Zhi staring at him in fright from under the bed. Zheng Shouhe immediately clamped his hand over Lu Zhi’s mouth and darted out from underneath the bed. His other hand took out a dagger from behind his waist and pressed it against Lu Zhi’s neck.

Zheng Shouhe then saw Wen Xiangyu curled up in bed, trembling in fear. She had clearly also been woken up by Lu Zhi shrieking.

“You get up too! What an unlucky day it is today!” Zheng Shouhe cursed out loud. He found some ropes and tied Lu Zhi up, planning to kill both Lu Zhi and Wen Xiangyu after he finished getting his way with the latter.

Just then, a knocking sound came from downstairs.

“Is anyone there? I'm here to deliver the food.”

Zheng Shouhe clicked his tongue. My luck today is really terrible! After binding Lu Zhi up, he coerced Wen Xiangyu to go downstairs with him.

Drawing his knife to threaten Wen Xiangyu, Zheng Shouhe growled in a low voice, “Tell the person outside to leave!”

Everyone in Yanjiang Commandery knew that the pretty widow lived alone. If he asked the person outside to leave, the other party would hear a male voice and get suspicious.

“Just leave it outside the door. I'll go out to get it in a bit,” Wen Xiangyu said in a soft voice.

“That won't do, you haven't paid yet,” the person at the door replied.

Zheng Shouhe’s face became warped in malice. Since you're courting death, you can't blame anyone!

Chapter 85: Lifespan-Reversal Talisman

“Open the door for him!” Zheng Shouhe gripped the dagger tightly as he pressed it against Wen Xiangyu’s back.

Wen Xiangyu had no choice but to open the door.

Upon opening the door, it revealed a delicate-looking person. It was none other than Lu Yang.

Wen Xiangyu tried her best to signal to Lu Yang with her eyes, urging him to run away immediately, but Lu Yang didn't seem to notice. A professional false smile appeared on his visage. “Your barbeque skewers.”

Zheng Shouhe also flashed a professional false smile. It's so obvious that this person is foolishly honest. It'll be too easy to trick him into coming in. “Young lad, why don't you come in and have a seat? I'll get the money for you.”

Believing that it was real, Lu Yang walked inside. He saw that the house was pitch-black and smiled. “Even the lamps are not lit. You sleep so early.”

Watching Lu Yang come in foolishly, panic consumed Wen Xiangyu’s heart. She steeled herself, planning to push Lu Yang out. But how could Zheng Shouhe not see through her intentions?

It's too late. Zheng Shouhe sneered and tossed Wen Xiangyu behind him, thrusting the dagger toward Lu Yang in the darkness.

Having spent long durations in darkness, Zheng Shouhe's eyes were already accustomed to it. Since this lad walked in from the streets, he'll definitely need some time to adjust to the darkness. This is my chance!

It looks like tonight is destined to be a night of bloodshed!

Lu Yang sent Zheng Shouhe flying four to five meters away with a single kick.

There's no point in talking about science with a cultivator.

Zheng Shouhe hadn't expected the kick from Lu Yang to be so powerful and heavy like a boulder crushing his chest. He began to see stars, and he had several broken ribs, causing him to vomit out a copious amount of blood!

He realized that he had encountered a tough one. If I want to live, I must take a hostage!

Forcefully using his willpower to suppress the pain in his chest, Zheng Shouhe flipped over to grab Wen Xiangyu’s wrist. “If you dare to move, I'll kill her!” he threatened fiercely.

The person in Zheng Shouhe’s arms sneered. “Who did you say you wanted to kill?”

Zheng Shouhe lowered his head. To his horror, the person he had caught was not Wen Xiangyu but Lu Yang!

Lu Yang used one hand to push against Zheng Shouhe's chin, while his other hand snatched the dagger and disabled all four of Zheng Shouhe’s limbs effortlessly.

“Jeez, what luck I have! I can come across so many problems when I'm just delivering food.” Lu Yang breathed out. He lit a candle, filling the room with a dim glow.

Wen Xiangyu hadn't expected the tables to turn so quickly. The waiter from the barbeque shop was like a god descending from heaven, subduing the ruthless villain in the blink of an eye.

“Are you alright?” Lu Yang helped the stupefied Wen Xiangyu up from the floor.

“I-I’m fine.”

“That’s good to hear. You can pass me the money for the barbeque skewers then,” Lu Yang said politely.

“Ah? Oh...oh.” Only then did Wen Xiangyu remember that Lu Yang had just come to deliver the food and saved her in passing.

Even after giving Lu Yang the money, Wen Xiangyu still hadn't recovered from the trauma, so she tried to say something to ease the fear lingering in her heart. “You...you're a cultivator?”

“That’s right.”

“Cultivators also open shops?”

“Gotta make a living somehow.”

Zheng Shouhe was lying on the ground and howling in pain, regret flooding him. What luck I have! I just have to bump into a cultivator when I go out. Are cultivators already at the point where they have to deliver food to make ends meet?

Noticing that Wen Xiangyu was still dazed from having narrowly escaped death, Lu Yang chuckled and shook his head. “Let me accompany you to report this case to the authorities.”

“Thank you.” Wen Xiangyu remembered the thief upstairs. “Oh right, there’s another person upstairs, probably his accomplice.” When Wen Xiangyu first woke up, she saw Zheng Shouhe and Lu Zhi together, so she assumed that they were together but simply had a falling out because of her beauty.

When Lu Yang went upstairs and saw the tightly bound Lu Zhi, he also assumed that Lu Zhi was Zheng Shouhe’s accomplice. “A gang-related crime, huh?”

Lu Zhi cried out in protest, “Don’t say that! I’m not with him! He’s a kidnapper, while I’m just a thief. The punishments for both are completely different!”

Lu Yang was amused. “You know the law quite well.”

“Those in our line of work always check the law before committing a crime to check how many years we’ll be sentenced to,” Lu Zhi explained in a manner that showed how adroit he was.

“Let’s go to the yamen then. We’ll see how many years you get sentenced to.”

As soon as Lu Zhi heard the word “yamen,” he grew so terrified that he implored, “No, no, please don’t, brother! We can discuss it peacefully. We are all just trying to get by in the jianghu, so why push things so far? How about this? Why don’t I give you something good and you’ll let me off the hook?”

Lu Yang sized up Lu Zhi and determined that he was just a mortal. “What good thing?”

“A yellow paper that can make people sleep. With this paper, you can make anyone fall asleep, and you can do whatever you want with her!”

Associating it with the strange occurrences recently, Lu Yang furrowed his brow as he realized that things weren’t as they seemed. He asked in a cold voice, “Where’s the thing?”

Lu Zhi thought to himself, I’m not silly! How could I answer just because you asked? “Promise to let me go first!”

Lu Yang solemnly vowed, “I, Chi Xulong, swear to the heavens that if I don’t let you go, may Chi Xulong be struck by five bolts of lightning!”

Lu Zhi was overjoyed. “The yellow paper is on the corner of the outer wall on the first floor.”

Evidently, Lu Zhi was also not very clever.

Lu Yang jumped down from the second floor and circled around the first floor, discovering a piece of yellow paper. There was an indecipherable symbol drawn on it, which made it look like some kind of talisman.

He stowed away the talisman and returned to the second floor. “Where did you get this thing from?”

“Right under the Big Stone Bridge. I once fled by boat and happened to see a yellow paper pasted to the bottom of the Big Stone Bridge when I looked up.”

Lu Yang nodded. He went downstairs to connect Zheng Shouhe’s legs and sent the two of them to the yamen with Wen Xiangyu following closely behind.

“Hey hey hey, you went back on your word!” Lu Zhi hollered.

Lu Yang snorted. The one getting struck by lightning is Chi Xulong. What does that have to do with me, Lu Yang?

Captain Wei happened to be on duty tonight. When he saw Lu Yang escorting two criminals to the yamen, the feeling of “it’s you again” sprouted in his heart.

After listening to the situation regarding the two criminals, he was no longer in a mood to joke. Zheng Shouhe is wanted for murder and is a major criminal. Lu Yang has accomplished a meritorious achievement.
