Lu Yang passed the yellow paper to Captain Wei. “This is the yellow paper Lu Zhi mentioned.” He had already noted down the symbol on the yellow paper.

Captain Wei took the yellow paper and also realized the gravity of the issue. I’ve been hearing subordinates mention that they were sleepy in the morning. Since I didn’t feel anything, I didn’t think it was anything significant. But it now looks like someone is purposely causing trouble!

We don’t even know how many yellow papers there are in Yanjiang Commandery!

However, Captain Wei also didn’t know what the symbol on the yellow paper represented. I’ll ask the chief constable when he gets to work in the morning.

“Thank you, I’ll send you another silk banner tomorrow.” After recording Lu Yang’s and Wen Xiangyu’s statements, Captain Wei waved goodbye.

Before leaving, Lu Yang made a trip to the prison and found Chi Xulong. “I have a brother called Zheng Shouhe who will be coming in for a while. Please look after him.”

Chi Xulong sneered. To think that you also need to beg me for help. Look after him? I have already mastered my stone-spitting divine arts. Watch how I’ll sort him out!

After sending Wen Xiangyu back to the tofu shop, Lu Yang firmly refused the tofu she offered.

Having gone through all that, the barbeque shop had already closed by the time Lu Yang returned. The two tiger-henchman ghosts were washing the dishes.

Lu Yang passed the drawings of the symbol from the yellow paper to Lan Ting. “Take a look at this sigil. Can its effects cause people to fall asleep?”

After examining it, shock spread across her visage. “Where did you find this? This is a Lifespan-Reversal Talisman. It will absorb people’s lifespans. On the surface, symptoms are a lack of energy and excessive sleepiness. This type of sigil only affects mortals, whereas cultivators are completely unaffected.”

Chapter 86: Spy Within the Authorities

“There are currently numerous people showing symptoms of excessive sleepiness. Could the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman already be absorbing the lifespans of ordinary people?”

Lan Ting shook her head. “It’s not like that. Lifespan is a root of life and is not so easily affected. From your description, the people have only started exhibiting sleepiness recently. This is just the prelude. It’ll take at least half a month before it begins to truly absorb lifespans.

“The actual process of absorbing lifespans is extremely slow and hard to detect. But there’s also a method to forcefully activate it.”

“What method?!” Lu Yang pressed further.

Lan Ting replied solemnly, “Using Lifespan-Reversal Talismans as a node to set up a Lifespan-Reversal Array with human blood as a catalyst. This can activate the array without having to wait for half a month and use the lifespans of mortals to enhance one’s cultivation!”

In reality, the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman and Lifespan-Reversal Array were not commonly accessible knowledge, with only mentions of it in a few books. Furthermore, as the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman was truly wicked, books with their records became classified as forbidden. Even those erudite array masters might have only heard of the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman but not know its pattern.

Lan Ting was qualified to access these forbidden books only because she hailed from the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace. Despite claiming that her knowledge of arrays was superficial, what she just displayed was far beyond what one could consider as superficial.

Lan Ting continued, “However, the person who wrote the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman probably doesn’t know how to set up the Lifespan-Reversal Array. Before the array is activated, it should be more secretive with no warning signs of sleepiness. However, that doesn’t rule out the possibility that the culprit is still in the middle of setting up the array.”

While listening by the side, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu also realized the gravity of the situation. If everyone in Yanjiang Commandery is experiencing sleepiness, that implies that the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans are hidden in various locations across Yanjiang Commandery! The mastermind behind the scenes is plotting something big!

“After the Lifespan-Reversal Array is activated, to what extent can it elevate the caster’s cultivation?”

Lan Ting shook her head. “It’s hard to say. This depends on how much lifespan the array absorbs. I can’t tell at the moment.”

“Come on, let’s go to the Big Stone Bridge to take a look. Maybe there are more there!” Lu Yang called the three of them to follow him.

To the west of Yanjiang Commandery was a large river called the Hidden Dragon River. The section passing through Yanjiang Commandery flowed slower, making it a popular scenic spot. The name “Yanjiang,” which meant “delayed river,” was thus derived.

The “Big Stone Bridge” the unsuccessful thief, Lu Zhi, had mentioned was located right here.

It was currently in the middle of the night. There was not a single soul at the Hidden Dragon River. The four of them searched the whole Big Stone Bridge thoroughly for Lifespan-Reversal Talismans but to no avail.

“As expected, the other party isn’t foolish. They wouldn’t place two Lifespan-Reversal Talismans at the same place.”

~~~

The next morning, Captain Wei went to look for the chief constable, Fang Qingyun.

“Little Wei, what brings you here?”

“Shifu, have you noticed that the civilians of Yanjiang Commandery have been going to bed early and having trouble waking up in the morning?”

Fang Qingyun nodded. “That’s indeed the case. I think a possible reason is the increased cost of living amidst stagnant income in Yanjiang Commandery. Stressed about their livelihood, the people have to work hard in the day to earn money.”

Captain Wei rubbed his forehead in frustration, cautiously finding the appropriate words. “Shifu, I know that you’re eager for a promotion and have been reading socio-economic books recently to build a solid foundation. But have you considered that you might not be suited for development work?”

“Don’t beat about the bush, be it something you have to say or fart you have to release!”

“...It’s like this. Last night, a zealous civilian caught a thief red-handed. According to the thief’s confession, he had stumbled across a talisman that made people fall asleep, and it can make anyone sleepy within a radius of fifty meters.”

Captain Wei took out the talisman from a box with a paper strip seal[1] pasted outside.

The paper strip seal had a suppressing effect of a seal. He realized that despite the sleep-inducing talisman not affecting him, it worked extremely well on ordinary people—his fellow companions on the night shift had all fallen asleep. Therefore, he could only lock the talisman in a box.

“Do you recognize this thing?”

Fang Qingyun examined it for a moment, then shook his head, expressing that he also didn’t recognize it. “Commandery Governor Li is very knowledgeable. Perhaps he’ll know.”

When the two of them found Commandery Governor Li, the latter was currently buried in his work affairs. The two were very impressed by Commandery Governor Li. He was a Golden Core cultivator who had been in Yanjiang Commandery for twenty years, and throughout the years, Yanjiang Commandery had not changed in the slightest bit. However, every time a superior arrived in Yanjiang Commandery for inspection or Commandery Governor Li went to deliver a report to the higher-ups, the best side of Yanjiang Commandery would always be presented, as if the commandery had undergone some monumental change in these twenty years.

“Commandery Governor Li, I have something to report!” Fang Qingyun called out.

Commandery Governor Li placed his writing brush down and gestured for him to take a seat.

Captain Wei truthfully reported what had transpired last night and took out the talisman for Commandery Governor Li to have a look.

Commandery Governor Li narrowed his eyes, slightly surprised. He seemed to have thought of something and fell into contemplation for a few minutes before saying, “If my memory serves me right, this is a Lifespan-Reversal Talisman? Thirty years ago, I was in charge of cracking down on the diabolic path in Poyang Commandery. During my exchanges with colleagues from other commanderies. Someone had mentioned this talisman and called it the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman. It is said to be able to absorb people’s lifespans and convert them into one’s cultivation. This is undoubtedly a method of the diabolic path.”

He continued in a solemn tone, “With the Spring Harvest Festival around the corner, many people from other commanderies will come pouring in, and that includes both ordinary people and cultivators. The Spring Harvest Festival is the icon of Yanjiang Commandery. Nothing is allowed to go wrong. You must apprehend these diabolic culprits who posted these talismans before the Spring Harvest Festival begins! These diabolic followers are lawless and have no regard for the imperial court!

“Chief Constable Fang, you have to pay special attention to this matter. If the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman is allowed to fully take form, the repercussions will be dire!”

He then suddenly changed his tone, “Of course, if you manage to capture the main culprit, that will be a great meritorious achievement, and I will report that to the higher-ups. If possible, you should aim for a breakthrough in your cultivation. That way, your promotion will be set in stone.”

“Understood!”

“There’s nothing else from me. You may leave. I have another meeting later.”

~~~

The next day, Lu Yang and the rest wanted to follow up on the clues to search for the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans’ locations. Before they could depart, however, Branch Leader Chu sent someone to summon Lu Yang over.

Lu Yang didn’t understand why Branch Leader Chu had only called for him. He silently put on his guard, finding the matter to be a little strange.

Branch Leader Chu was sitting on the jade chair, his hands supporting his head. His hoarse voice came from behind his mask. “I heard that you caught a thief last night and even found a yellow talisman capable of making people fall asleep?”

Lu Yang replied respectfully, “Yes, I suspect that the yellow talisman is one of our methods from the diabolic path, so I wanted to track down the person who drew the talisman, kill them, and master the art of drawing such talismans!”

Branch Leader Chu waved his hand. “Maintaining connections with the authorities on the surface is important, but it’s different this time around. The authorities will be taking this matter seriously and investing their resources in pursuing the investigation. Even a Golden Core cultivator will be involved. The truth will be uncovered soon. Don’t meddle in this further, lest you expose your identity and get yourself implicated.

“It’s just a talisman that makes people fall asleep. It’s not worth the risk.”

Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. It’s only morning, yet Branch Leader Chu has already learned about last night’s events. He even knows that a Golden Core cultivator will be involved. I didn’t even know that.

That can only mean one thing—the Yanjiang Branch has planted a spy within the authorities!

1. A strip of paper that indicates something is sealed or cordoned off. In Chinese dramas, you often see them pasted on the door or boxes confiscated by the authorities. ☜

Chapter 87: Learning the Invisibility Talisman

When the trio first entered Yanjiang Commandery, Man Gu had suggested tipping off the local authorities about the Yanjiang Branch so that they could search for Qin Yuanhao together. However, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou had rejected his idea with the reason that the authorities couldn’t be trusted.

And now it seemed like both of them had made the right call in taking precautions.

The Yanjiang Branch had planted a spy within the authorities, and it was someone in a high position at that!

Branch Leader Chu spoke unhurriedly, “Lu Yang, among the upper ranks of the Yanjiang Branch, I have the highest hopes for you. After the Spring Harvest Festival, the higher-ups will dispatch someone to evaluate the Yanjiang Branch. The inspection this time around will be different. We now have you, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu, who are three diabolic spawns. The higher-ups' assessment of me will improve significantly.

“There’s an extremely high chance of me getting promoted. If that happens, the position of Branch Leader will become vacant. The usual practice is that the new branch leader will be chosen from the upper ranks of the same branch. Although you lack experience, considering the creed leader’s appraisal of you, it is possible for the higher-ups to appoint you as the new branch leader. Your competitors are still locked up in prison and won’t be released for another three days. On account of their foolish behavior, the higher-ups won’t look upon them fondly.

“The Spring Harvest Festival is a major festival among the nearby commanderies and wields considerable influence. If you cause some commotion during such a festival, the higher-ups will hold you in even higher regard,” Branch Leader Chu subtly hinted to Lu Yang.

~~~

Lu Yang relayed Branch Leader Chu’s words to the rest. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were glad that they had decided to start rumors about Qin Yuanhao instead of seeking help from the authorities.

Otherwise, we wouldn’t have such a thriving barbeque business now.

Lu Yang somehow sensed that their focus was not on the right thing.

“We just don’t know who Branch Leader Chu’s spy is.” The four of them found themselves in a bind. They didn’t know who was qualified to be privy to the matters of the yellow talisman within the authorities.

“There’s nothing to fear. You’ll know who the spy is once you become the branch leader. With how much Branch Leader Chu values you, he’ll definitely tell you before he leaves!” Meng Jingzhou laughed out loud.

I didn’t expect Lu Yang to get promoted so quickly. If Lu Yang gets promoted, Man Gu and I have free rein to stir up whatever trouble we want in Yanjiang Commandery.

That’s the beauty of having someone backing you up.

While the four were in the middle of their fervent discussion, Captain Wei knocked on the door. “Shop Owner Lu, I’ve brought you another silk banner.”

Lu Yang opened the door, and the cordial Captain Wei came in.

“Oh, it’s quite the lively atmosphere, everyone’s here,” Captain Wei casually commented.

“We were discussing yesterday’s case.”

Captain Wei warned sternly, “Shop Owner Lu, you must keep yesterday’s case a secret. Don’t let anyone else know. I am aware that all of you are not ordinary people but cultivators who are here to experience life, and you will even courageously stand up for justice at times.

“But it’s not the same this time. Ruthless diabolic cultivators are involved. One wrong move and it could cost you your life. You must not seek out the owner of the talisman.”

Lu Yang couldn’t help but chuckle. The diabolic path is warning me not to meddle in this matter, and now the righteous path is also warning me to do the same.

“Don’t laugh! This is an extremely serious matter!” Captain Wei assumed that Lu Yang didn’t take this matter to heart.

Lu Yang straightened his face and guaranteed that he wouldn’t intervene in this affair. Only then did Captain Wei feel reassured to leave.

“Drink some tea before you go.”

Captain Wei waved his hand. “I’ll have to decline. Our leader is pressing me. I still have to gather my men to search for the other talismans.”

After seeing Captain Wei off, the four of them were worried that the yamen lacked manpower and might not be able to catch the culprit working in the shadows. If this goes wrong, countless people will have their lifespans secretly robbed.

Lu Yang lowered his head pensively. “We have already learned how to conceal our breaths, but relying on just that wouldn’t necessarily be safe.” He raised his head to look at Lan Ting who was learning how to skewer from the tiger-henchman ghosts.

An idea sparked in his mind.

“Daoist Friend Lan Ting, I have a request.”

Lan Ting smiled. “All of us are fellow immortal sect disciples who exterminate evil together. Besides, I’m your subordinate now. Don’t stand on ceremony with me. Just call me Lan Ting.”

Lu Yang followed without hesitation, “Lan Ting, can you teach us the Invisibility Talisman?”

Lan Ting immediately deduced what Lu Yang was getting at. “Do you intend to use the Invisibility Talisman to conceal yourselves and secretly help Captain Wei?”

Lu Yang nodded.

“Of course, that’s not a problem. The Invisibility Talisman doesn’t require any complicated runes. Anyone who isn’t severely lacking in talent will be able to pick it up in half a day.”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were overjoyed to hear that they could learn something new again, especially something that was not taught by Lu Yang.

“Have the three of you learned the art of talismans before?”

The three shook their heads.

Lan Ting didn’t show any signs of surprise. “I’ll start from the beginning then.”

Lan Ting was also very excited. It was her first time teaching others. Back in the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, it has always been my senior sisters teaching me, and now it’s finally my turn to be a teacher.

“The original essence of talismans is to materialize spells with symbols on paper. Since the three of you are from the Dao-Seeking Sect and talented in spells, it will be very easy for you to learn.

“...The Talisman Gall is the soul of a talisman. Whether a talisman can manifest power to its potential largely depends on whether there is a Talisman Gall standing guard in the center...

“...The most commonly used symbol in talismans is the Cloud Sigil. It is a design that imitates the ever-changing shapes of clouds in the sky and is drawn from nature...

“As for the Invisibility Talisman, it uses the “Gang” character for gale as the Talisman Gall and the ethereal Cloud Sigil as its pattern.”

Lan Ting dipped her fingertip in water. With a few swift strokes, she traced an Invisibility Talisman on the table. Then she used her hand to absorb the Invisibility Talisman from the table to her palm and slapped it to herself. Following which, the three of them saw Lan Ting vanish right before their very eyes.

A few moments later, Lan Ting appeared again with a faint smile. “This is the most basic Invisibility Talisman. It can only conceal the body from sight. You should still be able to detect my presence and location through details like my breathing and heartbeat.”

The three nodded. Even if that’s the case, it’s already pretty impressive.

“Give it a try.”

After half a day of training, the three gained a preliminary understanding of talismans. They pulled out their calligraphy tool set.[1] However, they were still unable to use water as a medium to draw talismans like Lan Ting.

As Meng Jingzhou had practiced calligraphy for years, his handwriting was excellent, and his grip on the brush was steady. As spirit energy flowed at the tip of the brush, an Invisibility Talisman was soon drawn. It looked eighty percent similar to Lan Ting’s. After a few more attempts, it became almost identical to Lan Ting’s version.

Meng Jingzhou gleefully pasted it on himself. As expected, he disappeared.

Man Gu was slightly less talented in this aspect. His control over spirit energy was not adequately precise. It took him dozens of attempts to succeed once. However, with every attempt, his success rate grew.

Lan Ting inwardly exclaimed in admiration, As one would expect from disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. They’re naturally talented in talismans.

What about Lu Yang? Lan Ting turned to look in Lu Yang’s direction.

Lu Yang also finished drawing an Invisibility Talisman very quickly, and he even succeeded on his first try, demonstrating truly terrifying talent.

He stuck the Invisibility Talisman on himself, and he completely disappeared.

However, only his body vanished—his clothes remained visible. It was just like a haunted ghost scene.

“What the ghost?!” In a strange turn of events, even clothes could speak.

Lu Yang was thinking that since he was currently invisible, he might as well remove his clothes. To his despair, he realized that the Invisibility Talisman was also still visible.

Invisibility my ass!

He almost wanted to rip off the talisman in frustration. Thankfully, his sense of reason was still working to stop him from doing so.

1. The Four Treasures of the Study (Wen Fang Si Bao) refer to brush, ink, paper, and inkstone. ☜

Chapter 88: Lan Ting’s Growth

Lan Ting spiraled into self-doubt regarding her teaching abilities. She had heard that Lu Yang ranked first among the new joiners of the Dao-Seeking Sect, which implied that his talent in spells must be exceptional. The Animal Form Fist I witnessed previously was a testament to his superb talent in spells that is capable of creating miracles.

But why is it that as soon as I get into the picture, it turns into this?

Did I teach him wrongly?

That shouldn’t be the case. This is how my senior sisters have taught me. I also taught Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu the same way. There was no problem at all. Could it be that I’ve underestimated Lu Yang’s talent in spells? Maybe an extraordinary genius like him requires extraordinary teaching methods?

In the process of doubting herself, she even felt guilty.

On the other hand, Lu Yang was in his own world as he studied his own talisman, completely oblivious to all the self-doubt that wrecked a talisman genius’ heart because of him. “Say, is there a talisman that can make other talismans invisible? That way, my Invisibility Talisman can become invisible.”

Meng Jingzhou mused over it for quite a while before replying, “I can’t imagine why someone would invent this kind of talisman.”

Lu Yang’s head drooped, deflated. He put his clothes back on and continued practicing drawing the Invisibility Talisman. However, the result was the same as before—his body turned invisible as it should, but his clothes weren’t cooperative.

In contrast, Man Gu’s drawing made progress with every attempt, giving Lan Ting a sense of accomplishment.

Meng Jingzhou gloated, “Haha, just give up! You will never draw a proper Invisibility Talisman.”

Lu Yang was irked. Pinching the Invisibility Talisman with his two fingers, he pasted it on Meng Jingzhou’s forehead. “Ha! Demon, have a taste of my talisman!”

Meng Jingzhou vanished, but his clothes remained.

Not accepting defeat, Meng Jingzhou also fished out his Invisibility Talisman and slapped it on Lu Yang’s forehead. “Daoist, you’re not the only one who can draw talismans!”

Both Lu Yang and his clothes vanished.

The two kept up with their flurry of attacks with talismans, though they lacked any form of offensive power.

Sandwiched between the two of them, Man Gu simply concentrated on drawing his talisman.

“I’m done.” Man Gu was pleased as he took out a stash of successfully drawn Invisibility Talismans. Through constant practice, his success rate was already approaching a hundred percent.

And thus, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu graduated.

And so did Lu Yang. By taking Lan Ting’s Invisibility Talisman.

“By the way, Lan Ting, do you know how the Lifespan-Reversal Array is set up?” Lu Yang asked. He wondered if the mastermind was truly using Lifespan-Reversal Talismans to set up the Lifespan-Reversal Array but was simply not done with it yet.

If that’s really the case, after finding a dozen Lifespan-Reversal Talismans or so, it should be very easy to reference their positions to deduce the locations of the other talismans.

Lan Ting nodded. She used her spirit energy to draw an extremely intricate array with over a thousand nodes in the air. “The scale of the Lifespan-Reversal Array is massive with numerous nodes. If there are only a few culprits behind the scenes, considering the time it takes to place the talismans in secret locations, they wouldn’t be able to complete setting everything up in a short span of time.”

“Got it. In that case, please watch the shop for us. The three of us will go out and see if there is anything we can help with,” Lu Yang said.

“Ah? Me? Watch the shop?” Lan Ting was a little uneasy. In the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, I’ve always listened to my senior sister’s instructions without having much of an opinion. Now that she suddenly had to look after such a huge shop by herself, she couldn’t help but lack the confidence.

“No worries, nothing will happen. If something does come up, just make the decision yourself.” Lu Yang didn’t see anything wrong with the arrangement and immediately left.

After the trio departed, Lan Ting couldn’t sit still as realization sank in that she had to temporarily manage a large store by herself.

“I’ll first set up a Spirit-Energy Gathering Array then,” Lan Ting muttered to herself as she tried to keep herself occupied.

The Spirit-Energy Gathering Array was a foundational array for cultivators. She realized that there wasn’t one in the barbeque shop and was puzzled how the three of them had been cultivating without it.

“Since everyone stays on the second floor, I’ll set it up there.”

Since the Spirit-Energy Gathering Array was a fundamental array, Lan Ting could set it up with ease. She took out spirit stones from her jade tablet and arranged them exactly according to what she had learned in class.

“I’ll set up a Mind Concentration Array too so that one can quickly enter a suitable state for cultivation.

“And a Soundproofing Array too; things will be quieter that way.”

Lan Ting was meticulous in her work. Considering that the Spirit-Energy Gathering Array might be too effective and attract the attention of other cultivators, Lan Ting set up another array that would block out the fluctuations in spirit energy.

“It should be foolproof now,” Lan Ting was satisfied with her attention to detail.

“Hello, is anyone here?” A voice came from downstairs, startling Lan Ting. It sounded like it belonged to a woman.

Lan Ting went downstairs and saw a fair-skinned woman standing at the entrance and hesitating whether she should step in.

“Hello, may I ask who you are...”

“I’m Wen Xiangyu. I run the tofu shop on Qianmen Street. May I know if Shop Owner Lu is around?” Wen Xiangyu’s voice was so tender that it sent a tingling sensation through whoever listened to it.

“He went out. Is anything the matter?” Lan Ting recalled that Lu Yang had mentioned her briefly when recounting how he had discovered the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman.

“Ah, it’s like this, isn’t the Spring Harvest Festival just around the corner? I was thinking of working on a collab event together with your barbeque shop.”

Lan Ting invited Wen Xiangyu in and poured some tea. “What kind of event?”

“I’m not trying to brag, but my tofu shop has many customers, and the number will only increase during the Spring Harvest Festival. Hence, I was thinking that we could organize a joint promotion where those who buy at my tofu shop can enjoy a ten-percent discount when they dine at your barbeque shop and vice versa.

“We can also add in elements like a spin-to-win wheel and masks.”

“Masks?”

Wen Xiangyu took out a few masks. They were square and looked soft and white like blocks of tofu.

“These are masks created based on my tofu shop’s mascot. They have a high sales volume.”

Lan Ting contemplated for a bit and felt that Wen Xiangyu’s idea was a good one. Moreover, the barbeque shop could only stand to benefit. Recalling how Lu Yang had completely placed the barbeque shop in her hands during this period of time, she agreed to Wen Xiangyu’s proposal.

Wen Xiangyu was elated to have Lan Ting accept her suggestion. With that, the two women began discussing from the minute details of the event to the rewards for the wheel of fortune then to the concept of gravity.

“There’s an invisible force pulling on everything in this world. Lu Yang also agrees with my viewpoint, and he called this force ‘gravity’... However, Lu Yang thinks that this kind of invisible force is a natural phenomenon, while I think that someone has set up a colossal array that is pulling at us.

“Oh right, you’re not familiar with arrays. Let me tell you about them. Arrays are very interesting. This book, The True Insight to Arrays, is able to take a complicated subject and unpack it in a digestible manner...”

When Wen Xiangyu came, her heart was filled with gratitude toward Lu Yang, and when she left, her head was filled with concepts of arrays.

After seeing Wen Xiangyu off, Lan Ting noticed the tiger-henchman ghosts skewering in a corner, and something sparked in her mind.

Since Lu Yang’s ideas are so bold and imaginative, if I want to teach him well, should I learn how to think like him? For example, maybe I can use the Levitation Array and Fire-Gathering Array as the basis for designing an Automatic Barbecue Array?

Hmm, that sounds like a pretty good idea.

Chapter 89: It Is Not Recommended for Diabolic Cultivators To Dine at the Barbeque Shop

Meanwhile, Lu Yang was still not aware that Lan Ting had successfully clinched a big business deal. He was currently using the Invisibility Talisman and Concealment Technique to tail the bailiffs and search for the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans.

The trio split up to cover as much ground as possible and locate the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans. They could tell that the authorities took this matter very seriously from how the authorities had mobilized almost all their manpower, as if they were ready to turn Yanjiang Commandery inside out.

The authorities started off by summarizing data on the areas where civilians easily became fatigued or sleepy, then proceeded with their search according to these demarcated zones.

Fang Qingyun even manifested two clones of himself. His real self and two clones spread their spiritual consciousness, leading the troops to search for the talismans.

As Fang Qingyun’s cultivation was too high, the trio didn’t dare to follow him directly.

Soon after, a bailiff found a Lifespan-Reversal Talisman. While hiding in the shadows, Lu Yang silently noted down the location.

When evening came around, Lu Yang reconvened with the other two and took out a map of Yanjiang Commandery with the locations of the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman marked out.

“One at the Big Stone Bridge, one in the rogue shop on Qianman Street, one in the pawn shop... These are the locations of the six Lifespan-Reversal Talismans we have found.

“These inconsequential pieces of information alone can’t let us ascertain if they’re indeed arranged according to the Lifespan-Reversal Array. Let’s take a look again tomorrow.”

Upon returning to the barbeque shop, the three saw Lan Ting assiduously improving the Automatic Barbecue Array while wearing a tofu mask.

The barbeque skewers hovered over the table as it became roasted under the high temperatures.

The two tiger-henchman ghosts knelt on the ground, tears and snot streaming down as they thanked Lan Ting for her great favor in rescuing them from their endless hell of barbecuing.

Question marks appeared above Lu Yang’s head. We were gone for just an afternoon. What exactly happened?

“Where did you get this mask from?”

Lan Ting swelled with pride. “Oh, it’s from the tofu shop lady boss who you saved last night. She even said that she wants to organize a collab event during the period of the Spring Harvest Festival. This is the event plan we drafted after discussion.

“When I was working yesterday, I realized that efficiency is too low with only two tiger-henchman ghosts working. Some customers get impatient from waiting. Hence, I designed this Automatic Barbecue Array to raise the efficiency by a significant margin.

“The Automatic Barbecue Array can be considered an innovation. When I return to the Celestial Palace, I can even use this to exchange for contribution points.

“This array is also simple. Who knows if I can promote it on a greater scale in the future?”

The Moon Laurel Celestial Palace was also similar to the Dao-Seeking Sect in that they had similar long-term missions.

Lu Yang, “...”

It looks like the rapid growth of the barbeque shop is inexorable.

Meng Jingzhou gleefully took a tofu mask. “This tofu mask looks pretty good. Come, one for each person. Lu Yang, look at how well this tofu mask complements you. Both of you are practically identical.”

Lu Yang stared at the square-shaped tofu mask and rolled his eyes as he accepted the mask. I won’t lower myself to the level of an idiot.

Lan Ting continued, “I also set up a Spirit-Energy Gathering Array, Soundproofing Array, and other arrays to aid in cultivation on the second floor.”

This was the only good news Lu Yang had heard ever since he stepped inside the shop. “That’s too expensive. Setting up the array requires many spirit stones right? Calculate how many you’ve used; the three of us will fork out the cost.”

Lan Ting waved her hand. “They’re all just pocket money.”

Meng Jingzhou suddenly raised his head, eyeing Lan Ting warily. It was his first time meeting an opponent in the field of flaunting one’s wealth.

With Lan Ting’s addition, the trio’s life became much more relaxed, and they could focus on searching for the talismans in the day.

Over the next ten days, the trio had managed to pinpoint the locations of more than two hundred talismans, and they were in the same positions as the nodes of the Lifespan-Reversal Array.

After determining the pattern, they went to other node positions and did end up finding more Lifespan-Reversal Talismans.

“What do we do? Should we inform Captain Wei?” Meng Jingzhou asked.

Lu Yang was in a dilemma.

If we tell Captain Wei the positions of the talismans, his superior will definitely know that someone is helping them in secret. Once Branch Leader Chu learns of this, he may suspect that it’s our doing.

But if we don’t tell him and leave the talismans scattered throughout Yanjiang Commandery, they will remain a threat.

“Waiter! Give us two hundred lamb skewers and two hundred beef skewers!” an unrestrained voice bellowed. Even the tiger-henchman ghosts in the backyard could hear it.

Normally, the information in this voice would have scared them out of their wits. However, with the introduction of the Automatic Barbecue Array, their workload had decreased appreciably. Two hundred lamb skewers and two hundred beef skewers? Even if you count in another two hundred pork skewers, we’re not afraid at all!

“Another two hundred pork skewers!” the spirited voice continued to shout. Whoever it was, they sounded wealthy.

Lu Yang narrowed his eyes, finding the owner of the voice to be somewhat familiar. “It’s One Zhang Red. He participated in the creed’s selection trials. The two behind him are also at the Foundation Establishment Stage like One Zhang Red is.”

These three people didn’t pass the selection trials.

“Would they recognize us? Man Gu asked. The three of us previously masqueraded as examiners and tricked One Zhang Red.

Lu Yang shook his head. “They won’t. The branch leader had mentioned before that to maintain the confidentiality of the branches, those who didn’t pass will have their memories erased. They no longer remember what transpired at the selection trials.”

With no one serving him for a while, One Zhang Red hollered in a gruff voice, “Where’s everyone? Are all of you deaf?!”

“Coming, I’m here! What do you wish to order, patron?” Lu Yang scampered over.

One Zhang Red's attitude was insufferable. “Two hundred each for the pork, beef, and lamb skewers. As for the rest, you can make the call. I heard from my grandfather that your food is the most delicious here. If it’s not tasty, I’m going to smash your store!”

Clearly, he hadn’t recognized Lu Yang. If he had, he would have directly smashed Lu Yang’s store.

Lu Yang greeted with a smile and bowed. “Please rest assured, our barbeque skewers will be so delicious that you wish you could eat them for your whole life.”

One Zhang Red snorted and didn't bother with Lu Yang. His two companions also closed their eyes and didn't deign to talk to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang transmitted an auditory message to Meng Jingzhou. “Inform Captain Wei that there are three rogue diabolic cultivators who are at the Foundation Establishment Stage. He can gather his men to arrest them.”

These rogue diabolic cultivators kill people like flies. They would have died countless times according to the law. Lu Yang was not going to be benevolent to them.

Let me show you the power of the diabolic path’s method—whistleblowing!

Meng Jingzhou was stunned. “We don't have evidence, right? How can we tell that they are rogue diabolic cultivators and also at the Foundation Establishment Stage? Will Captain Wei believe that?”

Lu Yang smirked. “What's not to believe? Just say that we noticed that he seems to be carrying talismans that cause people to fall asleep.”

Meng Jingzhou got Lu Yang’s cue. They had a few Lifespan-Reversal Talismans in their hands—perfect for framing others.

“Alright, I'll be right back.” Meng Jingzhou sprinted away.

~~~

After Captain Wei heard the news, he was shocked to hear that three Foundation Establishment diabolic cultivators had appeared and that they seemed to have Lifespan-Reversal Talismans in their possession. This is not a small matter!

He hurriedly reported it to Fang Qingyun.

After learning of the news, Fang Qingyun immediately led a huge group to surround and apprehend the three diabolic cultivators. Regardless of whether they possessed Lifespan-Reversal Talismans, three Foundation Establishment diabolic cultivators warranted such a massive operation.

Upon arriving at the barbeque shop, Fang Qingyun released the oppressive aura of a Golden Core cultivator, freezing One Zhang Red and his group in place. With a wave of his hand, he sternly ordered, “Take them down! Frisk them!”

Before One Zhang Red and the gang could register what was happening, several Foundation Establishment constable captains had already tackled them to the ground.

What on earth is going on? Is eating barbeque skewers in Yanjiang Commandery illegal?

Next, Captain Wei found a whopping number of Lifespan-Reversal Talismans on One Zhang Red, far more than the few talismans Lu Yang had planted to frame them with.

“It was indeed you guys who placed those Lifespan-Reversal Talismans!” Fang Qingyun glared at One Zhang Red. It’s all because of him that I didn’t get to rest for days.

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Wow, did you have to be this cooperative?

One Zhang Hong and his companions were even more baffled. Our execution has been flawless without leaving behind any traces. Why did the constables come to arrest us?

What exactly went wrong?!

Chapter 90: Interrogation Transcript

“Name?”

“One Zhang Red.”

“Be honest, I’m asking for your real name!”

“Zhang Little Red.”[1]

The oil lamp flickered inside the dingy interrogation chamber. Fang Qingyun crossed his arms as he sneered at the suspect they had just apprehended. Constable Captain Wei locked his gaze onto One Zhang Red as he fired one question after another, while a young constable diligently scribbled down the details of the interrogation at a table by the side.

“Gender?”

“Male.”

“Cultivation?”

“Great Perfection Apex Late Foundation Establishment Stage.”

Captain Wei snorted. “Jot down ‘Late Foundation Establishment Stage’ and skip everything before that. Zhang Little Red, I’m telling you now, if you think that fairness is compromised with us handling this case, you can request recusal, in other words, to have someone else take over. Do you want to request a recusal?”

“I request...”

Captain Wei made a drawn-out “Hmm,” his voice rising in pitch.

Zhang Little Red hastily corrected himself, “No no no, I’m not requesting recusal.”

“Tell me then, what got you in here?”

“Not paying for barbeque skewers?”

Fang Qingyun was annoyed. “Forget about interrogating him and execute him on the spot. We’ll just say that he violently resisted during arrest and would rather die than surrender, taking his own life with poison.” This was something Fang Qingyun was definitely capable of doing.

Still shackled, One Zhang Red hurriedly blurted out, “I’ll confess, I’ll confess. It was around ten days ago. I woke up at the bottom of a cliff. I probably slipped by accident when I passed by the mountain on the west side of Yanjiang Commandery. By the time I came to, I realized that I was in a mountain cave, likely a dwelling of some cultivator. It looked like nobody’s been there for a long time. I gingerly walked in, but apart from a book, I found nothing valuable.

“In fact, this was the book you confiscated when you frisked us. The book recorded some obscure talismans and complementary arrays. One example is the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman and Lifespan-Reversal Array. According to the description in the book, the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman can convert lifespans into cultivation for myself. I happened to be at a bottleneck stage, so I was hoping to break through in one go and advance to the Golden Core Stage. It will be carefree for me then. Besides, this breakthrough method can also allow one to extend their lifespan. It was too tempting.”

Fang Qingyun lashed out in ire. “I’ve consulted the commandery governor. Based on the scale of your setup, breaking through from the Foundation Establishment to the Golden Core Stage is nothing; it’s more than enough for you to break through from the Golden Core to Nascent Soul Stage!”

One Zhang Red grumbled inwardly, I know that it’s wasteful too, but I didn’t know of other methods.

Naturally, he couldn’t say that out loud. One Zhang Red pretended that he didn’t hear Fang Qingyun chiding him. “I’m a talisman cultivator myself, so it didn’t take long for me to master the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman. Setting up the Lifespan-Reversal Array is also not difficult. I just have to arrange the talismans in the shape of the array.

“Since the talisman’s effects on cultivators are undetectable and only induces sleepiness in mortals, it’s easily overlooked. Moreover, once the array is fully set up, there wouldn’t even be signs of sleepiness.

“However, the array requires too many talismans, so it’s impossible to paste them up in a short span of time. Fortunately, I met two companions. They are the other two people you’ve arrested.”

“Speaking of which, there’s something I find strange. Those two people aren’t from Yanjiang Commandery, but they happened to show up here, and they couldn’t remember the reason for coming. Anyway, we hit it off right away and decided to break through the Foundation Establishment Stage together.

“We were prudent in not leaving any traces and laying low when you were making a fuss to search for the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans. We felt that this place was becoming more dangerous, so we wanted to leave Yanjiang Commandery. Before we left though, we heard that there is a very famous barbeque shop here and wanted to give it a try. All of you turned up before the skewers were even served.” One Zhang Red’s face was contorted in bemusement. He just couldn’t figure out where they had slipped up.

Captain Wei naturally wouldn’t tell him that the zealous shop owner had reported them.

After the interrogation ended, Captain Wei ordered him to sign his name and fingerprint. “Write down your name at the bottom of every page. On the last page, write ‘I have reviewed the above statements and they are consistent with what I have said.’ After that, press your fingerprint wherever you sign.”

~~~

As usual, the next day, Captain Wei brought a silk banner. He was even wondering if he should set up an office at the barbeque shop and live there. The efficiency of capturing offenders here is much higher than patrolling all day! If this goes on, becoming the chief constable will be within sight.

“Shop owner Lu, your barbeque shop has good feng shui, outstanding people, and a prime place.”

Lu Yang gave a humble smile. “Whether the place is prime is secondary; what’s most important is having outstanding people.”

“Things have been too busy at the yamen lately. Once it’s less busy, I’ll see if I can apply to award you with an ‘Excellent Establishment’ wooden plaque.”

“That would be amazing. Here, I just boiled some water; have a drink while it’s hot.” Lu Yang enthusiastically poured a cup of water. “Why are you still so busy? Haven’t you caught the perpetrators?”

“Well, we have arrested the culprits and also found the place where one of them had confessed. It’s a deserted mountain cave. Some wanted criminals from the diabolic path probably hid in there before. After the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans are torn down from the locations, it should be considered case closed.

“The problem is the coming Spring Harvest Festival. By the looks of it, there will be twenty percent more people compared to the previous year. I wanted time off, but the chief constable didn’t approve of it. He said that I should patrol more during this festive period.”

“Feel free to come and take a break here if you’re tired from patrolling. Our shop will be operating as usual during the festival.”

After seeing Captain Wei off, Meng Jingzhou let out a long breath. “Finally, it’s over. The last few days had us on edge hunting for those Lifespan-Reversal Talismans every day. Maybe One Zhang Red saw how hard of a time we were having and came here to surrender himself.”

Man Gu paused for a moment. I don’t think this was what One Zhang Red really had in mind.

Lu Yang noticed that Lan Ting had been making some gestures for a while now and asked curiously, “What are you doing?”

Lan Ting didn’t even look up. “I’m experimenting with a new automatic skewering array where the bamboo skewers can automatically string the meat together.”

Lu Yang picked up a bamboo skewer with two fingers and lifted it pensively. Suddenly, he tossed a few pieces of meat into the air, then hurled the bamboo skewer out. Unfortunately, the bamboo skewer brushed past the meat without stringing them together.

Man Gu didn’t understand what Lu Yang was trying to do and thought that the latter was playing some new game.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. “Are you thinking of practicing covert weapon techniques by skewering meat with the bamboo skewers?”

Lu Yang smiled, implicitly affirming Meng Jingzhou’s conjecture.

Soon, Meng Jingzhou joined in the training and experimented with how he should apply precise force to skewer the moving pieces of meat in midair.

Man Gu hesitantly asked, “This...isn’t something the righteous path does, right?”

Lu Yang answered in a prim and proper manner, “That’s not quite right. Have you not heard of the saying ‘The bamboo clings to the green mountains unyieldingly, its roots firmly planted inside cracks of the rock. It stands resolute despite weathering through countless trials, unafraid of wind from the four directions?’

“Bamboo is resilient and refined—the mark of a humble gentleman. How could using bamboo as a weapon be considered a covert weapon? This is a weapon only a gentleman uses.”

Man Gu felt as if he had just seen the light. “So that’s how it is. Let me try too then.”

Lan Ting was focused on experimenting with her array, a few bamboo skewers hovering in midair. Whoosh! The skewers lodged themselves straight into the wall, their ends still vibrating.

Had the target been a person, they would have died.

“Its power is a bit too much.” Lan Ting scratched her head in frustration. I’ve already tried my best to reduce its power. “If I can’t make an automatic skewering array, I might as well crank the power up to the maximum.”

The two tiger-henchman ghosts trembled uncontrollably as they watched the scene of “devils dancing around madly.”

1. His real name is “Zhang Xiaohong.” The only character that is the same is “red” or “hong.” ☜

Chapter 91: After the Sun Extinguishes, It Is the Moon

Prior to Lan Ting setting up the Spirit-Energy Gathering Array, the trio had individually trained in a bid to enhance their Foundation Establishment cultivation. With the introduction of the Spirit-Energy Gathering Array on the second floor, the four of them now cultivated together. During their free pockets of time, they would even gain deep insights into cultivation through their exchanges with one another.

For example, Lu Yang learned that Man Gu couldn’t recite Words of Sages while in horse stance but could be in horse stance while reciting Words of Sages, and that Man Gu found the former to be a form of disrespect to the sages.

For example, Man Gu learned that Meng Jingzhou would often visit the brothel in the day and do nothing else but listen to songs in order to strengthen his mental power, something Man Gu found admirable.

For example, Meng Jingzhou learned that when Lu Yang had food stuck between his teeth, the latter would use cowhair sword qi to pick it out, which Meng Jingzhou found to be an entirely novel cultivation method.

For example, Lan Ting learned that the Central Continent was once refined from stars.

“Never have I once expected something like that.” Lan Ting was dumbstruck, though this new piece of information also helped to alleviate some of her doubts. Lan Ting pondered about it for a bit and figured that it wasn’t something she couldn’t share. “As all of you know, our name, Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, carries two layers of meaning. The first meaning is derived from the moon laurel trees that grow throughout the celestial palace. The second interpretation comes from the celestial palace’s belief that the moon holds some special significance.”

The Moon Laurel Celestial Palace was built atop a snowy mountain so that it could be as close as possible to the moon, a testament to the moon’s importance to the celestial palace.

“When I joined the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, I asked my shifu, “‘Why does the moon hold a special meaning? What about the sun and other stars? Can we draw power from stars such as the Big Dipper?’

“My shifu answered that the moon and sun are one. As for the other stars, she had simply smiled meaningfully without saying anything else. However, she would always smile like that when faced with something she wasn’t sure about, so I didn’t make much of it. Linking that with what you’ve just told me, I feel that she probably knew the truth about the stars.”

Lu Yang knitted his brow. “The moon and the sun are one?”

Lan Ting nodded. “I initially didn’t know what that meant until one time after class, I heard two of my senior sisters talking and mentioning ‘after the sun extinguishes, it is the moon.’”

“After the sun extinguishes, it is the moon?” Lu Yang was surprised. He had never heard of such a concept before.

Could it be the stars scattered across the sky are unreal shadow images while the sun and moon truly exist and are two sides of the same entity? It’s the sun when it blazes in the day, and it’s the moon when it extinguishes at night?

The sun’s energy is extremely terrifying. One theory is that the sun is the source of all living beings. Even now, there are people who harness the sun’s power to cultivate, visualize, or comprehend.

If the sun is the moon, what happens to all that energy after it extinguishes? This should be an enormous amount of power! Does the sun withdraw this energy into itself and transform into the moon at night?

“Come to think of it, why did the Ancient Nameless One refine all the stars except the sun?” Lu Yang muttered to himself. If the sun is gone, the world will be consumed by darkness, and countless beings will wither. According to Branch Leader Chu, the Ancient Nameless One had no regard for lives, so they probably wouldn’t have spared the sun out of benevolence.

Meng Jingzhou suddenly asked, “Have you heard of the Radiant Sun Creed?”

“Do you mean one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds?” Lu Yang hardly knew anything about them.

“That’s the one. The Radiant Sun Creed worships the sun, believing that it possesses some divine and wondrous power. When the sun reawakes, all things will perish, and they advocate for self-destruction before that happens so that they can head to the Kingdom of Elysium.” Meng Jingzhou added, “I don’t mean to be disrespectful to the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, but if the sun and moon are one, we can draw some similarities between the Radiant Sun Creed’s views and that of the Celestial Palace. Both believe that the sun and moon respectively hold a special significance and possess terrifying power.”

Lan Ting shook her head, not finding Meng Jingzhou’s words offensive. There were similar opinions within the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, including even more radical ones.

Meng Jingzhou voiced his conjecture, “Perhaps the Ancient Nameless One is hiding right inside the sun. Since time immemorial, the sun has been hanging in the sky without anyone questioning it. It’s a blind spot.”

Lu Yang offered another theory, “Or it could be that the sun contains such immense power within that even the Ancient Nameless One was unwilling to touch it.”

That said, no matter what the truth is, the sun and moon are definitely not as peaceful as they appear to be.

“Never mind, let’s not think about it anymore. It’s the Spring Festival after all; let’s go out and have some fun.” Meng Jingzhou gave up on ruminating over the issue further and encouraged everyone to take some time off. Rather than overthinking it now, I should just go home and ask the elders. Those people surely know more than I do. Just like how they kept their mouths tight despite knowing that I have a Single’s Spirit Root, even telling me that I’ll find out once I get to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

With the Spring Harvest Festival coming up, the festive mood had intensified. Various shops ran their own events, preparing to receive a flood of customers. The barbeque shop was also in the preparatory phase, offering complimentary tofu masks with each purchase of skewers, which was a hit among the children. Small colorful flags decorated the whole street, a tradition in Yanjiang Commandery that was funded and organized by the authorities. They were meant to symbolize the colors of spring to welcome the season.

It was said that Commandery Governor Li had specifically instructed for the flags to be set up quickly to avoid disrupting the daily lives of the civilians, deploying much manpower in the process. In reality, it wouldn’t have affected the civilian’s normal routine. Commandery Governor Li was just putting on a show for the people.

Meng Jingzhou smiled. “These small flags really add to the festive atmosphere.” Even the entrance of the barbeque shop had a small red flag planted there.

“Come check this out! These are all rare books!” An old man with yellow teeth was hawking on the street, drawing the group’s attention.

“What books do you have?”

“Martial arts secret manuals, limited editions of cultivation techniques, you name it.” The old man grinned.

Meng Jingzhou casually browsed through the collection. Suddenly, his eyes lit up as he found a martial arts secret manual. “Lu Yang, look! This book is perfect for you. If you’re willing to cultivate this, I guarantee you’ll reach the highest level.”

Lu Yang looked at the cover.

Toad-Style Kungfu.

“Get lost!”

Soon, Lu Yang also came across a secret manual and recommended it to Meng Jingzhou. “This secret manual is practically tailor-made for you. If you’re willing to cultivate this, it’s possible for you to become a Martial Immortal in the future!”

Meng Jingzhou looked at the cover.

Sunflower Manual. [1]

The two exchanged glances and chuckled, “kindly” buying the secret manual for the other party.

Man Gu saw that the first page of the Sunflower Manual wrote “One who wishes to practice this kungfu must first self-castrate.” He couldn’t help but ponder, Can’t women practice this martial art?

On the other hand, Lan Ting was oblivious to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou’s banter for she was engrossed in reading a classical zhanghuiti novel. [2]

The story was about a renowned courtesan who pursued true love and entrusted her life to a scholar in order to buy her freedom and quit the trade. However, the scholar was weak and selfish. Although he loved the courtesan, he was embarrassed to marry a courtesan as his wife. Under his friends’ instigation, he eventually betrayed the courtesan, culminating in the tragic ending of the courtesan drowning herself in the river.

Tears streamed down Lan Ting’s eyes as she found the courtesan’s fate to be very pitiful.

Noticing how immersed Lan Ting was in the story, Lu Yang craned his neck to have a peer. He also found the story to be vivid and touching.

He tilted his head to look at the title of the book.

Dream of the Green Brothel Chamber. [3]

Lu Yang, “...”

He found the title to be particularly amusing.

1. Written for a eunuch for eunuch. ☜

2. Zhanghuiti is a type of long-form classical novel. The Four Classic Novels of China are famous examples of this. ☜

3. There are two jokes here, First, it is a reference to one of the Four Classics, Dream of the Red Chamber. Second, “green chamber” here also literally means “brothel.” ☜

Chapter 92: Cultivators’ Bazaar

The four of them purchased the respective books they had taken a liking to. Out of a fascination for history, Man Gu had bought a copy of The Wild Unofficial History of Great Xia. Inscribed were numerous stories that even an insider like Meng Jingzhou found wild. Regardless, the four of them were satisfied with their choices.

As they continued sauntering, they began to realize that there were increasingly more cultivators in proportion to mortals in the crowd, as if some mysterious force had separated these two groups.

Lan Ting transmitted an auditory message to the other three, “An expulsion-type array has been set up nearby. Cultivators are unaffected, while mortals will involuntarily distance themselves.”

Meng Jingzhou immediately associated it with the news he had heard during his usual stroll. “It’s the monthly bazaar! They’re likely opening early for the upcoming Spring Harvest Festival.”

The Spring Harvest Festival attracted both mortals and cultivators alike.

They were currently at a proper bazaar, not a black market where killing and looting were common occurrences; in fact, they could even see constables patrolling the area. That said, there were still some people masking their faces and wearing black robes to conceal their identity.

This was nothing surprising. Some cultivators hid among mortals. If they showed their faces around here, wouldn’t that be akin to exposing their identities?

Lu Yang and gang were such examples.

The four had concealed their identities in different manners.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu chose to wear black robes because they found them to be cool; Meng Jingzhou even cackled sinisterly to add to the vibes.

Lan Ting removed her Shapeshifting Talisman, revealing her original peerless appearance which she donned whenever she was searching for clues about the diabolic creeds in Yanjiang Commandery.

Lu Yang tried to persuade Meng Jingzhou, “Why don’t I use the Animal Form Fist to turn into you?”

Meng Jingzhou responded by smacking a tofu mask onto Lu Yang’s face.

And thus, Lu Yang put on a tofu mask.

Inside the bazaar, it was quite the ambiance for cultivators, completely different from that of the outside world. A gigantic protective barrier enveloped the whole bazaar, emitting a soft glow. Cultivators who hadn’t seen each other in a while stopped by at roadside taverns to have a drink while freely exchanging news of their recent encounters. Vendors and cultivators would also get into quarrels over the prices, each of them haggling to squeeze out a few more spirit stones from the other party. The authorities had even put up an arena where cultivators could fight it out to their heart’s content.

“Come check this out! Ultra-Strength Pills concocted from an ancestral secret technique! One pill to gain infinite strength!”

Lu Yang was intrigued. He followed the voice and found himself at a medical clinic. It looks like this medical clinic is run by cultivators. I wonder if the one hawking is an apprentice or a pill-concocting master.

“How many spirit stones for one pill?”

The pill-concocting master’s apprentice replied, “Ten spirit stones for one. Buy three, get one free; buy five, get two free.”

Since the price was affordable, it implied that the pill’s target audience was Qi Training cultivators rather than Foundation Establishment cultivators like Lu Yang. Nonetheless, Lu Yang wanted to buy two pills as keepsakes; it was his first time seeing someone else not from the Dao-Seeking Sect concocting pills. “What about its effects?”

“It can boost your strength for a short span of time, but after the effect wears off, you’ll be left in a weak state for half a day.”

Lu Yang bought one pill. Just as he was about to leave, he saw a constable enter, and it was someone he recognized. The constable’s surname was Sun, and he was Captain Wei’s sidekick.

“I received a report that your Ultra-Strength Pills involve false advertising.”

The pill-concocting apprentice was stunned. False advertising?

Constable Captain Sun solemnly explained, “According to the law, one is not allowed to use words such as ‘limit’ and ‘most’ when advertising their products. Through our investigation, we found that your Ultra-Strength Pills are only suitable for cultivators at Level Three Qi Training Stage and below with no observed effects of ‘infinite strength.’ After this warning, we expect you to make the relevant amendments.”

The pill-concocting apprentice nodded compliantly. After Lu Yang left, he heard the voice from the medical clinic again, “Come check this out! Ultra-Strength Pills concocted from an ancestral secret technique! One pill to gain finite strength!”

Lu Yang suddenly thought to himself, Senior Brother Wu Ming’s Ten-Buffalo Strength Pills are really flawless. They don’t even face common problems like false advertising.

As for Meng Jingzhou, not only was he well-informed, but there were also fairly legitimate pill-concocting masters at home, so he wasn’t very interested in common items.

“What is this?” Meng Jingzhou picked up a small item from a stall; it encompassed two wooden sticks glued together. “For making jianbing guozi? [1] Even something like this is sold at the bazaar?”

The stall owner was a middle-aged man with a full beard with a calm and stern visage. He had been resting with his eyes closed. Upon hearing Meng Jingzhou, he reluctantly opened his eyes, exuding the aura of a great artifact-crafting master. “This item is called the Flying Apsara[2] Rod. Place it on the top of your head and activate it with spirit energy, and it will spiral upward to the sky. Level Seven Qi Training Stage is sufficient.”

Meng Jingzhou was astonished. This little bazaar is truly full of hidden dragons and crouching tigers in hiding to have hidden gems such as this great artifact-crafting master.

Without special means, cultivators have to be minimally at the Golden Core Stage to fly high up in the sky. If we consider special means, however, Lu Yang can already fly on his sword at the Foundation Establishment Stage, or he can use Animal Form Fist to turn into an immortal crane. That would let him fly too. In any case, barring special circumstances, the point stands that the minimal requirement for cultivators to fly is the Foundation Establishment Stage.

I’ve never heard of a Level Seven Qi Training Cultivator being able to fly. Since their power would be sparse at this stage, it would be challenging for them to command flying enchanted treasures.

“You don’t seem to believe it. That doesn’t matter, I’ll demonstrate it once for you.” The bearded middle-aged man confidently took out a wooden puppet. He tied the Flying Apsara Rod to the wooden puppet and shot a wisp of spirit energy from his fingertip at the Flying Apsara Rod.

As if it had just woken up from its slumber, the Flying Aspara Rod began rotating slowly. It then sped up until only a blur remained. Together with the wooden puppet, the Flying Aspara Rod flew upward.

There appeared to be no problem.

However, if one had to insist on picking out a problem, it would be that as the Flying Aspara Rod spun, the wooden puppet would spin along with its head as the pivot and its body twirling at the same breakneck speed as the Flying Aspara Rod!

Had it been a human underneath the Flying Apsara Rod, their brain juices would probably have blended into a mixture!

“See, I told you that my puppet is of supreme quality. It doesn’t come apart even when whirling at such rapid speed. I’m not trying to brag, but this puppet of mine can even hold its own when faced with a Foundation Establishment cultivator. The price is also a bargain. I'll give you a one-time offer of just eight hundred!”

“Give it to your grandpa!” Meng Jingzhou finally caught on to the other party’s tactic. He’s just promoting his puppet under the banner of the Flying Apsara Rod!

Evidently, the bazaar was riddled with trickery and schemes. Honest people like Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were becoming rare nowadays.

Lu Yang and the other three planned to head to the district under the Luodi Merchant Guild. It was supposed to be more regulated, and they hoped that they wouldn’t meet with similar scams again.

“Dear customers, would you like to have your fortune told?”

Lu Yang turned back and saw that it was a fortune teller with a bagua flag behind him who had called out to them. The flag wrote “Vaticinate not heaven and earth but people.” The business seemed to be dismal with not a customer in sight.

Noticing that he had caught the attention of Lu Yang’s group, he added, “No need to pay if it’s inaccurate. Do you want to give it a try?”

Lu Yang scrutinized whatever he had on his table: a bagua compass, dice, Four Treasures of the Study,[3] nine copper coins, a crystal ball...

Everything that is even slightly related to fortune-telling is on display.

Is this reliable?

And why is there a crystal ball?!

1. Jianbing guozi is a type of Chinese street food. You can try to imagine it as fried pancake skin wrapped into a roll with fillings inside. It is softer on the outside and partly crunchy on the inside. ☜

2. Apsara is a type of celestial being that flies in Buddhism. ☜

3. The Four Treasures of the Study refer to the brush, ink, paper, and inkstone. ☜

Chapter 93: Fortune-Telling

The fortune teller was a cultivator around the same age as Lu Yang. Upon noticing Lu Yang’s gaze, he begrudgingly explained, “I have no choice. People nowadays don’t really believe in fortune-telling. They keep chanting things like ‘fate lies in my hands, not the heavens’[1] and ‘I am the master of my own destiny.’ It’s honestly hard to make a living.

"Some people prefer to use the bagua compass for divination, so I prepared one.”

“Some people want to predict their luck in gambling, so I prepared dice.

“Some people find logomancy to be accurate, so I prepared the Four Treasures of the Study.

“Some people think that tossing copper coins is the most effective, so I prepared nine copper coins.

“And this crystal ball? It’s a trend that emerged in the East Sea in recent years. Since people like to use crystal balls for fortune-telling, I even specially traveled to the East Sea to pick up a thing or two. Besides, this crystal ball can not only perform divinations, it also secretly plays short videos. One tool for twice the income.

“How about it? Do you want to choose one and give it a try? No need to pay if it isn’t effective,” the fortune teller touted his services fervently.

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou peered at the fortune teller in suspicion as they put on their guard. They couldn’t help but feel that the fortune teller was not as simple as he seemed. It looked like he had seen through something.

It was Man Gu’s first time encountering a fortune teller, and he found it very interesting. “Can you tell my fortune?”

The corners of the fortune teller’s mouth curved into a smile. “Sure, which divination method do you prefer, and what do you want to inquire about?”

Man Gu contemplated for a bit, taking into account that he was a Confucian cultivator. “Let’s go with logomancy then. I’ll write a character, and you’ll analyze if I can become a great Confucian scholar.”

“Please write.” The fortune teller skillfully laid out the calligraphy tools and invited Man Gu to begin.

Man Gu deftly wrote a character, his brush flying across the paper.

The fortune teller tapped on it and let out a long hiss, “Your character...”

“What’s the problem?” Man Gu asked anxiously.

“Your handwriting is so ugly. What character is this?”

“Ru for Confucian.”

Despite being speechless, the fortune teller collected himself and evaluated, “The Confucian is one who embodies softness, often referred to as a skilled savant. Its character encompasses the ‘human’ radical, and ‘xu’ guides its pronunciation.[2]

“You have a strong body and appear to be indestructible, yet you actually possess a soft heart. You are vacillating, taking in everything at face value and imitating everything you learn.

“Look at the character for ‘xu,’ which means ‘need’. It is made up of the character ‘rain’ at the top and ‘will’ at the bottom. As the adage goes, ‘Clouds gather in the sky; when the need arises, it will bring about rain at the right time.’ This implies that you will be needed by others in the future.

Notice that the radical for ‘human’ stands to the side. This suggests that not only can you become a great Confucian scholar, you can even become a new style of a great Confucian scholar.”

Man Gu was over the moon to hear that he could become a great Confucian scholar. His level of Confucianism ranked one of the lowest under Fourth Elder. However, Fourth Elder didn’t mind it and firmly supported the notion of “education without discrimination,” claiming that Man Gu had simply not become enlightened yet. As long as Man Gu achieved enlightenment, Fourth Elder was confident that Man Gu would be able to comprehend the Dao of Confucianism in one go, his future one of boundless opportunities.

In spite of all that, Man Gu kept losing confidence. After hearing the fortune teller’s analysis which asserted that he could become a great scholar, Man Gu regained his confidence.

I do have great potential!

”Oh, there’s one more thing.”

“What?”

“Practice your writing more when you get back.”

“Oh.”

“Do you need a copybook? I happen to have one right here. You should take one. This is a necessary expense for your journey to becoming a great Confucian scholar.”

Man Gu felt that he made a lot of sense, so he bought the copybook.

Seeing that Man Gu was done, Lan Ting also got interested in giving fortune-telling a try and sat down. “I want to know whether I’ll have greater achievements in arrays or talismans. Let’s use the crystal ball.”

She hadn’t focused much on arrays recently, yet her interest in arrays seemed to have surpassed that in talismans. That prompted her to contemplate whether she should change her area of specialization.

The fortune teller raised the crystal ball toward Lan Ting, rubbing it with both hands as he chanted, “Heavenly spirits, earthly spirits, crystal ball, show yourself! Heavenly spirits, earthly spirits, crystal ball, show yourself!”[3]

When he saw the results displayed by the crystal ball, he was completely floored. “Uh, in the future, you will write arrays on talismans, combining arrays and talismans into one?” He cast a strange gaze at Lan Ting. What kind of unorthodox thought process is this? This female cultivator is peerlessly beautiful, but why are her ideas so different from those of normal people?

Lan Ting tilted her head, finding that the fortune teller’s words were not without merit, so she readily paid him.

It was now Meng Jingzhou’s turn. He raised an eyebrow. “Are you a disciple of the Heaven Strategy Sect?”

The Heaven Strategy Sect was the number one fortune-telling sect on the Central Continent. They had once prophesied the time of resurgence of the Great Ancient Era. As they were a sect that emphasized karma, ordinary identity concealment methods were practically ineffective in front of them. All it took was a glance for the disciples of the Heaven Strategy Sect to discern the other party’s background.

Perhaps this fortune teller has managed to identify that we come from the Dao-Seeking Sect and Moon Laurel Celestial Palace.

“Haha, junior brother, you must be mistaken. I am but a free spirit and idler. How could I possibly be a disciple of the Heaven Strategy Sect?”

Meng Jingzhou fell silent for a bit. Then, he took out a blood contract scroll from his identity jade pendant. “Three hundred years ago, the grand elder of the Heaven Strategy Sect borrowed a large sum of top-grade spirit stones from the Meng Family. He couldn’t repay it and hid inside a cave abode, claiming that he was in absolute seclusion.

“When we went to the Heaven Strategy Sect to collect the debt, your sect leader signed a blood contract, promising to repay it. Furthermore, when any direct descendant of the Meng Family meets a disciple of the Heaven Strategy Sect, they can demand repayment with this blood contract.

“Do you want to test the power of this blood contract?”

Lu Yang had heard that the Meng Family was the creditor of the world. It looks like this rumor didn’t come out of nowhere.

The fortune teller plonked himself to the ground with a thud, hugging Meng Jingzhou’s leg as he burst out crying, “Big Brother Meng, please have a sliver of mercy; maybe we’ll cross paths again in the future!

“Our sect is so poor that the disciples have to leave the mountain and eke out a living for ourselves. If I, Luo Bu, had the money, I wouldn’t have been reduced to scamming people here! To make things worse, setting up a stall requires a fee, and I can’t even afford that!” Luo Bu bewailed his poverty. “Look at the magua I’m wearing![4] I’ve been sewing and mending this for many years. I don’t even have the money to replace it!”

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes. It’s so obvious that this magua has been refined and fetches an exorbitant price.

“I’m not expecting you to pay up, so get up first.” Meng Jingzhou forcefully extricated his leg. “Give the two of us a free reading, and I will let it slide. Remember, don’t lie!”

“Hahaha, that’s not difficult.”

“Come come come! What are my destiny and future achievements like?” Lu Yang spread his hands, allowing Luo Bu to read his palm.

Luo Bu laughed heartily, confident as usual in his domain of expertise. “That’s a common question. Let me take a look then.”

To their surprise, Luo Bu’s eyes widened, and he sprung up. Incredulity distorted his face as he stumbled a few steps backward until he hit the wall. “You...you...what’s with your destiny? It’s all hazy. In the future, you will be entangled in karmic ties with several immortals!”

Despite all these karmic entwinements, he can still move freely, as if he isn’t affected!

And that’s not the most terrifying part.

The most terrifying thing is that this guy will be a scourge in the cultivation world, propagating the ethos of the Dao-Seeking Sect through the entire cultivation community! The Dao-Seeking Sect’s ethos is already outrageous; if the whole cultivation world gets brainwashed, how are people going to survive?!

I definitely mustn’t get myself involved in any karmic entanglements with someone like this!

Luo Bu whined inside his heart. I saw that the four of them came from the Five Great Immortal Sects, perfect lambs for slaughter. I thought I could cheat some money out of them, but I totally didn’t expect that there’s someone like this guy who I certainly can’t mess with!

Wait, from the palm reading, this guy isn’t the only one who will be spreading toxic influence to the rest of the cultivation world; someone else is in cahoots.

This other person is...

Luo Bu looked toward the major creditor, Meng Jingzhou.

I better run right now!

Without any hesitation, Luo Bu activated an escape spell, not even bothering to pack up the items on the table. “I...I...I didn’t see all of you today!” He was worried that staying even a moment longer might cost him his life.

Before the four could register what was happening, Luo Bu had already escaped without a trace.

Lu Yang blamed Meng Jingzhou, “You must have scared him off with your debt collection!”

1. This is a very common phrase found in Chinese novels and shows. ☜

2. This phrase is adopted from the explanation of the word for “scholar” or “Confucian” in the book Shuowen Jiezi, a Chinese dictionary compiled by Xu Shen during the Han Dynasty around the 2nd century. Another point to note is how Chinese characters are structured. For the sake of simplification, we can understand it as complex characters containing a radical that confers the “meaning” of the character and a phonetic component that provides an idea of how the whole Chinese character is pronounced. ☜

3. Up until the part before the crystal ball, this is a common incantation used. ☜

4. Magua is a style of buttoned jacket worn by males in the Qing dynasty. ☜

Chapter 94: Could This Be That Legendary Book Which Hides

Not a stranger to Lu Yang’s skills in the art of framing and accusations, Meng Jingzhou retorted in disdain, “What do you mean I scared him away? Didn’t you hear him say that you will be involved in karmic entanglements with immortals in the future? I bet you’ll do something that triggers the wrath of the immortals so much that they unite against you!”

Lu Yang waved his hand dismissively. “That’s impossible. I know myself; I wouldn’t go that overboard. It must be an excuse Luo Bu fabricated.”

The two kept passing the buck to each other, resolute in not admitting any fault of their own.

Man Gu tried to open his mouth. Could it be that the problem lies with both of you? However, he held those words back in the end.

After a few days of interaction, Lan Ting had gradually become familiar with Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s style of speaking, so she treated their argument as mere background noise.

“Look, it’s the Luodi Merchant Guild. Let me take you there for a tour!”

At the entrance of the Luodi Merchant Guild was a small, chubby pig holding a coin. This display was none other than the merchant guild’s classic mascot.

Lu Yang had long heard of the Luodi Merchant Guild’s resounding reputation and wanted to take a look around.

The interior of the merchant guild was tastefully decorated in a subdued manner, exuding a palatable elegance as opposed to other chambers of commerce that tried to flaunt their wealth in every way possible with their ostentatious decorations.

The Luodi Merchant Guild had no need for showing off; its name alone spoke volumes. Everyone on the Central Continent knew that they were the number one merchant guild.

The assortment of goods on display left Man Gu dazzled. There were pills meticulously crafted by masters, spirit treasures painstakingly crafted by artisans, natural materials and treasures unearthed from perilous places by fearless ones, and the gamut of talismans and arrays from simple to complex...

When Man Gu saw the price tags, he felt like he was a pauper. Despite noticing that Meng Jingzhou and Lan Ting were casually strolling around without fretting over the prices, he found it somewhat acceptable. However, he was flabbergasted that his Brother Lu, whom he thought was of a similar financial status, appeared indifferent to the prices.

Man Gu silently asked, “Brother Lu, the things here are so expensive. I can’t afford any of them.” That was naturally an exaggeration; what he couldn’t afford were those impressive-looking items suitable for Foundation Establishment cultivators.
