Lu Yang stared at Man Gu in astonishment. “Why would you want to buy the things here? Look at all these pills, magical treasures; they may look opulent and extravagant, but they’re actually just for show. In terms of practicality, can any of them compare to what our sect produces?”

Man Gu nodded. True indeed. Our sect’s youtiao are cheap, sturdy, and chewy. More than a month has passed, yet Brother Meng still hasn’t finished eating the youtiao Brother Lu gave him, with half remaining.

“Besides, if we have no money, can’t we try to earn some? With our status, we can make money just by selling any random thing. Just watch, I’ll demonstrate.”

Lu Yang approached an attendant quietly standing at the side. “Excuse me, do you accept spells here?”

The attendant replied respectfully, “Greetings, yes, we do accept spells. However, we only accept those that are not available in our merchant guild. We have all the common cultivation techniques here. May I know if you are looking to sell a cultivation technique?”

Lu Yang nodded. “I have a shapeshifting technique here. One can shapeshift and attack at the same time. It’s a family secret of mine.”

The attendant was astounded. I’ve been working here for ten years, but I’ve never heard of such a shapeshifting technique.

“Please come with me. There’s an auction today, and master appraiser Yang Xuanling is overseeing it. We will ask him to assess the value of your shapeshifting technique.”

The four were brought into a room. An elderly man with glasses had his head buried in a book, looking like an experienced and knowledgeable person.

The attendant whispered into Yang Xuanling’s ear.

“Oh? There’s such a spell? I got it. You may withdraw.”

“Understood.” The attendant retreated from the room deferentially.

“I heard that you four have a shapeshifting technique that allows one to shapeshift and attack at the same time?” Yang Xuanling asked.

“That’s right.” Lu Yang took out a copy of his Lu-Style Animal Form Fist.

Yang Xuanling paused for a moment. “...Unless my eyesight has deteriorated to the point of misreading things, the book seems to write ‘Animal Form Fist?’”

Lu Yang stepped forward and crossed out the words “Animal Form Fist” and changed it to “Shapeshifting Technique.”

“It’s now a shapeshifting technique.”

It was Yang Xuanling’s first time meeting someone who named things so casually. When you have worked long enough, you truly get to meet all kinds of people.

Yang Xuanling slowly turned the page and analyzed every single word, flying into a rage. “This is just Animal Form Fist!”

“How could that be?” Lu Yang was nonplussed. “This is definitely a shapeshifting technique. Let me demonstrate it to you!”

Lu Yang delivered a set of Animal Form Fist on the spot, turning from Man Gu into Meng Jingzhou, then into the tiger demon, his strikes imposing and looking to be radiating with immense might.

Yang Xuanling stared at him wide-eyed for a long while, utterly baffled by how Lu Yang had transformed. He’s indeed using Animal Form Fist. The process matches exactly with what is written in the book. He also didn’t secretly use any other spells.

How much should this be valued at?!

Yang Xuanling stroked his beard, appearing to have understood everything. “Your shapeshifting technique is indeed interesting. It would be a waste to sell it as a regular item on display outside. Why don’t we take this shapeshifting technique book to the auction? There’s one happening in a bit.

“That works.”

At the auction site, Lu Yang spotted an old acquaintance.

It was none other than Chi Xulong, who had mastered his wondrous stone-spitting technique.

Chi Xulong didn’t disguise himself. True to his previous self-introduction, he was flamboyant and hated pretense. With his notable cultivation in the whole of Yanjiang Commandery, it was not surprising that he didn’t see the need for disguise.

A person in black robes sat beside Chi Xulong, someone who Lu Yang guessed was the killer, Shen Jinyi.

Lu Yang decided to sit beside Chi Xulong. When the latter saw the childish tofu mask, he snorted in contempt. For some reason, he felt a surge of anger coursing through him at the sight of the other party.

The well-dressed auctioneer stepped onto the stage. From his resonant and clear voice which didn’t rely on cultivation, it was evident that he had been professionally trained.

“Good afternoon, everyone. Thank you for coming here to support us. Without further ado, let’s get started.

“The first item for auction today is three Foundation Establishment Pills.”

At his words, the entire venue stirred restlessly; they hadn’t expected the auction to kick off with such a priority item.

Many of those attending the auction were at the Intermediate or Advanced Qi Training Stages; the Basic Qi Training cultivators were aware of their limited finances and wouldn’t attend the auction. Even Foundation Establishment cultivators felt tempted; after all, whose family didn’t have a junior at the Qi Training Stage?

Though Lu Yang was apparently not one of them. After musing for a bit, he realized that out of the people he knew, his cultivation was the lowest.

When the ancient forebears forged a new path of cultivation, they naturally didn’t rely on external objects. However, breaking through to the Foundation Establishment Stage by themselves posed enormous risks; countless people had perished in the process. Later, someone developed Foundation Establishment Pills that not only enhanced the efficiency of hitting the Foundation Establishment Stage but also ensured that failures wouldn’t leave behind hidden potential dangers or cause one’s cultivation to regress. Even Lan Ting had taken Foundation Establishment Pills when she was trying to break through to the Foundation Establishment Stage.

She transmitted an auditory message, “Did all of you use Foundation Establishment Pills?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “Our philosophy on taking pills is quite advanced. When one is trying to break through to the Foundation Establishment Stage, they would directly ingest the raw materials for the Foundation Establishment Pill, using their own bodies as pill furnaces to refine the raw materials such that the medicinal effects can be thoroughly absorbed into the meridians.

“Our research has shown that this method yields the highest absorption efficiency. When Seventh Elder of the Pill Cauldron Peak was young, he had tried to break through to the Foundation Establishment Stage a hundred times to arrive at this conclusion, so the data is absolutely reliable. At the time, Seventh Elder was even conferred the title of 'Strongest Foundation Establishment Cultivator.’ However, due to his overly solid foundation, he later faced excruciating pain during his Golden Core formation process, as if he had gallstones.”

Lan Ting, “...”

While the two were conversing, the three Foundation Establishment Pills had already been auctioned off.

“Next up for auction is a shapeshifting technique.” The auctioneer presented the book Lu Yang had just submitted.

Lu Yang softly exclaimed, muttering to himself just loud enough for Chi Xulong to hear, “Could this be that legendary book which hides...”

Despite originally showing no interest in the book, Chi Xulong perked up at that moment.

Chapter 95: How Could There Be a Spy From the Righteous Path in the Everlasting Creed?!

A wave of sighs swept through the audience. Although shapeshifting techniques were hard to pick up, they were very common and had no auction value at all.

There were a few exceptions who didn’t sigh. One example was Lu Yang. Another example was Chi Xulong.

The auctioneer continued introducing the item, “This is not a book on an ordinary shapeshifting technique. During the transformation process, one can also make an offense. If you use this shapeshifting technique in a battle, I believe it could produce unexpected results.”

Only then did the crowd become slightly more interested, though not by much. After all, who would use a shapeshifting technique in the middle of battle?

The auctioneer reminded, “Something to note is that this shapeshifting technique is extremely difficult to master. Even master appraiser Yang Xuanling remarked that while this book appears nondescript on the surface, it is far more complex than what meets the eye!”

Lu Yang continued to mutter to himself just loud enough for Chi Xulong to hear, “As I thought, this book seems too similar to that legendary book.”

As Meng Jingzhou was seated beside him, he heard Lu Yang murmuring to himself and hastily whispered, “Shut up! You can’t say things like that out loud! When can you break the habit of muttering to yourself?!”

Lu Yang appeared to be visibly startled as he immediately closed his mouth and fixed his gaze on the shapeshifting technique book technique on stage.

Chi Xulong observed Lu Yang from the corner of his eye, growing more certain of his suspicions.

“The starting bid is one hundred spirit stones!” The price was far below that of a typical shapeshifting technique, indicating that even the merchant guild was likely unsure about the value of Animal Form Fist.

“One hundred and ten!” Someone quickly placed a bid. To them, this little bit of spirit stones probably meant nothing to them, and it wouldn’t hurt to buy something unusual out of novelty.

“One hundred and twenty!” Chi Xulong lazily called out.

“One hundred and forty!”

“One hundred and eighty”

“Two hundred!”

The price of Animal Form Fist soared rapidly.

“Eight hundred!” Lu Yang shouted.

Meng Jingzhou hurriedly held Lu Yang’s hand down. “Why are you bidding so high? Are you afraid that people won’t notice you?!”

“I...I was just afraid that someone else would win it.”

Eight hundred spirit stones might not be a considerable sum for a Foundation Establishment cultivator, but it was not the same for Qi Training cultivators.

“One thousand!” A voice rang out from beside Lu Yang.

Lu Yang stared at Chi Xulong in shock, as if he couldn’t understand why the other party was competing with him for the transformation technique book.

It’s clearly just a technique that appears to have some special traits! Could the other party also have discerned something? But how did he figure it out? Lu Yang beat himself up. Could he have heard me muttering to myself just now?

Lu Yang whispered to Chi Xulong, “Fellow Daoist, this book seems to be one that has been long lost in my family. Could you let me have it? I will definitely reward you generously after the auction!”

Chi Xulong snickered. Long lost? Only ghosts would believe you! There are definitely ancient secrets hidden in this book!

Shen Jinyi wanted to say something to persuade him but decided to stay silent upon seeing Chi Xulong’s firm stance.

Since the negotiations didn’t seem to work, Lu Yang decided to raise his bid, saying, “One thousand and two hundred low-grade spirit stones!”

“Two thousand.” Chi Xulong didn’t even bat an eyelid. With how the other party is bidding so timidly, he’s definitely not at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Lu Yang went all in, “Two thousand and three hundred low-grade spirit stones!”

“Three thousand.” Chi Xulong remained as nonchalant as ever.

Lu Yang turned to Meng Jingzhou. “Lend me one thousand spirit stones. I promise I’ll pay you back next year!”

“Alright,” Meng Jingzhou readily agreed.

“Three thousand and three hundred low-grade spirit stones!”

“Four thousand!”

Lu Yang continued to borrow money, but his efforts were futile in the face of Chi Xulong’s wealth.

In the end, Chi Xulong won the shapeshifting technique book with an astonishing bid of eight thousand spirit stones, while Lu Yang shed hidden tears of joy at having earned eight thousand spirit stones. It was a win-win situation for both, leaving everyone satisfied.

After the auction ended, Lu Yang and the others had just arrived at the foot of a desolate mountain when they were blocked by Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi.

“What...what are you trying to do?!”

The corners of Chi Xulong’s mouth twisted into a cruel smile. “What do you think I want to do? Don’t play dumb with me, kid. No one has ever fooled me before!” Chi Xulong took out the copy of Lu-Style Shapeshifting Technique and released his aura waves of a Foundation Establishment cultivator. “Tell me, what ancient secret is hidden in this book! Speak the truth, and I’ll spare your lives. If you dare lie, don’t blame me for being ruthless!”

That said, Chi Xulong had no intention of letting the four of them go. The fewer the people who know about this, the better. Besides, this girl is gorgeous; I must play with her before killing her!

Since these four people can’t even fork out a few thousand spirit stones, they must be at the Qi Training Stage, and Qi Training cultivators stand no chance before me!

Lu Yang sighed. I remember that Branch Leader Chu reminded me to stir up more trouble during the Spring Harvest Festival. Could Branch Leader Chu have already foreseen today’s situation and was hinting to me to kill Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi?

Nothing escapes Branch Leader Chu’s masterful strategy!

Lu Yang removed his mask, revealing his true appearance. “Chi Xulong, we don’t have to make things so tense between us, right?” Then, he stealthily took out a recording orb.

“Lu Yang! Die!” Chi Xulong burst into anger, instantly realizing that Lu Yang had been toying with him. Everything that happened at the auction was a play staged for me!

“There must be some misunderstandings between us. Some vile person is surely trying to sow discord. How about this, let’s go to Branch Leader Chu and clear things up. Even if you don’t believe me, you should at least trust Branch Leader Chu, right?”

At the mention of Branch Leader Chu, it only further incurred Chi Xulong’s wrath. “How dare you bring up Branch Leader Chu? You have no face to do that! He must have been hoodwinked by you to let you become an administrator. What vile person are you talking about? You are the vile person!”

“Me, a vile person? Don’t talk nonsense!” Lu Yang desperately tried to defend himself.

Chi Xulong sneered. “Don't think I don’t know that you motherf*cker have done all those dirty deeds! In front of Branch Leader Chu, you pretend to be a goody-two-shoes and a yes-man, but ever since you joined the creed, everything you’ve done has been to sabotage us. I suspect you’re a spy sent by the righteous path!”

Naturally, Chi Xulong had uttered those words in a fit of anger. If he had really thought that Lu Yang was a spy from the righteous path, he would have been secretly monitoring Lu Yang for evidence a long time ago.

Lu Yang let out a long sigh and put away the recording orb. Pulling out his Qingfeng Sword, he reluctantly said, “In that case, it seems like the only option left for us is to fight.”

Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi curled their lips in contempt as they readied their weapons.

Meng Jingzhou, Man Gu, and Lan Ting did the same.

The battle commenced.

~~~

Lu Yang brought the news of Chi Xulong’s and Shen Jinyi’s demise to Branch Leader Chu.

No matter how strong Chi Xulong and Shen Jinyi were, there was no way they could survive against four disciples from the immortal sects. It was a one-sided crushing defeat. The two died so gruesomely that Lan Ting lost her appetite.

As Lu Yang presented the recording orb, he explained to Branch Leader Chu, “You know Chi Xulong’s temper; he kills at the slightest disagreement. I was worried that something like this would happen, so I prepared the recording orb in advance, lest he comes to you complaining about his grievances and that I am mistreating him.

“But it looks like he wouldn’t be able to do that now.

“I’m not sure what went wrong with the recording orb; it recorded intermittently. Fortunately, it can still roughly reflect the situation at that time. Please take a look.”

Sitting in his jade chair, Branch Leader Chu picked up the recording orb and watched the scenes unfold.

“Chi Xulong, we don’t have to make things so tense between us, right?” Lu Yang tried his best to salvage the relationship between the two of them.

“Lu Yang! Die!” Clearly, Chi Xulong did not appreciate the gesture.

“There must be some misunderstandings between us. Some vile person is surely trying to sow discord. How about this, let’s go to Branch Leader Chu and clear things up. Even if you don’t believe me, you should at least trust Branch Leader Chu, right?”

“Branch Leader Chu...let you become an administrator...the vile person!”

“...a vile person? Don’t talk nonsense!” Lu Yang tried to convince him with logic.

“Don't think I don’t know...motherf*cker...done all those dirty deeds!”

“...Branch Leader Chu...pretend to be a goody-two-shoes and a yes-man...joined the creed, everything has been to sabotage us...I suspect...a spy sent by the righteous path!”

The recording ended here, leaving Branch Leader Chu gnashing his teeth.

Lu Yang spoke up indignantly, “Branch Leader, even if we are from the diabolic path and have our share of rivalries and instances of fury, I know to repay kindness. You’ve treated me well, so when I saw Chi Xulong framing you and Shen Jinyi not attempting to stop him, rage swelled in my heart. Overwhelmed by anger, I got Meng Jingzhou and the others to kill him together! It wasn’t convenient to record during the fight, so I put away the recording orb.”

Lu Yang naturally wouldn’t let Branch Leader Chu see their fighting styles.

Branch Leader Chu commended him loudly, his voice laced with ire toward Chi Xulong, “Well done killing them! Those two bastards deserve to die!”

Branch Leader Chu was aware of Chi Xulong’s dissatisfaction toward him, but on the account that Chi Xulong was a talent, he had called him over to offer him some advice. At the time, Chi Xulong had even pledged loyalty, claiming that he would do better than Lu Yang. But now, it seems like Chi Xulong still harbored resentment inside his heart. To think he even made such absurd statements like accusing me of being a spy from the righteous path.

How could there be a spy from the righteous path in the Everlasting Creed?!

“Lu Yang, you’ve done me a great service by eliminating two major threats! I’ll make sure to put in a good word for you when the inspecting officer gets here!”

Chapter 96: Long Vacation

“I have received a message from the inspecting officer. He said that he had long heard of the Spring Harvest Festival and has brought forward his agenda to arrive in Yanjiang Commandery during the festival. You need to be mentally prepared; don’t be timid in front of the inspecting officer.”

“Understood.”

When Lu Yang was leaving the Yanjiang Branch, he saw other administrators like Wang He and Bai Zifang walking in his direction. They nodded at him slightly in greeting. This newly promoted administrator, Lu Yang, is Branch Leader Chu’s favorite; we mustn't offend him.

Wang He and the others had worked in the branch for several decades and were thus privy to certain matters. They speculated that Branch Leader Chu had directly appointed Lu Yang and the other two because of their impressive performance during the selection trials, especially Lu Yang, who might have received the highest appraisal among the three.

Wang He muttered, “The branch leader has always been a materialistic person who doesn’t rise early if there are no profits to be gained. It’s very likely that he is aware that Lu Yang will rise to greatness in the future, so he wishes to build a good relationship with Lu Yang before his prominence to attain better chances of promotion.

They knew that the branch leader’s biggest ambition was to rise in rank to become the branch leader in an economically prosperous region. Hence, he placed particular significance on the upcoming visit by the inspecting officer.

“Perhaps the reason for summoning us this time is related to the inspecting officer.”

“Speaking of which, the branch leader still lacks a criterion for promotion, right? Has he reached the Nascent Soul Stage?”

Not only was one’s faith in the Everlasting Immortal an important metric for promotion, the Everlasting Creed also paid attention to one’s cultivation.

“Who knows? Maybe he has already long reached the stage but simply didn’t tell us. He never explains to us what he does, and we also don’t know the intentions behind his actions.”

Branch Leader Chu’s style reflected the whole diabolic creed’s style—steeped in distrust. Although Branch Leader Chu seemed to trust Lu Yang, in reality, he had never revealed any information about himself to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang hardly knew anything about Branch Leader Chu.

~~~

The Spring Harvest Festival arrived, and the barbeque shop’s customer traffic peaked. Many foreign merchants had already discovered business opportunities with the barbeque shop and proposed to Lu Yang to open branches. Lu Yang would provide the recipe, while they would provide the funds.

Without any exception, Lu Yang shooed them away with a stormy expression.

There were also cultivators who wanted to dine and dash, but when they saw the three silk banners hanging on the wall, they swallowed their unrealistic ideas and paid up obediently.

With the help of the automatic barbeque array, the two tiger-henchman ghosts had more time to skewer. This allowed the barbeque shop to operate smoothly despite receiving more customers than usual.

“One More Time Barbeque Shop...yes, it’s this one! My aunt told me that the food here is especially delicious and that if I come to Yanjiang Commandery, I must try it at least once!”

“Look, this shop is also running a promotion.

With every purchase in our shop, you can collect a voucher and receive a 10% discount at the tofu shop on Qianmen Street. Spend one silver to participate in the spin-to-win wheel once; chances can be accumulated with no upper limit. Prizes are limited and available on a first-come first-served basis.

“Come on, let’s try it.”

The two lined up at the back of the snaking queue, unsure how long they had to wait.

At the entrance of the barbeque shop, Meng Jingzhou was extremely busy working on the spin-to-win wheel. The lucky wheel read “One More Time,” “Third-Tier Prize,” “Second-Tier Prize,” “First-Tier Prize,” and “Special Prize.”

“Congratulations to this customer for winning the second-tier prize. You can enjoy 60% off your current bill! Let us give him a round of applause!” Meng Jingzhou clapped enthusiastically, looking even more jubilant than the prize winner.

“A first-tier prize has appeared! This customer’s entire bill is on the house!”

“Special prize! Someone actually won the special prize!”

The customer was surprised to have won the special prize and asked gleefully, “What is the special prize?”

Meng Jingzhou held the customer’s hand and ardently said, “Congratulations, you’ve won a chance to experience being a waiter at our shop! Others have to pay for the experience and joy of working as a waiter here, but you’re very lucky. You get to experience it for free!

“Considering that the smoky and scorching backyard may be an unpleasant environment for you, our professional staff will carry the skewers to the entrance of the backyard for you so that you won’t have to go to the backyard!” Meng Jingzhou had an expression that said “No need to thank us for our thoughtfulness.”

The customer asked, “...Can I exchange this for the first-tier prize?”

“No.”

The customer rejected the special prize.

Up until now, Meng Jingzhou still hadn’t successfully duped anyone into accepting the special prize, but he enjoyed the process of trying to dupe others.

Inside the barbeque shop, Lu Yang carried a tray as he weaved in and out among the customers. His steps were light and his movements agile. With his stable lower body, the tray with the skewers remained steady and upright, never bumping into customers, as if he could traverse through a garden of flowers without touching a single leaf. After more than a month of training as a waiter, his footwork had improved by a large margin.

“Advisor Ma, Registrar Chi, how’s the food?” Lu Yang greeted the two customers with a smile. The two customers were commandery officials who often came here for some skewers and drinks.

“Delicious as ever! Shop Owner Lu, if you ask me, your skills are wasted here; you should open shops in larger commanderies. I guarantee that you’d make more than you do now!”

“Jeez, stop talking nonsense. Didn’t you hear that Shop Owner Lu isn’t even opening a branch? It’s clear that he opened the shop out of interest and not in it for the money.”

Lu Yang could only smile apologetically, “Hope the both of you enjoy the Spring Harvest Festival.”

The two were clearly tipsy, their cheeks flushed red. Advisor Ma poured out all his grievances, “Just speaking of the Spring Harvest Festival makes me angry. It was originally a seven-day holiday, finally a long vacation, but I don’t know whose brilliant idea it was to cut it down to just three days!

“What can you even do in three days? They even have the nerve to palliate it by calling it a ‘short long vacation.’ Just listen to that! Does it even make sense? When the word ‘short’ is added before ‘long vacation,’ does it still count as a long vacation?

“I wish whoever came up with this term ‘short longevity!’”

Registrar Chi hurriedly covered Advisor Ma’s mouth. “You can’t casually say things like that! You came late, so it’s understandable that you don’t know, but this was Commandery Governor Li’s idea!”

Advisor Ma scoffed. “So it’s him. Not much ability but plenty of ideas!”

Registrar Chi was more informed and shared, “Keep your voice down! You can’t speak ill of Commandery Governor Li now. I heard that he has found a path for himself and apprehended three vicious diabolic cultivators in the commandery. With such a great meritorious achievement, he is bound for promotion soon. Chief Constable Fang Qingyun will be taking over his position!”

Advisor Ma’s mouth twitched in disdain for Commandery Governor Li. In any case, Commandery Governor Li wouldn’t care about a small fry like me. “A few days ago, a coworker was complaining to me that Commandery Governor Li randomly issued an order for the yamen bailiffs to work overtime in the wee hours, demanding that all small flags be set up in one night with not a single mistake in their positions. He even put on an act by personally acting as the supervisor to oversee them. He doesn’t need sleep as a Golden Core cultivator, but others do! Many of the yamen bailiffs fell asleep while working!”

Lu Yang poured wine for the two. “I’ll be attending to other matters.”

“Go ahead, Shop Owner Lu, you don’t need to worry about us.”

On the first night of the Spring Harvest Festival, the four people and two ghosts were completely drained.

Before sleeping, Man Gu recalled something. “If I'm not wrong, ghosts don’t need to sleep. Should we arrange work for them at night too?”

Chapter 97: Notch the Boat To Find What Again?

Lan Ting was originally used to sitting in a meditative state instead of sleeping at night, but ever since she joined the barbeque shop, she had developed the good habit of sleeping at night.

When the four of them woke up, they felt rejuvenated, and this was partially due to the array set up by Lan Ting.

“Let’s go! I still haven’t had enough fun!” Meng Jingzhou was the most energetic, trying to wake Lu Yang up as if he were chasing a pig.

Lu Yang kicked Meng Jingzhou before reluctantly getting out of bed.

Man Gu had risen the earliest and had already gone to the market to stock up. He prepared a pot of Dough Drop Soup, cracked in four eggs, and added a few drops of sesame oil, filling the entire hall with a fragrant aroma.

Lu Yang liked vinegar, so he added a small spoonful of vinegar to his soup. After the four of them finished their meal, they set off, feeling invigorated.

It was still somewhat early, but the streets were already teeming with tourists. Lu Yang heard that the inns were long fully booked, and many people chose to stay in guesthouses. People’s faces were wreathed in jovial smiles; children wore tofu masks of a similar design to Lu Yang’s, holding large pinwheels as they jumped about, while parents grabbed their children’s hands tightly, fearing that they might get lost.

“It’s as lively as a temple fair.”

“Have you heard? Someone brought a colossal creature from the southern region; it’s right by the river! Let’s go check it out!” someone shared the news with their companion excitedly.

Overhearing their conversation, Meng Jingzhou couldn’t contain his curiosity and led the three of them to the riverbank to see the colossal creature.

The four of them arrived at the familiar Big Stone Bridge once again, but the difference was that they stood on it this time. Small flags were planted all along the bridge’s sides.

Upon seeing the colossal creature, Meng Jingzhou was disappointed. “I thought it would be something extraordinary; turns out it’s just an elephant.”

Every year, the banks of the Hidden Dragon River were a gathering place for tourists. With someone now showing off an elephant to attract attention, even more curious onlookers had congregated in the area.

Lu Yang had certainly seen elephants before. As Meng Jingzhou and Lan Ting came from aristocratic families, they had encountered more strange things than Lu Yang had ever heard of. Since Man Gu had lived in the wilderness, he had even hunted and killed elephants.

However, most people didn’t have similar experiences to the four of them. They were extremely interested in colossal creatures like the elephant.

A tourist marveled, “Is this a demon beast? It’s so huge, and it even has such a long nose and teeth?”

The owner of the elephant, a Foundation Establishment cultivator, explained, “It is indeed a demon beast, but it’s hard to gauge the cultivation level of demon beasts; it should be roughly at the Level Six Qi Training Stage. However, its size has nothing to do with being a demon beast. This type of living being is called ‘elephant,’ and they all grow this big upon reaching adulthood.”

The tourist continued to ask, “How heavy is a huge creature like this?”

The elephant’s owner involuntarily chuckled. Who knows? It’s not like there’s a scale big enough to weigh it.

Another tourist suggested, “Since we happen to be right next to the river, we can place the elephant on a large boat and mark the spot where the water level rises to. Afterward, we can load the boat with stones. Once the marked spot touches the water again, we can weigh the stones to find out how heavy the elephant is.”

The elephant’s owner also wanted to know how much his spirit pet weighed and readily agreed.

Under the owner’s command, the elephant was chased onto a boat. However, it was too heavy for the boat in shallow water, so the owner paddled the boat to the river’s center and took out a small knife, notching the spot where the boat contacted the water surface.

Just as the owner was about to paddle back, the elephant happened to lift its head and spotted Man Gu, getting startled instantly.

Demon beasts were highly sensitive to aura waves. Since the Ancient Barbarian Tribe often hunted elephants in the wilderness, their intrepid killing intent flowed through their bloodline. Although the elephant didn’t understand the deeper reason, it couldn’t help but feel a chill creep into its heart—this stemmed from a bloodline suppression.

In a frenzy, the elephant fell into the water with a splash, sinking straight to the bottom.

The people by the banks gasped in confusion, urging the elephant’s owner to quickly save the elephant. To their surprise, the elephant’s owner calmly marked the spot where the elephant had fallen. “This is where the elephant fell into the water.”

The crowd was perplexed, but the elephant’s owner didn’t bother explaining. When he was about to reach the bank, he pointed at the mark and shouted, “My elephant fell from here, and it’s still right here!”

Everyone burst into laughter, thinking that he was joking.

Suddenly, the river churned, and a whirlpool appeared. The elephant flew out from beneath the mark, flapping its large ears.

It was an endemic species limited to the southern region—the Giant Flying Elephant.

Witnessing the whole scene unfold before him, Man Gu furrowed his brow before hammering his palm in realization. “I remember now! We learned this idiom in class—this is called ‘notch the boat to find the elephant!’”[1]

I now have a profound understanding of this idiom.

Lu Yang, “...”

What on earth did you learn in class?

Meng Jingzhou laughed. “I remember when we first found the first Lifespan-Reversal Talisman under the bridge, I was really shocked to learn that such a thing existed. Fortunately, we had already reported it.”

Lu Yang was about to join in on Meng Jingzhou’s joke when the small flag before him suddenly caught his attention. The smile faded from his visage, as if he had recalled something. He pulled the flag out, frowning as he examined it under the sunlight. Upon witnessing how the small flag appeared under sunlight, a chill seized his heart.

“What’s wrong?” Meng Jingzhou noticed something off with Lu Yang when he didn’t hear Lu Yang tease him back for a long time.

Lu Yang’s expression grew grave as he pointed at a faintly indiscernible pattern on the small flag. “Look at this pattern. What does it remind you of?”

“The Lifespan-Reversal Talisman?!” Lan Ting was the first to react as she was the most familiar with the pattern.

Meng Jingzhou widened his eyes. The pattern on the small flag was almost indistinct; it was hardly perceptible without direct sunlight. Even if someone could see it, tourists would most likely think of it as a special feature of the Spring Harvest Festival. How many people would know what the symbol of the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman looks like?

“Don’t panic! Maybe the Lifespan-Reversal Array hasn’t been completely set up yet!” Meng Jingzhou convinced himself to remain composed.

Lu Yang calmly analyzed, “That’s impossible. Don’t forget that it’s not just one or two of these small flags, the whole Yanjiang Commandery is planted with such flags!”

Who could have thought that the small flags with the Lifespan-Reversal Talisman’s design are hidden among the ordinary flags?!

Lu Yang continued, “In other words, the Lifespan-Reversal Array is already completed and is blatantly displayed in front of everyone, but no one has noticed it yet!”

“Then why hasn’t the array been activated?” Meng Jingzhou recalled that apart from arranging Lifespan-Reversal Talismans to form the Lifespan-Reversal Array, one other condition was a blood sacrifice. It’s a cinch for the culprit to kill a few people; after all, he dares to even set up the array! What is he waiting for?

Lu Yang coldly stated, “He is waiting for people. There aren’t enough people at the Spring Harvest Festival yet; countless more are currently heading toward Yanjiang Commandery!” The Lifespan-Reversal Array robs the lifespans of mortals, converting them into cultivation for the one who set up the array. The more mortals it plunders from, the greater the boost in cultivation!

Meng Jingzhou also made the link. “According to tradition, on the second night of the Spring Harvest Festival, people would gather to sing on the streets, feast by the river, and conduct performances!”

Today was the second day of the Spring Harvest Festival.

1. The original idiom is ‘notch the boat to find the sword,’ and refers to being inflexible to change or clinging to outdated ideas. ☜

Chapter 98: Fail-Safe Plan

As more and more people congregated on the Big Stone Bridge, Lu Yang suggested that they leave the place first and find a more secluded spot.

When the four arrived in the remote mountain forest, Lu Yang took out the map of Yanjiang Commandery which marked the nodes of the Lifespan-Reversal Array they had previously deduced. “The nodes of the Lifespan-Reversal Array should still be in the same position. Before we proceed, I would like to confirm something. Lan Ting, when you mentioned ‘blood sacrifice,’ do you mean killing people at the nodes or offering cultivators’ essence blood to activate the array?”

Lan Ting was confused by Lu Yang’s question. “Both methods are possible, but the former would usually be opted for since it only requires the killing of mortals. If too much of a cultivator’s essence blood is used, it would affect their cultivation and be detrimental to their future training.

Lu Yang pondered for a bit. “Then the person who set up the array would likely use the second method.”

The other three were bewildered. They believed that the person who set up the array could only be a diabolic cultivator. For a diabolic cultivator, killing people would naturally be much more convenient than using essence blood.

Lu Yang challenged, “Who do you think has such influential power to hide the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans within the small flags and deliberately have them completely set up overnight to benefit from the cover of the night since no one would be suspicious even if someone got sleepy?”

The answer instantly clicked in Meng Jingzhou’s mind. “Someone from the authorities, and of high rank at that!”

Lu Yang nodded. “That’s right, or to be more specific, it’s the commandery governor!”

“What?!”

The color drained from Man Gu’s and Lan Ting’s faces, while Meng Jingzhou was not that taken aback, having already made similar speculations. Back when they just entered Yanjiang Commandery, Meng Jingzhou had already mentioned that it wasn’t uncommon for the authorities and diabolic path to collude with each other.

“Last night, I overheard people from the authorities saying that Commandery Governor Li personally oversaw the placement of the small flags, demanding that there must be no mistakes with their positions.”

“Would something like this really require the commandery governor’s personal supervision? Even the excuse that he was meticulous and dedicated to the people is too far-fetched!”

“This can only mean that Commandery Governor Li had made use of these small flags to set up a Lifespan-Reversal Array that covers the entire commandery!”

Man Gu suddenly realized how dark the world truly was. “That is to say that the spy planted by the Yanjiang Branch in Yanjiang Commandery is Commandery Governor Li. With his cultivation and position, the term ‘collaboration’ would be more apt to describe their relationship, right?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “He’s neither a spy nor a collaboration partner. I suspect that Commandery Governor Li and Branch Leader Chu are the same person! I don’t have any direct evidence, but there are two points of suspicion.

“First, Branch Leader Chu always summons us at night. I checked with the other administrators, and they said that it’s not the case in the other branches.

“Second, both Branch Leader Chu and Commandery Governor Li are about to be promoted, and the timings are nearly identical.”

Man Gu drew in a breath of cold air. The world is even darker than I had thought. If Branch Leader Chu and Commandery Governor Li are the same person, doesn’t that mean he is taking advantage of both the righteous and diabolic paths?!

“Of course, they might still be two different people. Ultimately, this is just speculation. But regardless of which possibility it is, the way to activate the Lifespan-Reversal Array is definitely not killing mortals!”

Man Gu still hadn’t fully wrapped his head around it, so Meng Jingzhou explained, “Commandery Governor Li is looking forward to his promotion. If a mass slaughter goes rampant during the Spring Harvest Festival, do you think he’ll still get that promotion? Even if he is connected to the higher-ups, they still can’t blatantly promote him under such circumstances. Besides, with his position of commandery governor, how hard would it be for him to obtain essence blood from cultivators? He could easily pick a few cultivators from the prison.”

Lan Ting still had some questions. “Regarding Commandery Governor Li and One Zhang Red setting up the Lifespan-Reversal Array, is it a coincidence, or are they related?”

“I believe they are closely related,” Lu Yang postulated. After figuring out the relationship between Branch Leader Chu and Commandery Governor Li, Lu Yang gained new perspectives on many matters.

“Capturing three Foundation Establishment diabolic cultivators alone is clearly an immense political achievement for Commandery Governor Li. If there is no diabolic branch, a small commandery wouldn’t have that many Foundation Establishment diabolic cultivators. It would essentially be equivalent to wiping out the leaders of the diabolic cultivators in a commandery.

“After the Lifespan-Reversal Array is activated, things might not be discernible on the surface, but over time, people will definitely start to notice something amiss.

“If One Zhang Red hadn’t acted first, the authorities would have spared no efforts in tracking down the culprit. Had that been the case, Yanjiang Branch and Commandery Governor Li would have been at risk of getting exposed.

“Commandery Governor Li was clever enough to arrange for One Zhang Red’s role. With One Zhang Red involved with setting up the Lifespan-Reversal Array first, even if Commandery Governor Li activates the array and reduces the lifespan of the mortals, the authorities would only place their sights on One Zhang Red.”

Man Gu was astounded. “But One Zhang Red didn’t succeed.”

Lu Yang snickered. “Not succeeding is only One Zhang Red’s side of the story. Maybe the array has been activated, but due to One Zhang Red’s improper handling, only reducing lifespans without boosting one’s cultivation is highly probable. After all, it is an unfamiliar array; any accident can happen.”

Man Gu still couldn’t grasp the full situation. “But One Zhang Red’s two companions could have also verified whether the setup was successful.”

Lu Yang objected, “Companions? Since when did diabolic cultivators have companions? They’re just mutually exploiting one another. It’s totally reasonable for One Zhang Red to not have told those two people the truth.

“With such an obvious suspect readily available, who else could they suspect? Besides, based on One Zhang Red’s lengthy list of crimes, the death penalty is inevitable. By the time the authorities realize that the Lifespan-Reversal Array has been activated, One Zhang Red might already have been sentenced to death. Who would still suspect Commandery Governor Li when there is a scapegoat like One Zhang Red around?”

Meng Jingzhou and Lan Ting nodded repeatedly at Lu Yang’s viewpoint.

Lu Yang questioned again, “Also, are there seven nodes that require a blood sacrifice?”

Lan Ting looked at Lu Yang in astonishment and nodded. How did Lu Yang know that? Didn’t he say that he doesn’t understand arrays?

“When I left last night, I encountered seven administrators; Branch Leader Chu had summoned them on short notice, probably because of some mission. I figured that it was to assign them the task of carrying the essence blood to the nodes and waiting for the right moment.

“How about you tell us more about the Lifespan-Reversal Array?”

Lan Ting didn’t hesitate and circled seven points on the map of Yanjiang Commandery. “These seven places are the key nodes for activation. They are located near scenic spots in Yanjiang Commandery, and the array’s focal point is...halfway up Pine Mountain!”

Using the Lifespan-Reversal Array to break through would naturally require a desolate place.

“Let’s remove some of the Lifespan-Reversal Talismans first to prevent the array from activating. However, in doing so, it is highly possible that we’ll attract the attention of Branch Leader Chu. Rather than waiting for him to come after us, we should set an ambush beforehand and catch him off guard,” Lu Yang proposed.

As Lu Yang had been worried that they might have to fight Branch Leader Chu, he had purposely not left their combat styles recorded by the recording orb.

The other three felt uneasy. Branch Leader Chu was at the Golden Core Stage; when the time came, it would be a fight to the death.

“Can we report this to the authorities? Inform Fang Qingyun about this?” Man Gu asked.

Lu Yang shook his head. “Once Fang Qingyun finds out about the arrays on the small flags, he’ll definitely link it to Commandery Governor Li, and if Commandery Governor Li gets caught, our identities as members of the diabolic creed will also be exposed.”

Lan Ting hesitatingly said, “But with just the four of us against a Golden Core cultivator, I’m afraid it’ll be hard to defeat the other party.”

On the contrary, Lu Yang was pretty confident. “Not to worry. Let’s just prepare ourselves to the fullest. If the worst-case scenario happens, I still have a fail-safe plan.

“What is it?”

“Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist!”

When Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu heard what he said, their expressions changed drastically. Lan Ting didn’t understand their extreme reactions. “What is Big Senior Sister Animal Form Fist?”

Lu Yang proudly replied, “It’s the ultimate technique of the Lu-Style Animal Form Fist!”

Lan Ting nodded, despite not truly understanding.

Chapter 99: The Most Powerful Weapon From the Merchant Guild

Fang Qingyun yawned out of sheer boredom. It was less than one hour until the grand festivities of the Spring Harvest Festival. Fortunately, they had made thorough preparations, including various kinds of contingency plans, and so far, there hadn’t been any unexpected incidents.

When Fang Qingyun heard about an elephant falling into the water and flying out again, he dispatched someone to issue a warning—flying without authorization was not permitted in the commandery as it was too much of a hazard. Furthermore, demon beasts entering the commandery needed to be put on record, so the elephant’s owner had to comply in taking his elephant for registration.

Such trivial matters took up Fang Qingyun’s entire day.

“I hope nothing goes wrong tonight. I hope no one lights a bonfire and causes a forest fire. I hope there are no stampedes from watching performances. I hope no one gets jealous and starts a street fight...” Fang Qingyun rambled on, listing all the incidents that had occurred in previous years.

“Qingyun, I’ll be heading off first.” Commandery Governor Li notified Fang Qingyun before leaving.

“Take care,” Fang Qingyun replied with greater respect than usual as he had heard that there would be no new leaders appearing out of nowhere this time. It’s all thanks to Commandery Governor Li’s kind words that I’m able to take over his position. I must remember this favor.

Commandery Governor Li wasn’t obliged to be present during the Spring Harvest Festival, but he did so anyway since it could reflect his diligence and leave a laudable reputation for himself. A good image was something he had always cherished. He discovered that it was easier to get promoted by saying nice things compared to doing actual work. There were also requirements for one’s cultivation when it came to promotion; it was an unspoken rule in officialdom.

It’s soon! Once I rise to the Nascent Soul Stage today, both my statuses as commandery governor and branch leader will change. At such thoughts, Commandery Governor Li’s steps became lighter.

He walked into a narrow alley, first changing his face before putting on a mask. That way, even if someone removed the mask, they would think that what lay beneath was his true appearance and wouldn’t suspect his identity as Commandery Governor Li.

Caution is indispensable when navigating both the righteous and diabolic paths.

Based on his talents, he wouldn’t have reached the Advanced Golden Core Stage. However, due to his associating with both the righteous and diabolic paths, he had access to resources far beyond what ordinary people could imagine, which led to his current accomplishments. In the past ten years, he realized that he had hit a bottleneck and wouldn’t be able to progress to the Nascent Soul Stage through ordinary means. In order to advance in both status and cultivation, he thought of the Lifespan-Reversal Array.

“Strange, the inspecting officer should have arrived in Yanjiang Commandery before noon. Why hasn’t he shown up yet?”

Commandery Governor Li, or rather, Branch Leader Chu, was a bit disgruntled at the inspecting officer’s tardiness after donning the mask. He had specifically told the inspecting officer to come before noon today because there was a surprise for him. The so-called surprise was inviting the inspecting officer to activate the Lifespan-Reversal Array together to have their cultivation enhanced at the same time.

“Could something have happened? I even specially waited until the optimal time when there’s the most number of people to activate the array. Oh well, since he isn’t coming, I’ll just elevate my own cultivation.”

Pine Mountain was remote, with trees sprawling in all directions, and the mountain paths were formed from the steps of travelers. People coming to enjoy the Spring Harvest Festival wouldn’t bore themselves by venturing to such a place.

Branch Leader Chu concealed his aura waves as he walked toward Pine Mountain. The further he went, the fewer tourists he saw. By the time he reached the foot of the mountain, there was already not a single person in sight. Finally, he stopped at a flat zone. The surrounding branches were hung with talismans that were slightly different from ordinary Lifespan-Reversal Talismans; they would serve as the array’s focal point.

He sat cross-legged, adjusting his state as he waited for the moment the array would activate. He had already sent six administrators to carry out the tasks with regard to the blood sacrifice. Calculating the time, the right moment was exactly now!

“Lifespan-Reversal Array, activate!” Branch Leader Chu raised his hands.

With him as the center, silent and invisible power spread outward from the array. When they reached a certain point, however, they halted abruptly.

“Someone has pulled out the flags!” Branch Leader Chu was momentarily dazed, but he quickly regained his senses to understand what had happened.

This isn’t an ordinary case of a few flags being pulled out by chance. The other party is definitely knowledgeable about the Lifespan-Reversal Array, otherwise, they wouldn’t have been so precise!

“Who is it?! Someone from the authorities? That doesn’t seem right, nothing from the authorities can escape my attention. Is it a traveler I am not aware of? Or could it be...Lu Yang?! He has seen the Lifespan-Reversal Array before!”

Lu Yang is an idiosyncratic person. He’s very well capable of such a thing! Branch Leader Chu’s gaze turned frigid. This is tantamount to severing my path ahead; it’s even more painful than killing me!

“Hmm? Is that how you view me, Branch Leader Chu?” Lu Yang’s lazy voice rang out from nearby.

“Lu Yang!” Branch Leader Chu’s anger flared up upon seeing Lu Yang. “Don’t think that just because the creed leader thinks highly of you means that I can’t kill you. It’s all too common to have diabolic cultivators dying from accidents. You have given me the perfect reason to do so!”

Lu Yang pondered for a bit and replied earnestly, “Didn’t you tell me to stir up trouble during the Spring Harvest Festival? I figured that the biggest trouble would be getting rid of the commandery governor. Look at what a coincidence it is! I followed the commandery governor for several days and ended up finding out that you are the commandery governor. I was thinking that it would only be right to carry things through, so I might as well get rid of you at that. Isn’t this also our diabolic creed’s tradition of disrespecting the superiors?” Lu Yang said gleefully.

“You’re courting death!” Branch Leader Chu’s fury erupted.

“How could that be? I still want to live forever.”

“You're a mere Foundation Establishment cultivator, yet you dare to make such audacious statements? Die!” Branch Leader Chu struck with his palm, the force so terrifying that it pulverized the trees it touched into powder!

Lu Yang swiftly escaped to a distance with Shrinking Earth. Branch Leader Chu suddenly stomped on the ground with his right foot, sending earthquake-like vibrations through the ground. The earth overturned, and Lu Yang was also hurled out along with it.

Shock gripped Lu Yang’s heart. So this is the power of an Advanced Golden Core cultivator. He tossed me out with just a kick. “Tsk, so hard to deal with.”

Branch Leader Chu moved like lightning, nimbly closing in on Lu Yang. His hand formed a fist seal with the force of its fist-like gale, bent on hammering Lu Yang to death.

Lu Yang held the Qingfeng Sword upright in front of himself. As long as Branch Leader Chu landed his hit, the Qingfeng Sword would be able to cleave his knuckles!

Branch Leader Chu immediately retracted his fist, opting for a kick instead. Having anticipated it, Lu Yang countered with a kick of his own. As the two legs clashed, Lu Yang flew out with the momentum!

Branch Leader Chu tried to launch another attack, but he found that he couldn’t draw his spirit energy at all, as if it seemed to be shackled.

“This is similar to the Spirit-Energy Disabling Array from the prison! As I thought, you understand arrays!” Branch Leader Chu glowered at Lu Yang. Although he was unable to manipulate his spirit energy, just his physical body’s defense alone would make it challenging for Lu Yang to harm him at all!

Lan Ting had temporarily set up the Spirit-Energy Disabling Array, and Lu Yang’s intention had been to lure Branch Leader Chu to this place. Lu Yang grinned and waved goodbye to Branch Leader Chu.

Branch Leader Chu scanned his surroundings but found nothing unusual. Suddenly, he raised his head and saw a flying vessel hovering above him.

It was the flying vessel Meng Jingzhou had just purchased from the merchant guild.

As it was now nighttime, it was so dark on Pine Mountain that even shadows were hardly perceptible, otherwise, Branch Leader Chu would have long noticed the shadow he was in.

The space above the Spirit-Energy Disabling Array similarly forbade the use of spirit energy, and the flying vessel lost its power. As it plummeted rapidly, Meng Jingzhou jumped down with a parachute.

Due to Branch Leader Chu’s inability to use spirit energy, his speed was limited and he would be unable to evade the flying vessel. On the contrary, Lu Yang had calculated the appropriate distance and hid far away.

The flying vessel fell from a low altitude like a meteor, heading straight for Branch Leader Chu!

Boom!

As it crashed to the ground, it kicked up dust everywhere and produced a deafening rumbling sound as the whole Pine Mountain shook. There seemed to also be explosives inside the flying vessel, which detonated upon impact. Pillars of flame soared into the sky with an ear-splitting explosion.

Lu Yang gave Meng Jingzhou a thumbs-up. “It’s great to have money; you can buy a flying vessel whenever you want!”

Meng Jingzhou also gave him a thumbs-up. “If not for them only having one flying vessel available, I would have bought several more!” Any treasure from the merchant guild was no match for the force of a flying vessel crashing down directly.

Just as Fang Qingyun was feeling nostalgic about the tranquility of time passing by, he witnessed a flying vessel plunging into the ground and was frightened into nearly having a heart attack.

“Are you messing with me?!”

Chapter 100: This Is the Surprise?

At the crash site of the flying vessel, smoke and dust permeated the air. Branch Leader Chu’s mask had shattered, and he couldn’t even maintain his shapeshifting technique, revealing his real appearance, which was none other than Commandery Governor Li’s! His left arm was dripping with blood and trembling uncontrollably; it was clearly useless now.

Meng Jingzhou landed, dissatisfied with the outcome. “If only we had another flying vessel.”

Branch Leader Chu heaved in a deep breath of air, wanting to make a few relevant remarks, but he suddenly coughed violently, and wisps of blood crawled to the corners of his eyes. “This smoke is poisonous!” He hurriedly held his breath, rage swelling his heart.

Truly the collaboration between the Innate Diabolic Spawn and Descended Dao Diabolic. First, they trapped me with the Spirit-Energy Disabling Array, then crashed a flying vessel filled with explosives sufficient to open a mine onto me, and even the smoke after the explosion was poisonous! You two are like old female pigs wearing bras—scheme after scheme! [1]

Branch Leader Chu had originally suspected that Lu Yang was a spy sent by the righteous path, prompting the latter to destroy the Lifespan-Reversal Array because it harmed others at the expense of personal gain; he thought that the creed leader had misjudged Lu Yang. But seeing this intricate chain of schemes now, I wouldn’t believe it even if Lu Yang claims to be a spy from the righteous path!

As the flying vessel had damaged the Spirit-Energy Disabling Array, Branch Leader Chu regained his spirit energy. However, he now had to divert part of his spirit energy to suppress the poison seeping into his body! Under normal circumstances, he would have been able to expel the toxins in just a few breaths, but Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou certainly weren’t giving him the chance!

Meng Jingzhou activated his cultivation technique, turning his body into a bronze color, becoming like a ferocious tiger with a roar that reverberated through the forest. “

“Heaven-Shaking Six Forms!” This was Third Elder’s unique art, though Meng Jingzhou had only scratched its surface.

His qi and blood surged, and every punch he hurled was brimming with bursts of force. Each strike lined up seamlessly with the previous one, waves of power booming repeatedly, as all of it greeted Branch Leader Chu’s face.

Despite Branch Leader Chu’s injuries, he was at the Advanced Golden Core Stage, after all. With just one hand, he blocked both of Meng Jingzhou’s fists.

On the other hand, Lu Yang moved like an assassin while holding his Qingfeng Sword, appearing behind Branch Leader Chu without a sound. However, Branch Leader Chu’s reactions were incredibly sharp. Deftly kicking with his right foot, he sent Lu Yang flying again.

Man Gu appeared in the direction Lu Yang was flung and grabbed his legs, spinning on the spot before hurling him back. Lu Yang was like a sharp sword, cutting through the air with his Qingfeng Sword and thrusting it toward Branch Leader Chu’s neck!

Branch Leader Chu swatted Meng Jingzhou away with one palm and nimbly turned around, catching the unstoppable Qingfeng Sword between his elbow and knee!

The trace of the Ancient Barbarian Bloodline in Man Gu was stimulated, causing his body to grow a full size larger. His muscles and bones cracked with strength and his flesh became coarse. He charged forward like a savage elephant that was ready to topple the mountains and overturn the seas!

Branch Leader Chu sneered. No matter how strong you are, do you honestly think you can surpass me, an Advanced Golden Core cultivator?

To his surprise, when Man Gu was about to collide into Branch Leader Chu, Man Gu flipped his palm, shooting out several sharp bamboo skewers toward Branch Leader Chu’s eyes. Branch Leader Chu immediately closed his eyes and dodged the bamboo skewers.

When another group of bamboo skewers emerged behind him, Branch Leader Chu could hear them. He channeled the power of his Golden Core and formed a golden membrane on the surface of his body, blocking out the ambush from the bamboo skewers. Turning around, he saw that the bamboo skewers hadn’t been thrown by anyone—they had been fired automatically by an array.

It was none other than the Automatic Skewering Array invented by Lan Ting, cranked up to maximum power. Lu Yang had arranged for Lan Ting to assist from the shadows to exert both psychological and physical pressure on Branch Leader Chu.

“All of you will die!” Branch Leader Chu pulled out a big scarlet flag from his storage ring; it seemed to have been soaked in fresh blood and exuded a sinister aura. As soon as the blood-red flag appeared, the temperature around them dropped by several degrees.

Branch Leader Chu spat out a mouthful of fresh blood. The blood-red flag absorbed its master’s blood, becoming even more eerie. The four of them could vaguely hear the cries of ghosts!

“Can’t you use a proper weapon for once? Why do you always come up with such bizarre and creepy items all the time?!” Lu Yang spat out a mixture of blood and phlegm. With his sword light leaping like a dragon returning to the sea, he sped through the earth with Shrinking Earth and suddenly darted out from beneath Branch Leader Chu!

Branch Leader Chu retreated by a step as the big flag and sharp sword clashed, producing a sonorous metallic sound. Lu Yang danced with his sword, unleashing a flurry of movements that resembled the pattern of a flower, alternating between speeds in a mesmerizing display.

The Heaven-Shaking Six Forms emerged once again as Meng Jingzhou rushed over to provide support. His fist seals thundered, and he landed a series of punches on the flagpole, nearly throwing Branch Leader Chu into disarray.

A massive tree descended from above. With a furious roar, Man Gu smashed the gigantic tree toward Branch Leader Chu!

“Fire Dragon Talisman!” A voice rang from within the forest as Lan Ting swiftly used her blood as ink to draw a talisman.

A crimson fire dragon bellowed and brandished its claws threateningly, its fiery presence scorching the air and alleviating the eerie atmosphere brought about by the blood-red flag.

“There’s a fourth person!” Branch Leader Chu’s eyes bulged in fury as he gnashed his teeth. This traitor Lu Yang! He has really made ample preparations.

“Wind-Control Wave!” Branch Leader Chu gripped the flagpole tightly and suddenly slammed it into the ground with a shout. Shockwaves of sound and energy rolled forth, knocking over the three of them and dispersing the fire dragon!

Branch Leader Chu had gone mad, his eyes bloodshot. If I hadn’t been struck by the flying vessel right at the beginning and didn’t have to allocate some of my spirit energy to suppress the poison, how could I have been put at such a disadvantage?!

He suddenly jumped, thrusting the flagpole at Man Gu, who was lying on the ground. Man Gu hurriedly tried to dodge, but it was too late. He had only managed to move half of his body when the flagpole pierced through his shoulder blade.

Blood flowed from between Man Gu’s teeth, but he did not utter a single cry of pain. The Ancient Barbarian Tribe fears no pain and death!

Branch Leader Chu was relentless, wanting to add another kick to trample Man Gu’s brain into a mush mixture. However, Meng Jingzhou seized the opportunity to toss out a magical artifact with an incensed yell. The magical artifact exploded, throwing Branch Leader Chu off balance and blasting him away. On the other hand, since Man Gu was impaled to the ground, he was unharmed.

Meng Jingzhou had many treasures with him, but they were of too high a grade, so he couldn’t activate or self-detonate them.

Branch Leader Chu kicked a boulder into smithereens, using the force to propel himself back. He retrieved the flag on his way, preparing to swipe it at Meng Jingzhou. Before he could do that, however, the Qingfeng Sword appeared right in front of him, deflecting the big flag. Lu Yang once again engaged in a fierce battle with Branch Leader Chu.

Lu Yang had already mastered the spell Shrinking Earth to perfection. Whenever Branch Leader Chu’s hits were about to strike him, he would shrink himself and evade the attack, enraging Branch Leader Chu so much that he ground his teeth.

Meanwhile, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu regrouped after their setbacks, launching yet another attack. At the same time, Lan Ting drew talismans with both hands. One water and one fire dragon soared into the sky, intertwining as they pounced toward Branch Leader Chu.

Having had enough of such humiliation, Branch Leader Chu planted the flagpole into the ground. The flag flapped in the wind like waves in the sea. Wails and howls of ghosts echoed from within, disrupting the minds of those nearby.

“Ghosts’ Mind Disruption!”

The sounds of the ghosts seemed to possess an indescribable enchanted power that froze the four of them in place. They all felt as if ghosts had entangled themselves around their bodies, preventing them from budging an inch.

Meng Jingzhou’s heart tightened. He wanted to scream and warn everyone that it was just an illusion, but not only was he unable to move, but he also couldn’t even speak.

Branch Leader Chu laughed maniacally. This was his trump card. He initially didn’t want to use it as he found it beneath him. These four brats have pushed me too far! I can’t be bothered about holding back my trump card anymore. I must kill all of them to wipe away my humiliation!

“Break.”

The Qingfeng Sword descended from the sky, as swift as lightning. Before Branch Leader Chu could react, it had already pierced through his head.

Branch Leader Chu stared at Lu Yang in disbelief. He saw Lu Yang’s clear eyes and the mocking smile tugging at his lips. He’s completely unaffected by the illusion!

“Why can you still move... How is this possible...” Branch Leader Chu collapsed backward to the ground, blood streaming from his seven orifices.

Lu Yang thrust his sword into Branch Leader Chu’s dantian and shattered his golden core. Only then could he be assured that Branch Leader Chu was truly dead.

I have no interest in telling a dead person that I had created my own technique, Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra, under Big Senior Sister’s guidance. It allows one to stay true to themselves and see through the essence of things.

He had just begun cultivating with it and still couldn’t discern the essence of things, but resisting the effects of illusionary domains and dreamscapes from cultivators a level higher was still manageable.

Meanwhile, the inspecting officer had been delayed by various matters and had just arrived from a neighboring commandery. He recalled Branch Leader Chu saying that he had a surprise for him and that the new recruit Lu Yang was a rare talent who would definitely shine during the Spring Harvest Festival.

“...This is the surprise Little Chu was talking about?”

Despite having lived for a hundred years, it was the inspecting officer’s first time encountering such a surprise.
